  254.     /** 
  255.      * Main singleton instance.

  257.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf)

  263.     private function __construct( $slug, $is_init = false ) { 
  264.         $this->_slug = $slug; 
  265.  
  266.         $this->_logger = FS_Logger::get_logger( WP_FS__SLUG . '_' . $slug, WP_FS__DEBUG_SDK, WP_FS__ECHO_DEBUG_SDK ); 
  267.  
  268.         $this->_storage = FS_Key_Value_Storage::instance( 'plugin_data', $this->_slug ); 
  269.  
  270.         $this->_plugin_main_file_path = $this->_find_caller_plugin_file( $is_init ); 
  271.         $this->_plugin_dir_path = plugin_dir_path( $this->_plugin_main_file_path ); 
  272.         $this->_plugin_basename = plugin_basename( $this->_plugin_main_file_path ); 
  273.         $this->_free_plugin_basename = str_replace( '-premium/', '/', $this->_plugin_basename ); 
  274.  
  275.         $base_name_split = explode( '/', $this->_plugin_basename ); 
  276.         $this->_plugin_dir_name = $base_name_split[0]; 
  277.  
  278.         if ( $this->_logger->is_on() ) { 
  279.             $this->_logger->info( 'plugin_main_file_path = ' . $this->_plugin_main_file_path ); 
  280.             $this->_logger->info( 'plugin_dir_path = ' . $this->_plugin_dir_path ); 
  281.             $this->_logger->info( 'plugin_basename = ' . $this->_plugin_basename ); 
  282.             $this->_logger->info( 'free_plugin_basename = ' . $this->_free_plugin_basename ); 
  283.             $this->_logger->info( 'plugin_dir_name = ' . $this->_plugin_dir_name ); 
  284.         } 
  285.  
  286.         // Remember link between file to slug. 
  287.         $this->store_file_slug_map(); 
  288.  
  289.         // Store plugin's initial install timestamp. 
  290.         if ( ! isset( $this->_storage->install_timestamp ) ) { 
  291.             $this->_storage->install_timestamp = WP_FS__SCRIPT_START_TIME; 
  292.         } 
  293.  
  294.         $this->_plugin = FS_Plugin_Manager::instance( $this->_slug )->get(); 
  295.  
  296.         $this->_admin_notices = FS_Admin_Notice_Manager::instance( 
  297.             $slug,  
  298.             is_object( $this->_plugin ) ? $this->_plugin->title : '' 
  299.  ); 
  300.  
  301.         if ( 'true' === fs_request_get( 'fs_clear_api_cache' ) || 
  302.              'true' === fs_request_is_action( 'restart_freemius' ) 
  303.  ) { 
  304.             FS_Api::clear_cache(); 
  305.         } 
  306.  
  307.         $this->_register_hooks(); 
  308.  
  309.         $this->_load_account(); 
  310.  
  311.         $this->_version_updates_handler(); 
  312.     } 
  313.  
  314.     /** 
  315.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  316.      * @since  1.0.9 
  317.      */ 
  318.     private function _version_updates_handler() { 
  319.         if ( ! isset( $this->_storage->sdk_version ) || $this->_storage->sdk_version != $this->version ) { 
  320.             // Freemius version upgrade mode. 
  321.             $this->_storage->sdk_last_version = $this->_storage->sdk_version; 
  322.             $this->_storage->sdk_version = $this->version; 
  323.  
  324.             if ( empty( $this->_storage->sdk_last_version ) || 
  325.                  version_compare( $this->_storage->sdk_last_version, $this->version, '<' ) 
  326.  ) { 
  327.                 $this->_storage->sdk_upgrade_mode = true; 
  328.                 $this->_storage->sdk_downgrade_mode = false; 
  329.             } else { 
  330.                 $this->_storage->sdk_downgrade_mode = true; 
  331.                 $this->_storage->sdk_upgrade_mode = false; 
  332.  
  333.             } 
  334.  
  335.             $this->do_action( 'sdk_version_update', $this->_storage->sdk_last_version, $this->version ); 
  336.         } 
  337.  
  338.         $plugin_version = $this->get_plugin_version(); 
  339.         if ( ! isset( $this->_storage->plugin_version ) || $this->_storage->plugin_version != $plugin_version ) { 
  340.             // Plugin version upgrade mode. 
  341.             $this->_storage->plugin_last_version = $this->_storage->plugin_version; 
  342.             $this->_storage->plugin_version = $plugin_version; 
  343.  
  344.             if ( empty( $this->_storage->plugin_last_version ) || 
  345.                  version_compare( $this->_storage->plugin_last_version, $plugin_version, '<' ) 
  346.  ) { 
  347.                 $this->_storage->plugin_upgrade_mode = true; 
  348.                 $this->_storage->plugin_downgrade_mode = false; 
  349.             } else { 
  350.                 $this->_storage->plugin_downgrade_mode = true; 
  351.                 $this->_storage->plugin_upgrade_mode = false; 
  352.             } 
  353.  
  354.             if ( ! empty( $this->_storage->plugin_last_version ) ) { 
  355.                 // Different version of the plugin was installed before, therefore it's an update. 
  356.                 $this->_storage->is_plugin_new_install = false; 
  357.             } 
  358.  
  359.             $this->do_action( 'plugin_version_update', $this->_storage->plugin_last_version, $plugin_version ); 
  360.         } 
  361.     } 
  362.  
  363.     /** 
  364.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  365.      * @since  1.1.5 
  366.      * 
  367.      * @param string $sdk_prev_version 
  368.      * @param string $sdk_version 
  369.      */ 
  370.     function _data_migration( $sdk_prev_version, $sdk_version ) { 
  371.         /** 
  372.          * @since 1.1.7.3 Fixed unwanted connectivity test cleanup. 
  373.          */ 
  374.         if ( empty( $sdk_prev_version ) ) { 
  375.             return; 
  376.         } 
  377.  
  378.         if ( version_compare( $sdk_prev_version, '1.1.5', '<' ) && 
  379.              version_compare( $sdk_version, '1.1.5', '>=' ) 
  380.  ) { 
  381.             // On version 1.1.5 merged connectivity and is_on data. 
  382.             if ( isset( $this->_storage->connectivity_test ) ) { 
  383.                 if ( ! isset( $this->_storage->is_on ) ) { 
  384.                     unset( $this->_storage->connectivity_test ); 
  385.                 } else { 
  386.                     $connectivity_data = $this->_storage->connectivity_test; 
  387.                     $connectivity_data['is_active'] = $this->_storage->is_on['is_active']; 
  388.                     $connectivity_data['timestamp'] = $this->_storage->is_on['timestamp']; 
  389.  
  390.                     // Override. 
  391.                     $this->_storage->connectivity_test = $connectivity_data; 
  392.  
  393.                     // Remove previous structure. 
  394.                     unset( $this->_storage->is_on ); 
  395.                 } 
  396.  
  397.             } 
  398.         } 
  399.     } 
  400.  
  401.     /** 
  402.      * This action is connected to the 'plugins_loaded' hook and helps to determine 
  403.      * if this is a new plugin installation or a plugin update. 
  404.      * 
  405.      * There are 3 different use-cases: 
  406.      *    1) New plugin installation right with Freemius: 
  407.      *       1.1 _activate_plugin_event_hook() will be executed first 
  408.      *       1.2 Since $this->_storage->is_plugin_new_install is not set,  
  409.      *           and $this->_storage->plugin_last_version is not set,  
  410.      *           $this->_storage->is_plugin_new_install will be set to TRUE. 
  411.      *       1.3 When _plugins_loaded() will be executed, $this->_storage->is_plugin_new_install will 
  412.      *           be already set to TRUE. 
  413.      * 
  414.      *    2) Plugin update, didn't have Freemius before, and now have the SDK: 
  415.      *       2.1 _activate_plugin_event_hook() will not be executed, because 
  416.      *           the activation hook do NOT fires on updates since WP 3.1. 
  417.      *       2.2 When _plugins_loaded() will be executed, $this->_storage->is_plugin_new_install will 
  418.      *           be empty, therefore, it will be set to FALSE. 
  419.      * 
  420.      *    3) Plugin update, had Freemius in prev version as well: 
  421.      *       3.1 _version_updates_handler() will be executed 1st, since FS was installed 
  422.      *           before, $this->_storage->plugin_last_version will NOT be empty,  
  423.      *           therefore, $this->_storage->is_plugin_new_install will be set to FALSE. 
  424.      *       3.2 When _plugins_loaded() will be executed, $this->_storage->is_plugin_new_install is 
  425.      *           already set, therefore, it will not be modified. 
  426.      * 
  427.      *    Use-case #3 is backward compatible, #3.1 will be executed since 1.0.9. 
  428.      * 
  429.      * NOTE: 
  430.      *    The only fallback of this mechanism is if an admin updates a plugin based on use-case #2,  
  431.      *    and then, the next immediate PageView is the plugin's main settings page, it will not 
  432.      *    show the opt-in right away. The reason it will happen is because Freemius execution 
  433.      *    will be turned off till the plugin is fully loaded at least once 
  434.      *    (till $this->_storage->was_plugin_loaded is TRUE). 
  435.      * 
  436.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  437.      * @since  1.1.9 
  438.      * 
  439.      */ 
  440.     function _plugins_loaded() { 
  441.         // Update flag that plugin was loaded with Freemius at least once. 
  442.         $this->_storage->was_plugin_loaded = true; 
  443.  
  444.         if ( ! isset( $this->_storage->is_plugin_new_install ) ) { 
  445.             $this->_storage->is_plugin_new_install = false; 
  446.         } 
  447.     } 
  448.  
  449.     /** 
  450.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  451.      * @since  1.0.9 
  452.      */ 
  453.     private function _register_hooks() { 
  454.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  455.  
  456.         if ( is_admin() ) { 
  457.             $plugin_dir = dirname( $this->_plugin_dir_path ) . '/'; 
  458.  
  459.             /** 
  460.              * @since 1.2.2 
  461.              * 
  462.              * Hook to both free and premium version activations to support 
  463.              * auto deactivation on the other version activation. 
  464.              */ 
  465.             register_activation_hook( 
  466.                 $plugin_dir . $this->_free_plugin_basename,  
  467.                 array( &$this, '_activate_plugin_event_hook' ) 
  468.  ); 
  469.             register_activation_hook( 
  470.                 $plugin_dir . $this->premium_plugin_basename(),  
  471.                 array( &$this, '_activate_plugin_event_hook' ) 
  472.  ); 
  473.  
  474.             /** 
  475.              * Part of the mechanism to identify new plugin install vs. plugin update. 
  476.              * 
  477.              * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  478.              * @since  1.1.9 
  479.              */ 
  480.             if ( empty( $this->_storage->was_plugin_loaded ) ) { 
  481.                 if ( $this->is_activation_mode( false ) ) { 
  482.                     add_action( 'plugins_loaded', array( &$this, '_plugins_loaded' ) ); 
  483.                 } else { 
  484.                     // If was activated before, then it was already loaded before. 
  485.                     $this->_plugins_loaded(); 
  486.                 } 
  487.             } 
  488.  
  489.             if ( ! $this->is_ajax() ) { 
  490.                 if ( ! $this->is_addon() ) { 
  491.                     add_action( 'init', array( &$this, '_add_default_submenu_items' ), WP_FS__LOWEST_PRIORITY ); 
  492.                     add_action( 'admin_menu', array( &$this, '_prepare_admin_menu' ), WP_FS__LOWEST_PRIORITY ); 
  493.                 } 
  494.             } 
  495.         } 
  496.  
  497.         register_deactivation_hook( $this->_plugin_main_file_path, array( &$this, '_deactivate_plugin_hook' ) ); 
  498.  
  499.         add_action( 'init', array( &$this, '_redirect_on_clicked_menu_link' ), WP_FS__LOWEST_PRIORITY ); 
  500.  
  501.         add_action( 'admin_init', array( &$this, '_add_tracking_links' ) ); 
  502.         add_action( 'admin_init', array( &$this, '_add_license_activation' ) ); 
  503.         $this->add_ajax_action( 'update_billing', array( &$this, '_update_billing_ajax_action' ) ); 
  504.         $this->add_ajax_action( 'start_trial', array( &$this, '_start_trial_ajax_action' ) ); 
  505.  
  506.         $this->add_action( 'after_plans_sync', array( &$this, '_check_for_trial_plans' ) ); 
  507.  
  508.         $this->add_action( 'sdk_version_update', array( &$this, '_data_migration' ), WP_FS__DEFAULT_PRIORITY, 2 ); 
  509.  
  510.         add_action( 'admin_init', array( &$this, '_add_trial_notice' ) ); 
  511.         add_action( 'admin_init', array( &$this, '_enqueue_common_css' ) ); 
  512.  
  513.         /** 
  514.          * Handle request to reset anonymous mode for `get_reconnect_url()`. 
  515.          * 
  516.          * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  517.          * @since  1.2.1.5 
  518.          */ 
  519.         if ( fs_request_is_action( 'reset_anonymous_mode' ) && 
  520.              $this->_slug === fs_request_get( 'fs_slug' ) 
  521.  ) { 
  522.             add_action( 'admin_init', array( &$this, 'connect_again' ) ); 
  523.         } 
  524.     } 
  525.  
  526.     /** 
  527.      * Keeping the uninstall hook registered for free or premium plugin version may result to a fatal error that 
  528.      * could happen when a user tries to uninstall either version while one of them is still active. Uninstalling a 
  529.      * plugin will trigger inclusion of the free or premium version and if one of them is active during the 
  530.      * uninstallation, a fatal error may occur in case the plugin's class or functions are already defined. 
  531.      * 
  532.      * @author Leo Fajardo (leorw) 
  533.      * 
  534.      * @since  1.2.0 
  535.      */ 
  536.     private function unregister_uninstall_hook() { 
  537.         $uninstallable_plugins = (array) get_option( 'uninstall_plugins' ); 
  538.         unset( $uninstallable_plugins[ $this->_free_plugin_basename ] ); 
  539.         unset( $uninstallable_plugins[ $this->premium_plugin_basename() ] ); 
  540.  
  541.         update_option( 'uninstall_plugins', $uninstallable_plugins ); 
  542.     } 
  543.  
  544.     /** 
  545.      * @since 1.2.0 Invalidate module's main file cache, otherwise, FS_Plugin_Updater will not fetch updates. 
  546.      */ 
  547.     private function clear_module_main_file_cache() { 
  548.         if ( ! isset( $this->_storage->plugin_main_file ) || 
  549.              empty( $this->_storage->plugin_main_file->path ) 
  550.  ) { 
  551.             return; 
  552.         } 
  553.  
  554.         $plugin_main_file = clone $this->_storage->plugin_main_file; 
  555.  
  556.         // Store cached path (2nd layer cache). 
  557.         $plugin_main_file->prev_path = $plugin_main_file->path; 
  558.  
  559.         // Clear cached path. 
  560.         unset( $plugin_main_file->path ); 
  561.  
  562.         $this->_storage->plugin_main_file = $plugin_main_file; 
  563.     } 
  564.  
  565.     /** 
  566.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  567.      * @since  1.0.9 
  568.      */ 
  569.     private function _register_account_hooks() { 
  570.         if ( is_admin() ) { 
  571.             // If user is paying or in trial and have the free version installed,  
  572.             // assume that the deactivation is for the upgrade process. 
  573.             if ( ! $this->is_paying_or_trial() || $this->is_premium() ) { 
  574.                 $this->add_ajax_action( 
  575.                     'submit_uninstall_reason',  
  576.                     array( &$this, '_submit_uninstall_reason_action' ) 
  577.  ); 
  578.  
  579.                 if ( $this->is_plugins_page() ) { 
  580.                     add_action( 'admin_footer', array( &$this, '_add_deactivation_feedback_dialog_box' ) ); 
  581.                 } 
  582.             } 
  583.  
  584.             if ( ! $this->is_addon() ) { 
  585.                 if ( $this->is_registered() ) { 
  586.                     $this->add_filter( 'after_code_type_change', array( &$this, '_after_code_type_change' ) ); 
  587.                 } 
  588.             } 
  589.         } 
  590.     } 
  591.  
  592.     /** 
  593.      * Leverage backtrace to find caller plugin file path. 
  594.      * 
  595.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  596.      * @since  1.0.6 
  597.      * 
  598.      * @param bool $is_init Is initiation sequence. 
  599.      * 
  600.      * @return string 
  601.      * 
  602.      * @uses   fs_find_caller_plugin_file 
  603.      */ 
  604.     private function _find_caller_plugin_file( $is_init = false ) { 
  605.         // Try to load the cached value of the file path. 
  606.         if ( isset( $this->_storage->plugin_main_file ) ) { 
  607.             $plugin_main_file = $this->_storage->plugin_main_file; 
  608.             if ( isset( $plugin_main_file->path ) && file_exists( $plugin_main_file->path ) ) { 
  609.                 return $this->_storage->plugin_main_file->path; 
  610.             } 
  611.         } 
  612.  
  613.         /** 
  614.          * @since 1.2.1 
  615.          * 
  616.          * `clear_module_main_file_cache()` is clearing the plugin's cached path on 
  617.          * deactivation. Therefore, if any plugin/theme was initiating `Freemius` 
  618.          * with that plugin's slug, it was overriding the empty plugin path with a wrong path. 
  619.          * 
  620.          * So, we've added a special mechanism with a 2nd layer of cache that uses `prev_path` 
  621.          * when the class instantiator isn't the module. 
  622.          */ 
  623.         if ( ! $is_init ) { 
  624.             // Fetch prev path cache. 
  625.             if ( isset( $this->_storage->plugin_main_file ) && 
  626.                  isset( $this->_storage->plugin_main_file->prev_path ) 
  627.  ) { 
  628.                 if ( file_exists( $this->_storage->plugin_main_file->prev_path ) ) { 
  629.                     return $this->_storage->plugin_main_file->prev_path; 
  630.                 } 
  631.             } 
  632.  
  633.             wp_die( 
  634.                 __fs( 'failed-finding-main-path', $this->_slug ),  
  635.                 __fs( 'error' ),  
  636.                 array( 'back_link' => true ) 
  637.  ); 
  638.         } 
  639.  
  640.         /** 
  641.          * @since 1.2.1 
  642.          * 
  643.          * Only the original instantiator that calls dynamic_init can modify the module's path. 
  644.          */ 
  645.         // Find caller module. 
  646.         $plugin_file = fs_find_caller_plugin_file(); 
  647.  
  648.         $this->_storage->plugin_main_file = (object) array( 
  649.             'path' => fs_normalize_path( $plugin_file ),  
  650.  ); 
  651.  
  652.         return $plugin_file; 
  653.     } 
  654.  
  655.  
  656.     #---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- 
  657.     #region Deactivation Feedback Form 
  658.     #---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- 
  659.  
  660.     /** 
  661.      * Displays a confirmation and feedback dialog box when the user clicks on the "Deactivate" link on the plugins 
  662.      * page. 
  663.      * 
  664.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  665.      * @author Leo Fajardo (@leorw) 
  666.      * @since  1.1.2 
  667.      */ 
  668.     function _add_deactivation_feedback_dialog_box() { 
  669.         /** Check the type of user: 
  670.          * 1. Long-term (long-term) 
  671.          * 2. Non-registered and non-anonymous short-term (non-registered-and-non-anonymous-short-term). 
  672.          * 3. Short-term (short-term) 
  673.          */ 
  674.         $is_long_term_user = true; 
  675.  
  676.         // Check if the site is at least 2 days old. 
  677.         $time_installed = $this->_storage->install_timestamp; 
  678.  
  679.         // Difference in seconds. 
  680.         $date_diff = time() - $time_installed; 
  681.  
  682.         // Convert seconds to days. 
  683.         $date_diff_days = floor( $date_diff / ( 60 * 60 * 24 ) ); 
  684.  
  685.         if ( $date_diff_days < 2 ) { 
  686.             $is_long_term_user = false; 
  687.         } 
  688.  
  689.         $is_long_term_user = $this->apply_filters( 'is_long_term_user', $is_long_term_user ); 
  690.  
  691.         if ( $is_long_term_user ) { 
  692.             $user_type = 'long-term'; 
  693.         } else { 
  694.             if ( ! $this->is_registered() && ! $this->is_anonymous() ) { 
  695.                 $user_type = 'non-registered-and-non-anonymous-short-term'; 
  696.             } else { 
  697.                 $user_type = 'short-term'; 
  698.             } 
  699.         } 
  700.  
  701.         $uninstall_reasons = $this->_get_uninstall_reasons( $user_type ); 
  702.  
  703.         // Load the HTML template for the deactivation feedback dialog box. 
  704.         $vars = array( 
  705.             'reasons' => $uninstall_reasons,  
  706.             'slug' => $this->_slug 
  707.  ); 
  708.  
  709.         /** 
  710.          * @todo Deactivation form core functions should be loaded only once! Otherwise, when there are multiple Freemius powered plugins the same code is loaded multiple times. The only thing that should be loaded differently is the various deactivation reasons object based on the state of the plugin. 
  711.          */ 
  712.         fs_require_template( 'forms/deactivation/form.php', $vars ); 
  713.     } 
  714.  
  715.     /** 
  716.      * @author Leo Fajardo (leorw) 
  717.      * @since  1.1.2 
  718.      * 
  719.      * @param string $user_type 
  720.      * 
  721.      * @return array The uninstall reasons for the specified user type. 
  722.      */ 
  723.     function _get_uninstall_reasons( $user_type = 'long-term' ) { 
  724.         $internal_message_template_var = array( 
  725.             'slug' => $this->_slug 
  726.  ); 
  727.  
  728.         if ( $this->is_registered() && false !== $this->get_plan() && $this->get_plan()->has_technical_support() ) { 
  729.             $contact_support_template = fs_get_template( 'forms/deactivation/contact.php', $internal_message_template_var ); 
  730.         } else { 
  731.             $contact_support_template = ''; 
  732.         } 
  733.  
  734.         $reason_found_better_plugin = array( 
  735.             'id' => self::REASON_FOUND_A_BETTER_PLUGIN,  
  736.             'text' => __fs( 'reason-found-a-better-plugin', $this->_slug ),  
  737.             'input_type' => 'textfield',  
  738.             'input_placeholder' => __fs( 'placeholder-plugin-name', $this->_slug ) 
  739.  ); 
  740.  
  741.         $reason_temporary_deactivation = array( 
  742.             'id' => self::REASON_TEMPORARY_DEACTIVATION,  
  743.             'text' => __fs( 'reason-temporary-deactivation', $this->_slug ),  
  744.             'input_type' => '',  
  745.             'input_placeholder' => '' 
  746.  ); 
  747.  
  748.         $reason_other = array( 
  749.             'id' => self::REASON_OTHER,  
  750.             'text' => __fs( 'reason-other', $this->_slug ),  
  751.             'input_type' => 'textfield',  
  752.             'input_placeholder' => '' 
  753.  ); 
  754.  
  755.         $long_term_user_reasons = array( 
  756.             array( 
  757.                 'id' => self::REASON_NO_LONGER_NEEDED,  
  758.                 'text' => __fs( 'reason-no-longer-needed', $this->_slug ),  
  759.                 'input_type' => '',  
  760.                 'input_placeholder' => '' 
  761.  ),  
  762.             $reason_found_better_plugin,  
  763.             array( 
  764.                 'id' => self::REASON_NEEDED_FOR_A_SHORT_PERIOD,  
  765.                 'text' => __fs( 'reason-needed-for-a-short-period', $this->_slug ),  
  766.                 'input_type' => '',  
  767.                 'input_placeholder' => '' 
  768.  ),  
  769.             array( 
  770.                 'id' => self::REASON_BROKE_MY_SITE,  
  771.                 'text' => __fs( 'reason-broke-my-site', $this->_slug ),  
  772.                 'input_type' => '',  
  773.                 'input_placeholder' => '',  
  774.                 'internal_message' => $contact_support_template 
  775.  ),  
  776.             array( 
  777.                 'id' => self::REASON_SUDDENLY_STOPPED_WORKING,  
  778.                 'text' => __fs( 'reason-suddenly-stopped-working', $this->_slug ),  
  779.                 'input_type' => '',  
  780.                 'input_placeholder' => '',  
  781.                 'internal_message' => $contact_support_template 
  782.  ) 
  783.  ); 
  784.  
  785.         if ( $this->is_paying() ) { 
  786.             $long_term_user_reasons[] = array( 
  787.                 'id' => self::REASON_CANT_PAY_ANYMORE,  
  788.                 'text' => __fs( 'reason-cant-pay-anymore', $this->_slug ),  
  789.                 'input_type' => 'textfield',  
  790.                 'input_placeholder' => __fs( 'placeholder-comfortable-price', $this->_slug ) 
  791.  ); 
  792.         } 
  793.  
  794.         $reason_dont_share_info = array( 
  795.             'id' => self::REASON_DONT_LIKE_TO_SHARE_MY_INFORMATION,  
  796.             'text' => __fs( 'reason-dont-like-to-share-my-information', $this->_slug ),  
  797.             'input_type' => '',  
  798.             'input_placeholder' => '' 
  799.  ); 
  800.  
  801.         /** 
  802.          * If the current user has selected the "don't share data" reason in the deactivation feedback modal, inform the 
  803.          * user by showing additional message that he doesn't have to share data and can just choose to skip the opt-in 
  804.          * (the Skip button is included in the message to show). This message will only be shown if anonymous mode is 
  805.          * enabled and the user's account is currently not in pending activation state (similar to the way the Skip 
  806.          * button in the opt-in form is shown/hidden). 
  807.          */ 
  808.         if ( $this->is_enable_anonymous() && ! $this->is_pending_activation() ) { 
  809.             $reason_dont_share_info['internal_message'] = fs_get_template( 'forms/deactivation/retry-skip.php', $internal_message_template_var ); 
  810.         } 
  811.  
  812.         $uninstall_reasons = array( 
  813.             'long-term' => $long_term_user_reasons,  
  814.             'non-registered-and-non-anonymous-short-term' => array( 
  815.                 array( 
  816.                     'id' => self::REASON_DIDNT_WORK,  
  817.                     'text' => __fs( 'reason-didnt-work', $this->_slug ),  
  818.                     'input_type' => '',  
  819.                     'input_placeholder' => '' 
  820.  ),  
  821.                 $reason_dont_share_info,  
  822.                 $reason_found_better_plugin 
  823.  ),  
  824.             'short-term' => array( 
  825.                 array( 
  826.                     'id' => self::REASON_COULDNT_MAKE_IT_WORK,  
  827.                     'text' => __fs( 'reason-couldnt-make-it-work', $this->_slug ),  
  828.                     'input_type' => '',  
  829.                     'input_placeholder' => '',  
  830.                     'internal_message' => $contact_support_template 
  831.  ),  
  832.                 $reason_found_better_plugin,  
  833.                 array( 
  834.                     'id' => self::REASON_GREAT_BUT_NEED_SPECIFIC_FEATURE,  
  835.                     'text' => __fs( 'reason-great-but-need-specific-feature', $this->_slug ),  
  836.                     'input_type' => 'textarea',  
  837.                     'input_placeholder' => __fs( 'placeholder-feature', $this->_slug ) 
  838.  ),  
  839.                 array( 
  840.                     'id' => self::REASON_NOT_WORKING,  
  841.                     'text' => __fs( 'reason-not-working', $this->_slug ),  
  842.                     'input_type' => 'textarea',  
  843.                     'input_placeholder' => __fs( 'placeholder-share-what-didnt-work', $this->_slug ) 
  844.  ),  
  845.                 array( 
  846.                     'id' => self::REASON_NOT_WHAT_I_WAS_LOOKING_FOR,  
  847.                     'text' => __fs( 'reason-not-what-i-was-looking-for', $this->_slug ),  
  848.                     'input_type' => 'textarea',  
  849.                     'input_placeholder' => __fs( 'placeholder-what-youve-been-looking-for', $this->_slug ) 
  850.  ),  
  851.                 array( 
  852.                     'id' => self::REASON_DIDNT_WORK_AS_EXPECTED,  
  853.                     'text' => __fs( 'reason-didnt-work-as-expected', $this->_slug ),  
  854.                     'input_type' => 'textarea',  
  855.                     'input_placeholder' => __fs( 'placeholder-what-did-you-expect', $this->_slug ) 
  856.  ) 
  857.  ) 
  858.  ); 
  859.  
  860.         // Randomize the reasons for the current user type. 
  861.         shuffle( $uninstall_reasons[ $user_type ] ); 
  862.  
  863.         // Keep the following reasons as the last items in the list. 
  864.         $uninstall_reasons[ $user_type ][] = $reason_temporary_deactivation; 
  865.         $uninstall_reasons[ $user_type ][] = $reason_other; 
  866.  
  867.         $uninstall_reasons = $this->apply_filters( 'uninstall_reasons', $uninstall_reasons ); 
  868.  
  869.         return $uninstall_reasons[ $user_type ]; 
  870.     } 
  871.  
  872.     /** 
  873.      * Called after the user has submitted his reason for deactivating the plugin. 
  874.      * 
  875.      * @author Leo Fajardo (@leorw) 
  876.      * @since  1.1.2 
  877.      */ 
  878.     function _submit_uninstall_reason_action() { 
  879.         $reason_id = fs_request_get( 'reason_id' ); 
  880.  
  881.         // Check if the given reason ID is an unsigned integer. 
  882.         if ( ! ctype_digit( $reason_id ) ) { 
  883.             exit; 
  884.         } 
  885.  
  886.         $reason_info = trim( fs_request_get( 'reason_info', '' ) ); 
  887.         if ( ! empty( $reason_info ) ) { 
  888.             $reason_info = substr( $reason_info, 0, 128 ); 
  889.         } 
  890.  
  891.         $reason = (object) array( 
  892.             'id' => $reason_id,  
  893.             'info' => $reason_info,  
  894.             'is_anonymous' => fs_request_get_bool( 'is_anonymous' ) 
  895.  ); 
  896.  
  897.         $this->_storage->store( 'uninstall_reason', $reason ); 
  898.  
  899.         // Print '1' for successful operation. 
  900.         echo 1; 
  901.         exit; 
  902.     } 
  903.  
  904.     #endregion 
  905.  
  906.     #---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- 
  907.     #region Instance 
  908.     #---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- 
  909.  
  910.     /** 
  911.      * Main singleton instance. 
  912.      * 
  913.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  914.      * @since  1.0.0 
  915.      * 
  916.      * @param string $slug 
  917.      * @param bool   $is_init Is initiation sequence. 
  918.      * 
  919.      * @return Freemius 
  920.      */ 
  921.     static function instance( $slug, $is_init = false ) { 
  922.         $slug = strtolower( $slug ); 
  923.  
  924.         if ( ! isset( self::$_instances[ $slug ] ) ) { 
  925.             if ( 0 === count( self::$_instances ) ) { 
  926.                 self::_load_required_static(); 
  927.             } 
  928.  
  929.             self::$_instances[ $slug ] = new Freemius( $slug, $is_init ); 
  930.         } 
  931.  
  932.         return self::$_instances[ $slug ]; 
  933.     } 
  934.  
  935.     /** 
  936.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  937.      * @since  1.0.6 
  938.      * 
  939.      * @param string|number $slug_or_id 
  940.      * 
  941.      * @return bool 
  942.      */ 
  943.     private static function has_instance( $slug_or_id ) { 
  944.         return ! is_numeric( $slug_or_id ) ? 
  945.             isset( self::$_instances[ strtolower( $slug_or_id ) ] ) : 
  946.             ( false !== self::get_instance_by_id( $slug_or_id ) ); 
  947.     } 
  948.  
  949.     /** 
  950.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  951.      * @since  1.0.6 
  952.      * 
  953.      * @param $id 
  954.      * 
  955.      * @return false|Freemius 
  956.      */ 
  957.     static function get_instance_by_id( $id ) { 
  958.         foreach ( self::$_instances as $slug => $instance ) { 
  959.             if ( $id == $instance->get_id() ) { 
  960.                 return $instance; 
  961.             } 
  962.         } 
  963.  
  964.         return false; 
  965.     } 
  966.  
  967.     /** 
  968.      * 
  969.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  970.      * @since  1.0.1 
  971.      * 
  972.      * @param $plugin_file 
  973.      * 
  974.      * @return false|Freemius 
  975.      */ 
  976.     static function get_instance_by_file( $plugin_file ) { 
  977.         $slug = self::find_slug_by_basename( $plugin_file ); 
  978.  
  979.         return ( false !== $slug ) ? 
  980.             self::instance( $slug ) : 
  981.             false; 
  982.     } 
  983.  
  984.     /** 
  985.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  986.      * @since  1.0.6 
  987.      * 
  988.      * @return false|Freemius 
  989.      */ 
  990.     function get_parent_instance() { 
  991.         return self::get_instance_by_id( $this->_plugin->parent_plugin_id ); 
  992.     } 
  993.  
  994.     /** 
  995.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  996.      * @since  1.0.6 
  997.      * 
  998.      * @param $slug_or_id 
  999.      * 
  1000.      * @return bool|Freemius 
  1001.      */ 
  1002.     function get_addon_instance( $slug_or_id ) { 
  1003.         return ! is_numeric( $slug_or_id ) ? 
  1004.             self::instance( strtolower( $slug_or_id ) ) : 
  1005.             self::get_instance_by_id( $slug_or_id ); 
  1006.     } 
  1007.  
  1008.     #endregion ------------------------------------------------------------------ 
  1009.  
  1010.     /** 
  1011.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  1012.      * @since  1.0.6 
  1013.      * 
  1014.      * @return bool 
  1015.      */ 
  1016.     function is_parent_plugin_installed() { 
  1017.         return self::has_instance( $this->_plugin->parent_plugin_id ); 
  1018.     } 
  1019.  
  1020.     /** 
  1021.      * Check if add-on parent plugin in activation mode. 
  1022.      * 
  1023.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  1024.      * @since  1.0.7 
  1025.      * 
  1026.      * @return bool 
  1027.      */ 
  1028.     function is_parent_in_activation() { 
  1029.         $parent_fs = $this->get_parent_instance(); 
  1030.         if ( ! is_object( $parent_fs ) ) { 
  1031.             return false; 
  1032.         } 
  1033.  
  1034.         return ( $parent_fs->is_activation_mode() ); 
  1035.     } 
  1036.  
  1037.     /** 
  1038.      * Is plugin in activation mode. 
  1039.      * 
  1040.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  1041.      * @since  1.0.7 
  1042.      * 
  1043.      * @param bool $and_on 
  1044.      * 
  1045.      * @return bool 
  1046.      */ 
  1047.     function is_activation_mode( $and_on = true ) { 
  1048.         return ( 
  1049.             ( $this->is_on() || ! $and_on ) && 
  1050.             ! $this->is_registered() && 
  1051.             ( ! $this->is_enable_anonymous() || 
  1052.               ( ! $this->is_anonymous() && ! $this->is_pending_activation() ) ) 
  1053.  ); 
  1054.     } 
  1055.  
  1056.     /** 
  1057.      * Get collection of all active plugins. 
  1058.      * 
  1059.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  1060.      * @since  1.0.9 
  1061.      * 
  1062.      * @return array[string]array 
  1063.      */ 
  1064.     private static function get_active_plugins() { 
  1065.         self::require_plugin_essentials(); 
  1066.  
  1067.         $active_plugin = array(); 
  1068.         $all_plugins = get_plugins(); 
  1069.         $active_plugins_basenames = get_option( 'active_plugins' ); 
  1070.  
  1071.         foreach ( $active_plugins_basenames as $plugin_basename ) { 
  1072.             $active_plugin[ $plugin_basename ] = $all_plugins[ $plugin_basename ]; 
  1073.         } 
  1074.  
  1075.         return $active_plugin; 
  1076.     } 
  1077.  
  1078.     /** 
  1079.      * Get collection of all plugins. 
  1080.      * 
  1081.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  1082.      * @since  1.1.8 
  1083.      * 
  1084.      * @return array Key is the plugin file path and the value is an array of the plugin data. 
  1085.      */ 
  1086.     private static function get_all_plugins() { 
  1087.         self::require_plugin_essentials(); 
  1088.  
  1089.         $all_plugins = get_plugins(); 
  1090.         $active_plugins_basenames = get_option( 'active_plugins' ); 
  1091.  
  1092.         foreach ( $all_plugins as $basename => &$data ) { 
  1093.             // By default set to inactive (next foreach update the active plugins). 
  1094.             $data['is_active'] = false; 
  1095.             // Enrich with plugin slug. 
  1096.             $data['slug'] = self::get_plugin_slug( $basename ); 
  1097.         } 
  1098.  
  1099.         // Flag active plugins. 
  1100.         foreach ( $active_plugins_basenames as $basename ) { 
  1101.             if ( isset( $all_plugins[ $basename ] ) ) { 
  1102.                 $all_plugins[ $basename ]['is_active'] = true; 
  1103.             } 
  1104.         } 
  1105.  
  1106.         return $all_plugins; 
  1107.     } 
  1108.  
  1109.  
  1110.     /** 
  1111.      * Cached result of get_site_transient( 'update_plugins' ) 
  1112.      * 
  1113.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  1114.      * @since  1.1.8 
  1115.      * 
  1116.      * @var object 
  1117.      */ 
  1118.     private static $_plugins_info; 
  1119.  
  1120.     /** 
  1121.      * Helper function to get specified plugin's slug. 
  1122.      * 
  1123.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  1124.      * @since  1.1.8 
  1125.      * 
  1126.      * @param $basename 
  1127.      * 
  1128.      * @return string 
  1129.      */ 
  1130.     private static function get_plugin_slug( $basename ) { 
  1131.         if ( ! isset( self::$_plugins_info ) ) { 
  1132.             self::$_plugins_info = get_site_transient( 'update_plugins' ); 
  1133.         } 
  1134.  
  1135.         $slug = ''; 
  1136.  
  1137.         if ( is_object( self::$_plugins_info ) ) { 
  1138.             if ( isset( self::$_plugins_info->no_update ) && 
  1139.                  isset( self::$_plugins_info->no_update[ $basename ] ) && 
  1140.                  ! empty( self::$_plugins_info->no_update[ $basename ]->slug ) 
  1141.  ) { 
  1142.                 $slug = self::$_plugins_info->no_update[ $basename ]->slug; 
  1143.             } else if ( isset( self::$_plugins_info->response ) && 
  1144.                         isset( self::$_plugins_info->response[ $basename ] ) && 
  1145.                         ! empty( self::$_plugins_info->response[ $basename ]->slug ) 
  1146.  ) { 
  1147.                 $slug = self::$_plugins_info->response[ $basename ]->slug; 
  1148.             } 
  1149.         } 
  1150.  
  1151.         if ( empty( $slug ) ) { 
  1152.             // Try to find slug from FS data. 
  1153.             $slug = self::find_slug_by_basename( $basename ); 
  1154.         } 
  1155.  
  1156.         if ( empty( $slug ) ) { 
  1157.             // Fallback to plugin's folder name. 
  1158.             $slug = dirname( $basename ); 
  1159.         } 
  1160.  
  1161.         return $slug; 
  1162.     } 
  1163.  
  1164.     private static $_statics_loaded = false; 
  1165.  
  1166.     /** 
  1167.      * Load static resources. 
  1168.      * 
  1169.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  1170.      * @since  1.0.1 
  1171.      */ 
  1172.     private static function _load_required_static() { 
  1173.         if ( self::$_statics_loaded ) { 
  1174.             return; 
  1175.         } 
  1176.  
  1177.         self::$_static_logger = FS_Logger::get_logger( WP_FS__SLUG, WP_FS__DEBUG_SDK, WP_FS__ECHO_DEBUG_SDK ); 
  1178.  
  1179.         self::$_static_logger->entrance(); 
  1180.  
  1181.         self::$_accounts = FS_Option_Manager::get_manager( WP_FS__ACCOUNTS_OPTION_NAME, true ); 
  1182.  
  1183.         self::$_global_admin_notices = FS_Admin_Notice_Manager::instance( 'global' ); 
  1184.  
  1185.         // Configure which Freemius powered plugins should be auto updated. 
  1186. //            add_filter( 'auto_update_plugin', '_include_plugins_in_auto_update', 10, 2 ); 
  1187.  
  1188.         add_action( 'admin_menu', array( 'Freemius', 'add_debug_page' ) ); 
  1189.  
  1190.         add_action( "wp_ajax_fs_toggle_debug_mode", array( 'Freemius', '_toggle_debug_mode' ) ); 
  1191.  
  1192.         add_action( 'plugins_loaded', array( 'Freemius', '_load_textdomain' ), 1 ); 
  1193.  
  1194.         self::$_statics_loaded = true; 
  1195.     } 
  1196.

  1218.  ); 
  1219.  
  1220.         // @todo Load for themes. 
  1221.     }

  1229.     /** 
  1230.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  1231.      * @since  1.0.8 
  1232.      */ 
  1233.     static function add_debug_page() { 
  1234.         if ( ! current_user_can( 'activate_plugins' ) ) { 
  1235.             return; 
  1236.         } 
  1237.  
  1238.         self::$_static_logger->entrance(); 
  1239.  
  1240.         $title = sprintf( '%s [v.%s]', __fs( 'freemius-debug' ), WP_FS__SDK_VERSION ); 
  1241.  
  1242.         if ( WP_FS__DEV_MODE ) { 
  1243.             // Add top-level debug menu item. 
  1244.             $hook = add_menu_page( 
  1245.                 $title,  
  1246.                 $title,  
  1247.                 'manage_options',  
  1248.                 'freemius',  
  1249.                 array( 'Freemius', '_debug_page_render' ) 
  1250.  ); 
  1251.         } else { 
  1252.             // Add hidden debug page. 
  1253.             $hook = add_submenu_page( 
  1254.                 null,  
  1255.                 $title,  
  1256.                 $title,  
  1257.                 'manage_options',  
  1258.                 'freemius',  
  1259.                 array( 'Freemius', '_debug_page_render' ) 
  1260.  ); 
  1261.         } 
  1262.  
  1263.         add_action( "load-$hook", array( 'Freemius', '_debug_page_actions' ) ); 
  1264.     } 
  1265.  
  1266.     /** 
  1267.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  1268.      * @since  1.1.7.3 
  1269.      */ 
  1270.     static function _toggle_debug_mode() { 
  1271.         if ( in_array( $_POST['is_on'], array( 0, 1 ) ) ) { 
  1272.             update_option( 'fs_debug_mode', $_POST['is_on'] ); 
  1273.         } 
  1274.  
  1275.         exit; 
  1276.     } 
  1277.  
  1278.     /** 
  1279.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  1280.      * @since  1.0.8 
  1281.      */ 
  1282.     static function _debug_page_actions() { 
  1283.         self::_clean_admin_content_section(); 
  1284.  
  1285.         if ( fs_request_is_action( 'restart_freemius' ) ) { 
  1286.             check_admin_referer( 'restart_freemius' ); 
  1287.  
  1288.             // Clear accounts data. 
  1289.             self::$_accounts->clear( true ); 
  1290.  
  1291.             // Clear SDK reference cache. 
  1292.             delete_option( 'fs_active_plugins' ); 
  1293.         } else if ( fs_request_is_action( 'simulate_trial' ) ) { 
  1294.             check_admin_referer( 'simulate_trial' ); 
  1295.  
  1296.             $slug = fs_request_get( 'slug' ); 
  1297.  
  1298.             $fs = freemius( $slug ); 
  1299.  
  1300.             // Update SDK install to at least 24 hours before. 
  1301.             $fs->_storage->install_timestamp = ( time() - WP_FS__TIME_24_HOURS_IN_SEC ); 
  1302.             // Unset the trial shown timestamp. 
  1303.             unset( $fs->_storage->trial_promotion_shown ); 
  1304.         } 
  1305.     } 
  1306.  
  1307.     /** 
  1308.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  1309.      * @since  1.0.8 
  1310.      */ 
  1311.     static function _debug_page_render() { 
  1312.         self::$_static_logger->entrance(); 
  1313.  
  1314.         $sites = self::get_all_sites(); 
  1315.         $users = self::get_all_users(); 
  1316.         $addons = self::get_all_addons(); 
  1317.         $account_addons = self::get_all_account_addons(); 
  1318.         $licenses = self::get_all_licenses(); 
  1319.  
  1320. //            $plans = self::get_all_plans(); 
  1321. //            $licenses = self::get_all_licenses(); 
  1322.  
  1323.         $vars = array( 
  1324.             'sites' => $sites,  
  1325.             'users' => $users,  
  1326.             'addons' => $addons,  
  1327.             'account_addons' => $account_addons,  
  1328.             'licenses' => $licenses,  
  1329.  ); 
  1330.  
  1331.         fs_enqueue_local_style( 'fs_account', '/admin/debug.css' ); 
  1332.         fs_require_once_template( 'debug.php', $vars ); 
  1333.     }

  1336.  
  1337.     #---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- 
  1338.     #region Connectivity Issues 
  1339.     #---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- 
  1340.  
  1341.     /** 
  1342.      * Check if Freemius should be turned on for the current plugin install. 
  1343.      * 
  1344.      * Note: 
  1345.      *  $this->_is_on is updated in has_api_connectivity() 
  1346.      * 
  1347.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  1348.      * @since  1.0.9 
  1349.      * 
  1350.      * @return bool 
  1351.      */ 
  1352.     function is_on() { 
  1353.         self::$_static_logger->entrance(); 
  1354.  
  1355.         if ( isset( $this->_is_on ) ) { 
  1356.             return $this->_is_on; 
  1357.         } 
  1358.  
  1359.         // If already installed or pending then sure it's on :) 
  1360.         if ( $this->is_registered() || $this->is_pending_activation() ) { 
  1361.             $this->_is_on = true; 
  1362.  
  1363.             return true; 
  1364.         } 
  1365.  
  1366.         return false; 
  1367.     } 
  1368.  
  1369.     /** 
  1370.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  1371.      * @since  1.1.7.3 
  1372.      * 
  1373.      * @param bool $flush_if_no_connectivity 
  1374.      * 
  1375.      * @return bool 
  1376.      */ 
  1377.     private function should_run_connectivity_test( $flush_if_no_connectivity = false ) { 
  1378.         if ( ! isset( $this->_storage->connectivity_test ) ) { 
  1379.             // Connectivity test was never executed, or cache was cleared. 
  1380.             return true; 
  1381.         } 
  1382.  
  1383.         if ( WP_FS__PING_API_ON_IP_OR_HOST_CHANGES ) { 
  1384.             if ( WP_FS__IS_HTTP_REQUEST ) { 
  1385.                 if ( $_SERVER['HTTP_HOST'] != $this->_storage->connectivity_test['host'] ) { 
  1386.                     // Domain changed. 
  1387.                     return true; 
  1388.                 } 
  1389.  
  1390.                 if ( WP_FS__REMOTE_ADDR != $this->_storage->connectivity_test['server_ip'] ) { 
  1391.                     // Server IP changed. 
  1392.                     return true; 
  1393.                 } 
  1394.             } 
  1395.         } 
  1396.  
  1397.         if ( $this->_storage->connectivity_test['is_connected'] && 
  1398.              $this->_storage->connectivity_test['is_active'] 
  1399.  ) { 
  1400.             // API connected and Freemius is active - no need to run connectivity check. 
  1401.             return false; 
  1402.         } 
  1403.  
  1404.         if ( $flush_if_no_connectivity ) { 
  1405.             /** 
  1406.              * If explicitly asked to flush when no connectivity - do it only 
  1407.              * if at least 10 sec passed from the last API connectivity test. 
  1408.              */ 
  1409.             return ( isset( $this->_storage->connectivity_test['timestamp'] ) && 
  1410.                      ( WP_FS__SCRIPT_START_TIME - $this->_storage->connectivity_test['timestamp'] ) > 10 ); 
  1411.         } 
  1412.  
  1413.         /** 
  1414.          * @since 1.1.7 Don't check for connectivity on plugin downgrade. 
  1415.          */ 
  1416.         $version = $this->get_plugin_version(); 
  1417.         if ( version_compare( $version, $this->_storage->connectivity_test['version'], '>' ) ) { 
  1418.             // If it's a plugin version upgrade and Freemius is off or no connectivity, run connectivity test. 
  1419.             return true; 
  1420.         } 
  1421.  
  1422.         return false; 
  1423.     } 
  1424.  
  1425.     /** 
  1426.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  1427.      * @since  1.1.7.4 
  1428.      * 
  1429.      * @return object|false 
  1430.      */ 
  1431.     private function ping() { 
  1432.         if ( WP_FS__SIMULATE_NO_API_CONNECTIVITY ) { 
  1433.             return false; 
  1434.         } 
  1435.  
  1436.         $version = $this->get_plugin_version(); 
  1437.  
  1438.         $is_update = $this->apply_filters( 'is_plugin_update', $this->is_plugin_update() ); 
  1439.  
  1440.         return $this->get_api_plugin_scope()->ping( 
  1441.             $this->get_anonymous_id(),  
  1442.             array( 
  1443.                 'is_update' => json_encode( $is_update ),  
  1444.                 'version' => $version,  
  1445.                 'sdk' => $this->version,  
  1446.                 'is_admin' => json_encode( is_admin() ),  
  1447.                 'is_ajax' => json_encode( $this->is_ajax() ),  
  1448.                 'is_cron' => json_encode( $this->is_cron() ),  
  1449.                 'is_http' => json_encode( WP_FS__IS_HTTP_REQUEST ),  
  1450.  ) 
  1451.  ); 
  1452.     } 
  1453.  
  1454.     /** 
  1455.      * Check if there's any connectivity issue to Freemius API. 
  1456.      * 
  1457.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  1458.      * @since  1.0.9 
  1459.      * 
  1460.      * @param bool $flush_if_no_connectivity 
  1461.      * 
  1462.      * @return bool 
  1463.      */ 
  1464.     function has_api_connectivity( $flush_if_no_connectivity = false ) { 
  1465.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  1466.  
  1467.         if ( isset( $this->_has_api_connection ) && ( $this->_has_api_connection || ! $flush_if_no_connectivity ) ) { 
  1468.             return $this->_has_api_connection; 
  1469.         } 
  1470.  
  1471.         if ( WP_FS__SIMULATE_NO_API_CONNECTIVITY && 
  1472.              isset( $this->_storage->connectivity_test ) && 
  1473.              true === $this->_storage->connectivity_test['is_connected'] 
  1474.  ) { 
  1475.             unset( $this->_storage->connectivity_test ); 
  1476.         } 
  1477.  
  1478.         if ( ! $this->should_run_connectivity_test( $flush_if_no_connectivity ) ) { 
  1479.             $this->_has_api_connection = $this->_storage->connectivity_test['is_connected']; 
  1480.             /** 
  1481.              * @since 1.1.6 During dev mode, if there's connectivity - turn Freemius on regardless the configuration. 
  1482.              * 
  1483.              * @since 1.2.1.5 If the user running the premium version then ignore the 'is_active' flag and turn Freemius on to enable license key activation. 
  1484.              */ 
  1485.             $this->_is_on = $this->_storage->connectivity_test['is_active'] || 
  1486.                             $this->is_premium() || 
  1487.                             ( WP_FS__DEV_MODE && $this->_has_api_connection && ! WP_FS__SIMULATE_FREEMIUS_OFF ); 
  1488.  
  1489.             return $this->_has_api_connection; 
  1490.         } 
  1491.  
  1492.         $pong = $this->ping(); 
  1493.         $is_connected = $this->get_api_plugin_scope()->is_valid_ping( $pong ); 
  1494.  
  1495.         if ( ! $is_connected ) { 
  1496.             // API failure. 
  1497.             $this->_add_connectivity_issue_message( $pong ); 
  1498.         } 
  1499.  
  1500.         $this->store_connectivity_info( $pong, $is_connected ); 
  1501.  
  1502.         return $this->_has_api_connection; 
  1503.     } 
  1504.  
  1505.     /** 
  1506.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  1507.      * @since  1.1.7.4 
  1508.      * 
  1509.      * @param object $pong 
  1510.      * @param bool   $is_connected 
  1511.      */ 
  1512.     private function store_connectivity_info( $pong, $is_connected ) { 
  1513.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  1514.  
  1515.         $version = $this->get_plugin_version(); 
  1516.  
  1517.         if ( ! $is_connected || WP_FS__SIMULATE_FREEMIUS_OFF ) { 
  1518.             $is_active = false; 
  1519.         } else { 
  1520.             $is_active = ( isset( $pong->is_active ) && true == $pong->is_active ); 
  1521.         } 
  1522.  
  1523.         $is_active = $this->apply_filters( 
  1524.             'is_on',  
  1525.             $is_active,  
  1526.             $this->is_plugin_update(),  
  1527.             $version 
  1528.  ); 
  1529.  
  1530.         $this->_storage->connectivity_test = array( 
  1531.             'is_connected' => $is_connected,  
  1532.             'host' => $_SERVER['HTTP_HOST'],  
  1533.             'server_ip' => WP_FS__REMOTE_ADDR,  
  1534.             'is_active' => $is_active,  
  1535.             'timestamp' => WP_FS__SCRIPT_START_TIME,  
  1536.             // Last version with connectivity attempt. 
  1537.             'version' => $version,  
  1538.  ); 
  1539.  
  1540.         $this->_has_api_connection = $is_connected; 
  1541.         $this->_is_on = $is_active || ( WP_FS__DEV_MODE && $is_connected && ! WP_FS__SIMULATE_FREEMIUS_OFF ); 
  1542.     } 
  1543.  
  1544.     /** 
  1545.      * Force turning Freemius on. 
  1546.      * 
  1547.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  1548.      * @since  1.1.8.1 
  1549.      * 
  1550.      * @return bool TRUE if successfully turned on. 
  1551.      */ 
  1552.     private function turn_on() { 
  1553.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  1554.  
  1555.         if ( $this->is_on() || ! isset( $this->_storage->connectivity_test['is_active'] ) ) { 
  1556.             return false; 
  1557.         } 
  1558.  
  1559.         $updated_connectivity = $this->_storage->connectivity_test; 
  1560.         $updated_connectivity['is_active'] = true; 
  1561.         $updated_connectivity['timestamp'] = WP_FS__SCRIPT_START_TIME; 
  1562.         $this->_storage->connectivity_test = $updated_connectivity; 
  1563.  
  1564.         $this->_is_on = true; 
  1565.  
  1566.         return true; 
  1567.     } 
  1568.  
  1569.     /** 
  1570.      * Anonymous and unique site identifier (Hash). 
  1571.      * 
  1572.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  1573.      * @since  1.1.0 
  1574.      * 
  1575.      * @return string 
  1576.      */ 
  1577.     function get_anonymous_id() { 
  1578.         $unique_id = self::$_accounts->get_option( 'unique_id' ); 
  1579.  
  1580.         if ( empty( $unique_id ) || ! is_string( $unique_id ) ) { 
  1581.             $key = get_site_url(); 
  1582.  
  1583.             // If localhost, assign microtime instead of domain. 
  1584.             if ( WP_FS__IS_LOCALHOST || 
  1585.                  false !== strpos( $key, 'localhost' ) || 
  1586.                  false === strpos( $key, '.' ) 
  1587.  ) { 
  1588.                 $key = microtime(); 
  1589.             } 
  1590.  
  1591.             $unique_id = md5( $key ); 
  1592.  
  1593.             self::$_accounts->set_option( 'unique_id', $unique_id, true ); 
  1594.         } 
  1595.  
  1596.         $this->_logger->departure( $unique_id ); 
  1597.  
  1598.         return $unique_id; 
  1599.     } 
  1600.  
  1601.     /** 
  1602.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  1603.      * @since  1.1.7.4 
  1604.      * 
  1605.      * @return \WP_User 
  1606.      */ 
  1607.     static function _get_current_wp_user() { 
  1608.         self::require_pluggable_essentials(); 
  1609.  
  1610.         return wp_get_current_user(); 
  1611.     } 
  1612.  
  1613.     /** 
  1614.      * Generate API connectivity issue message. 
  1615.      * 
  1616.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  1617.      * @since  1.0.9 
  1618.      * 
  1619.      * @param mixed $api_result 
  1620.      * @param bool  $is_first_failure 
  1621.      */ 
  1622.     function _add_connectivity_issue_message( $api_result, $is_first_failure = true ) { 
  1623.         if ( ! $this->is_premium() && $this->_enable_anonymous ) { 
  1624.             // Don't add message if it's the free version and can run anonymously. 
  1625.             return; 
  1626.         } 
  1627.  
  1628.         if ( ! function_exists( 'wp_nonce_url' ) ) { 
  1629.             require_once( ABSPATH . 'wp-includes/functions.php' ); 
  1630.         } 
  1631.  
  1632.         $current_user = self::_get_current_wp_user(); 
  1633. //            $admin_email = get_option( 'admin_email' ); 
  1634.         $admin_email = $current_user->user_email; 
  1635.  
  1636.         $message = false; 
  1637.         if ( is_object( $api_result ) && 
  1638.              isset( $api_result->error ) && 
  1639.              isset( $api_result->error->code ) 
  1640.  ) { 
  1641.             switch ( $api_result->error->code ) { 
  1642.                 case 'curl_missing': 
  1643.                     $message = sprintf( 
  1644.                         __fs( 'x-requires-access-to-api', $this->_slug ) . ' ' . 
  1645.                         __fs( 'curl-missing-message', $this->_slug ) . ' ' . 
  1646.                         ' %s',  
  1647.                         '<b>' . $this->get_plugin_name() . '</b>',  
  1648.                         sprintf( 
  1649.                             '<ol id="fs_firewall_issue_options"><li>%s</li><li>%s</li><li>%s</li></ol>',  
  1650.                             sprintf( 
  1651.                                 '<a class="fs-resolve" data-type="curl" href="#"><b>%s</b></a>%s',  
  1652.                                 __fs( 'curl-missing-no-clue-title', $this->_slug ),  
  1653.                                 ' - ' . sprintf( 
  1654.                                     __fs( 'curl-missing-no-clue-desc', $this->_slug ),  
  1655.                                     '<a href="mailto:' . $admin_email . '">' . $admin_email . '</a>' 
  1656.  ) 
  1657.  ),  
  1658.                             sprintf( 
  1659.                                 '<b>%s</b> - %s',  
  1660.                                 __fs( 'sysadmin-title', $this->_slug ),  
  1661.                                 __fs( 'curl-missing-sysadmin-desc', $this->_slug ) 
  1662.  ),  
  1663.                             sprintf( 
  1664.                                 '<a href="%s"><b>%s</b></a>%s',  
  1665.                                 wp_nonce_url( 'plugins.php?action=deactivate&plugin=' . $this->_plugin_basename . '&plugin_status=' . 'all' . '&paged=' . '1' . '&s=' . '', 'deactivate-plugin_' . $this->_plugin_basename ),  
  1666.                                 __fs( 'deactivate-plugin-title', $this->_slug ),  
  1667.                                 ' - ' . __fs( 'deactivate-plugin-desc', 'freemius', $this->_slug ) 
  1668.  ) 
  1669.  ) 
  1670.  ); 
  1671.                     break; 
  1672.                 case 'cloudflare_ddos_protection': 
  1673.                     $message = sprintf( 
  1674.                         __fs( 'x-requires-access-to-api', $this->_slug ) . ' ' . 
  1675.                         __fs( 'cloudflare-blocks-connection-message', $this->_slug ) . ' ' . 
  1676.                         __fs( 'happy-to-resolve-issue-asap', $this->_slug ) . 
  1677.                         ' %s',  
  1678.                         '<b>' . $this->get_plugin_name() . '</b>',  
  1679.                         sprintf( 
  1680.                             '<ol id="fs_firewall_issue_options"><li>%s</li><li>%s</li><li>%s</li></ol>',  
  1681.                             sprintf( 
  1682.                                 '<a class="fs-resolve" data-type="cloudflare" href="#"><b>%s</b></a>%s',  
  1683.                                 __fs( 'fix-issue-title', $this->_slug ),  
  1684.                                 ' - ' . sprintf( 
  1685.                                     __fs( 'fix-issue-desc', $this->_slug ),  
  1686.                                     '<a href="mailto:' . $admin_email . '">' . $admin_email . '</a>' 
  1687.  ) 
  1688.  ),  
  1689.                             sprintf( 
  1690.                                 '<a href="%s" target="_blank"><b>%s</b></a>%s',  
  1691.                                 sprintf( 'https://wordpress.org/plugins/%s/download/', $this->_slug ),  
  1692.                                 __fs( 'install-previous-title', $this->_slug ),  
  1693.                                 ' - ' . __fs( 'install-previous-desc', $this->_slug ) 
  1694.  ),  
  1695.                             sprintf( 
  1696.                                 '<a href="%s"><b>%s</b></a>%s',  
  1697.                                 wp_nonce_url( 'plugins.php?action=deactivate&plugin=' . $this->_plugin_basename . '&plugin_status=' . 'all' . '&paged=' . '1' . '&s=' . '', 'deactivate-plugin_' . $this->_plugin_basename ),  
  1698.                                 __fs( 'deactivate-plugin-title', $this->_slug ),  
  1699.                                 ' - ' . __fs( 'deactivate-plugin-desc', $this->_slug ) 
  1700.  ) 
  1701.  ) 
  1702.  ); 
  1703.                     break; 
  1704.                 case 'squid_cache_block': 
  1705.                     $message = sprintf( 
  1706.                         __fs( 'x-requires-access-to-api', $this->_slug ) . ' ' . 
  1707.                         __fs( 'squid-blocks-connection-message', $this->_slug ) . 
  1708.                         ' %s',  
  1709.                         '<b>' . $this->get_plugin_name() . '</b>',  
  1710.                         sprintf( 
  1711.                             '<ol id="fs_firewall_issue_options"><li>%s</li><li>%s</li><li>%s</li></ol>',  
  1712.                             sprintf( 
  1713.                                 '<a class="fs-resolve" data-type="squid" href="#"><b>%s</b></a>%s',  
  1714.                                 __fs( 'squid-no-clue-title', $this->_slug ),  
  1715.                                 ' - ' . sprintf( 
  1716.                                     __fs( 'squid-no-clue-desc', $this->_slug ),  
  1717.                                     '<a href="mailto:' . $admin_email . '">' . $admin_email . '</a>' 
  1718.  ) 
  1719.  ),  
  1720.                             sprintf( 
  1721.                                 '<b>%s</b> - %s',  
  1722.                                 __fs( 'sysadmin-title', $this->_slug ),  
  1723.                                 sprintf( 
  1724.                                     __fs( 'squid-sysadmin-desc', $this->_slug ),  
  1725.                                     // We use a filter since the plugin might require additional API connectivity. 
  1726.                                     '<b>' . implode( ', ', $this->apply_filters( 'api_domains', array( 'api.freemius.com' ) ) ) . '</b>' ) 
  1727.  ),  
  1728.                             sprintf( 
  1729.                                 '<a href="%s"><b>%s</b></a>%s',  
  1730.                                 wp_nonce_url( 'plugins.php?action=deactivate&plugin=' . $this->_plugin_basename . '&plugin_status=' . 'all' . '&paged=' . '1' . '&s=' . '', 'deactivate-plugin_' . $this->_plugin_basename ),  
  1731.                                 __fs( 'deactivate-plugin-title', $this->_slug ),  
  1732.                                 ' - ' . __fs( 'deactivate-plugin-desc', $this->_slug ) 
  1733.  ) 
  1734.  ) 
  1735.  ); 
  1736.                     break; 
  1737. //                    default: 
  1738. //                        $message = __fs( 'connectivity-test-fails-message', $this->_slug ); 
  1739. //                        break; 
  1740.             } 
  1741.         } 
  1742.  
  1743.         $message_id = 'failed_connect_api'; 
  1744.         $type = 'error'; 
  1745.  
  1746.         if ( false === $message ) { 
  1747.             if ( $is_first_failure ) { 
  1748.                 // First attempt failed. 
  1749.                 $message = sprintf( 
  1750.                     __fs( 'x-requires-access-to-api', $this->_slug ) . ' ' . 
  1751.                     __fs( 'connectivity-test-fails-message', $this->_slug ) . ' ' . 
  1752.                     __fs( 'connectivity-test-maybe-temporary', $this->_slug ) . '<br><br>' . 
  1753.                     '%s',  
  1754.                     '<b>' . $this->get_plugin_name() . '</b>',  
  1755.                     sprintf( 
  1756.                         '<div id="fs_firewall_issue_options">%s %s</div>',  
  1757.                         sprintf( 
  1758.                             '<a  class="button button-primary fs-resolve" data-type="retry_ping" href="#">%s</a>',  
  1759.                             __fs( 'yes-do-your-thing', $this->_slug ) 
  1760.  ),  
  1761.                         sprintf( 
  1762.                             '<a href="%s" class="button">%s</a>',  
  1763.                             wp_nonce_url( 'plugins.php?action=deactivate&plugin=' . $this->_plugin_basename . '&plugin_status=' . 'all' . '&paged=' . '1' . '&s=' . '', 'deactivate-plugin_' . $this->_plugin_basename ),  
  1764.                             __fs( 'no-deactivate', $this->_slug ) 
  1765.  ) 
  1766.  ) 
  1767.  ); 
  1768.  
  1769.                 $message_id = 'failed_connect_api_first'; 
  1770.                 $type = 'promotion'; 
  1771.             } else { 
  1772.                 // Second connectivity attempt failed. 
  1773.                 $message = sprintf( 
  1774.                     __fs( 'x-requires-access-to-api', $this->_slug ) . ' ' . 
  1775.                     __fs( 'connectivity-test-fails-message', $this->_slug ) . ' ' . 
  1776.                     __fs( 'happy-to-resolve-issue-asap', $this->_slug ) . 
  1777.                     ' %s',  
  1778.                     '<b>' . $this->get_plugin_name() . '</b>',  
  1779.                     sprintf( 
  1780.                         '<ol id="fs_firewall_issue_options"><li>%s</li><li>%s</li><li>%s</li></ol>',  
  1781.                         sprintf( 
  1782.                             '<a class="fs-resolve" data-type="general" href="#"><b>%s</b></a>%s',  
  1783.                             __fs( 'fix-issue-title', $this->_slug ),  
  1784.                             ' - ' . sprintf( 
  1785.                                 __fs( 'fix-issue-desc', $this->_slug ),  
  1786.                                 '<a href="mailto:' . $admin_email . '">' . $admin_email . '</a>' 
  1787.  ) 
  1788.  ),  
  1789.                         sprintf( 
  1790.                             '<a href="%s" target="_blank"><b>%s</b></a>%s',  
  1791.                             sprintf( 'https://wordpress.org/plugins/%s/download/', $this->_slug ),  
  1792.                             __fs( 'install-previous-title', $this->_slug ),  
  1793.                             ' - ' . __fs( 'install-previous-desc', $this->_slug ) 
  1794.  ),  
  1795.                         sprintf( 
  1796.                             '<a href="%s"><b>%s</b></a>%s',  
  1797.                             wp_nonce_url( 'plugins.php?action=deactivate&plugin=' . $this->_plugin_basename . '&plugin_status=' . 'all' . '&paged=' . '1' . '&s=' . '', 'deactivate-plugin_' . $this->_plugin_basename ),  
  1798.                             __fs( 'deactivate-plugin-title', $this->_slug ),  
  1799.                             ' - ' . __fs( 'deactivate-plugin-desc', $this->_slug ) 
  1800.  ) 
  1801.  ) 
  1802.  ); 
  1803.             } 
  1804.         } 
  1805.  
  1806.         $this->_admin_notices->add_sticky( 
  1807.             $message,  
  1808.             $message_id,  
  1809.             __fs( 'oops', $this->_slug ) . '...',  
  1810.             $type 
  1811.  ); 
  1812.     } 
  1813.  
  1814.     /** 
  1815.      * Handle user request to resolve connectivity issue. 
  1816.      * This method will send an email to Freemius API technical staff for resolution. 
  1817.      * The email will contain server's info and installed plugins (might be caching issue). 
  1818.      * 
  1819.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  1820.      * @since  1.0.9 
  1821.      */ 
  1822.     function _email_about_firewall_issue() { 
  1823.         $this->_admin_notices->remove_sticky( 'failed_connect_api' ); 
  1824.  
  1825.         $pong = $this->ping(); 
  1826.  
  1827.         $is_connected = $this->get_api_plugin_scope()->is_valid_ping( $pong ); 
  1828.  
  1829.         if ( $is_connected ) { 
  1830.             $this->store_connectivity_info( $pong, $is_connected ); 
  1831.  
  1832.             echo $this->get_after_plugin_activation_redirect_url(); 
  1833.             exit; 
  1834.         } 
  1835.  
  1836.         $current_user = self::_get_current_wp_user(); 
  1837.         $admin_email = $current_user->user_email; 
  1838.  
  1839.         $error_type = fs_request_get( 'error_type', 'general' ); 
  1840.  
  1841.         switch ( $error_type ) { 
  1842.             case 'squid': 
  1843.                 $title = 'Squid ACL Blocking Issue'; 
  1844.                 break; 
  1845.             case 'cloudflare': 
  1846.                 $title = 'CloudFlare Blocking Issue'; 
  1847.                 break; 
  1848.             default: 
  1849.                 $title = 'API Connectivity Issue'; 
  1850.                 break; 
  1851.         } 
  1852.  
  1853.         $custom_email_sections = array(); 
  1854.  
  1855.         if ( 'squid' === $error_type ) { 
  1856.             // Override the 'Site' email section. 
  1857.             $custom_email_sections['site'] = array( 
  1858.                 'rows' => array( 
  1859.                     'hosting_company' => array( 'Hosting Company', fs_request_get( 'hosting_company' ) ) 
  1860.  ) 
  1861.  ); 
  1862.         } 
  1863.  
  1864.         // Add 'API Error' custom email section. 
  1865.         $custom_email_sections['api_error'] = array( 
  1866.             'title' => 'API Error',  
  1867.             'rows' => array( 
  1868.                 'ping' => array( is_string( $pong ) ? htmlentities( $pong ) : json_encode( $pong ) ) 
  1869.  ) 
  1870.  ); 
  1871.  
  1872.         // Add PHP info for deeper investigation. 
  1873.         ob_start(); 
  1874.         phpinfo(); 
  1875.         $php_info = ob_get_clean(); 
  1876.         $custom_email_sections['php_info'] = array( 
  1877.             'title' => 'PHP Info',  
  1878.             'rows' => array( 
  1879.                 'info' => array( $php_info ) 
  1880.  ) 
  1881.  ); 
  1882.  
  1883.         // Send email with technical details to resolve CloudFlare's firewall unnecessary protection. 
  1884.         $this->send_email( 
  1885.             'api@freemius.com', // recipient 
  1886.             $title . ' [' . $this->get_plugin_name() . ']', // subject 
  1887.             $custom_email_sections,  
  1888.             array( "Reply-To: $admin_email <$admin_email>" ) // headers 
  1889.  ); 
  1890.  
  1891.         $this->_admin_notices->add_sticky( 
  1892.             sprintf( 
  1893.                 __fs( 'fix-request-sent-message', $this->_slug ),  
  1894.                 '<a href="mailto:' . $admin_email . '">' . $admin_email . '</a>' 
  1895.  ),  
  1896.             'server_details_sent' 
  1897.  ); 
  1898.  
  1899.         // Action was taken, tell that API connectivity troubleshooting should be off now. 
  1900.  
  1901.         echo "1"; 
  1902.         exit; 
  1903.     } 
  1904.  
  1905.     /** 
  1906.      * Handle connectivity test retry approved by the user. 
  1907.      * 
  1908.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  1909.      * @since  1.1.7.4 
  1910.      */ 
  1911.     function _retry_connectivity_test() { 
  1912.         $this->_admin_notices->remove_sticky( 'failed_connect_api_first' ); 
  1913.  
  1914.         $pong = $this->ping(); 
  1915.  
  1916.         $is_connected = $this->get_api_plugin_scope()->is_valid_ping( $pong ); 
  1917.  
  1918.         if ( $is_connected ) { 
  1919.             $this->store_connectivity_info( $pong, $is_connected ); 
  1920.  
  1921.             echo $this->get_after_plugin_activation_redirect_url(); 
  1922.         } else { 
  1923.             // Add connectivity issue message after 2nd failed attempt. 
  1924.             $this->_add_connectivity_issue_message( $pong, false ); 
  1925.  
  1926.             echo "1"; 
  1927.         } 
  1928.  
  1929.         exit; 
  1930.     } 
  1931.  
  1932.     static function _add_firewall_issues_javascript() { 
  1933.         $params = array(); 
  1934.         fs_require_once_template( 'firewall-issues-js.php', $params ); 
  1935.     } 
  1936.
