  1938.  
  1939.     #---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- 
  1940.     #region Email 
  1941.     #---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- 
  1942.  
  1943.     /** 
  1944.      * Generates and sends an HTML email with customizable sections. 
  1945.      * 
  1946.      * @author Leo Fajardo (@leorw) 
  1947.      * @since  1.1.2 
  1948.      * 
  1949.      * @param string $to_address 
  1950.      * @param string $subject 
  1951.      * @param array  $sections 
  1952.      * @param array  $headers 
  1953.      * 
  1954.      * @return bool Whether the email contents were sent successfully. 
  1955.      */ 
  1956.     private function send_email( 
  1957.         $to_address,  
  1958.         $subject,  
  1959.         $sections = array(),  
  1960.         $headers = array() 
  1961.  ) { 
  1962.         $default_sections = $this->get_email_sections(); 
  1963.  
  1964.         // Insert new sections or replace the default email sections. 
  1965.         if ( is_array( $sections ) && ! empty( $sections ) ) { 
  1966.             foreach ( $sections as $section_id => $custom_section ) { 
  1967.                 if ( ! isset( $default_sections[ $section_id ] ) ) { 
  1968.                     // If the section does not exist, add it. 
  1969.                     $default_sections[ $section_id ] = $custom_section; 
  1970.                 } else { 
  1971.                     // If the section already exists, override it. 
  1972.                     $current_section = $default_sections[ $section_id ]; 
  1973.  
  1974.                     // Replace the current section's title if a custom section title exists. 
  1975.                     if ( isset( $custom_section['title'] ) ) { 
  1976.                         $current_section['title'] = $custom_section['title']; 
  1977.                     } 
  1978.  
  1979.                     // Insert new rows under the current section or replace the default rows. 
  1980.                     if ( isset( $custom_section['rows'] ) && is_array( $custom_section['rows'] ) && ! empty( $custom_section['rows'] ) ) { 
  1981.                         foreach ( $custom_section['rows'] as $row_id => $row ) { 
  1982.                             $current_section['rows'][ $row_id ] = $row; 
  1983.                         } 
  1984.                     } 
  1985.  
  1986.                     $default_sections[ $section_id ] = $current_section; 
  1987.                 } 
  1988.             } 
  1989.         } 
  1990.  
  1991.         $vars = array( 'sections' => $default_sections ); 
  1992.         $message = fs_get_template( 'email.php', $vars ); 
  1993.  
  1994.         // Set the type of email to HTML. 
  1995.         $headers[] = 'Content-type: text/html'; 
  1996.  
  1997.         $header_string = implode( "\r\n", $headers ); 
  1998.  
  1999.         return wp_mail( 
  2000.             $to_address,  
  2001.             $subject,  
  2002.             $message,  
  2003.             $header_string 
  2004.  ); 
  2005.     } 
  2006.  
  2007.     /** 
  2008.      * Generates the data for the sections of the email content. 
  2009.      * 
  2010.      * @author Leo Fajardo (@leorw) 
  2011.      * @since  1.1.2 
  2012.      * 
  2013.      * @return array 
  2014.      */ 
  2015.     private function get_email_sections() { 
  2016.         // Retrieve the current user's information so that we can get the user's email, first name, and last name below. 
  2017.         $current_user = self::_get_current_wp_user(); 
  2018.  
  2019.         // Retrieve the cURL version information so that we can get the version number below. 
  2020.         $curl_version_information = curl_version(); 
  2021.  
  2022.         $active_plugin = self::get_active_plugins(); 
  2023.  
  2024.         // Generate the list of active plugins separated by new line.  
  2025.         $active_plugin_string = ''; 
  2026.         foreach ( $active_plugin as $plugin ) { 
  2027.             $active_plugin_string .= sprintf( 
  2028.                 '<a href="%s">%s</a> [v%s]<br>',  
  2029.                 $plugin['PluginURI'],  
  2030.                 $plugin['Name'],  
  2031.                 $plugin['Version'] 
  2032.  ); 
  2033.         } 
  2034.  
  2035.         $server_ip = WP_FS__REMOTE_ADDR; 
  2036.  
  2037.         // Generate the default email sections. 
  2038.         $sections = array( 
  2039.             'sdk' => array( 
  2040.                 'title' => 'SDK',  
  2041.                 'rows' => array( 
  2042.                     'fs_version' => array( 'FS Version', $this->version ),  
  2043.                     'curl_version' => array( 'cURL Version', $curl_version_information['version'] ) 
  2044.  ) 
  2045.  ),  
  2046.             'plugin' => array( 
  2047.                 'title' => 'Plugin',  
  2048.                 'rows' => array( 
  2049.                     'name' => array( 'Name', $this->get_plugin_name() ),  
  2050.                     'version' => array( 'Version', $this->get_plugin_version() ) 
  2051.  ) 
  2052.  ),  
  2053.             'site' => array( 
  2054.                 'title' => 'Site',  
  2055.                 'rows' => array( 
  2056.                     'unique_id' => array( 'Address', $this->get_anonymous_id() ),  
  2057.                     'address' => array( 'Address', site_url() ),  
  2058.                     'host' => array( 
  2059.                         'HTTP_HOST',  
  2060.                         ( ! empty( $_SERVER['HTTP_HOST'] ) ? $_SERVER['HTTP_HOST'] : '' ) 
  2061.  ),  
  2062.                     'server_addr' => array( 
  2063.                         'SERVER_ADDR',  
  2064.                         '<a href="http://www.projecthoneypot.org/ip_' . $server_ip . '">' . $server_ip . '</a>' 
  2065.  ) 
  2066.  ) 
  2067.  ),  
  2068.             'user' => array( 
  2069.                 'title' => 'User',  
  2070.                 'rows' => array( 
  2071.                     'email' => array( 'Email', $current_user->user_email ),  
  2072.                     'first' => array( 'First', $current_user->user_firstname ),  
  2073.                     'last' => array( 'Last', $current_user->user_lastname ) 
  2074.  ) 
  2075.  ),  
  2076.             'plugins' => array( 
  2077.                 'title' => 'Plugins',  
  2078.                 'rows' => array( 
  2079.                     'active_plugins' => array( 'Active Plugins', $active_plugin_string ) 
  2080.  ) 
  2081.  ),  
  2082.  ); 
  2083.  
  2084.         // Allow the sections to be modified by other code. 
  2085.         $sections = $this->apply_filters( 'email_template_sections', $sections ); 
  2086.  
  2087.         return $sections; 
  2088.     } 
  2089.  
  2090.     #endregion 
  2091.  
  2092.     #---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- 
  2093.     #region Initialization 
  2094.     #---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- 
  2095.  
  2096.     /** 
  2097.      * Init plugin's Freemius instance. 
  2098.      * 
  2099.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  2100.      * @since  1.0.1 
  2101.      * 
  2102.      * @param number $id 
  2103.      * @param string $public_key 
  2104.      * @param bool   $is_live 
  2105.      * @param bool   $is_premium 
  2106.      */ 
  2107.     function init( $id, $public_key, $is_live = true, $is_premium = true ) { 
  2108.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  2109.  
  2110.         $this->dynamic_init( array( 
  2111.             'id' => $id,  
  2112.             'public_key' => $public_key,  
  2113.             'is_live' => $is_live,  
  2114.             'is_premium' => $is_premium,  
  2115.  ) ); 
  2116.     } 
  2117.  
  2118.     /** 
  2119.      * Dynamic initiator, originally created to support initiation 
  2120.      * with parent_id for add-ons. 
  2121.      * 
  2122.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  2123.      * @since  1.0.6 
  2124.      * 
  2125.      * @param array $plugin_info 
  2126.      * 
  2127.      * @throws Freemius_Exception 
  2128.      */ 
  2129.     function dynamic_init( array $plugin_info ) { 
  2130.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  2131.  
  2132.         $this->parse_settings( $plugin_info ); 
  2133.  
  2134.         if ( $this->should_stop_execution() ) { 
  2135.             return; 
  2136.         } 
  2137.  
  2138.         if ( ! $this->is_registered() ) { 
  2139.             if ( $this->is_anonymous() ) { 
  2140.                 // If user skipped, no need to test connectivity. 
  2141.                 $this->_has_api_connection = true; 
  2142.                 $this->_is_on = true; 
  2143.             } else { 
  2144.                 if ( ! $this->has_api_connectivity() ) { 
  2145.                     if ( $this->_admin_notices->has_sticky( 'failed_connect_api_first' ) || 
  2146.                          $this->_admin_notices->has_sticky( 'failed_connect_api' ) 
  2147.  ) { 
  2148.                         if ( ! $this->_enable_anonymous || $this->is_premium() ) { 
  2149.                             // If anonymous mode is disabled, add firewall admin-notice message. 
  2150.                             add_action( 'admin_footer', array( 'Freemius', '_add_firewall_issues_javascript' ) ); 
  2151.  
  2152.                             $this->add_ajax_action( 'resolve_firewall_issues', array( 
  2153.                                 &$this,  
  2154.                                 '_email_about_firewall_issue' 
  2155.  ) ); 
  2156.  
  2157.                             $this->add_ajax_action( 'retry_connectivity_test', array( 
  2158.                                 &$this,  
  2159.                                 '_retry_connectivity_test' 
  2160.  ) ); 
  2161.                         } 
  2162.                     } 
  2163.  
  2164.                     return; 
  2165.                 } else { 
  2166.                     $this->_admin_notices->remove_sticky( array( 
  2167.                         'failed_connect_api_first',  
  2168.                         'failed_connect_api',  
  2169.  ) ); 
  2170.  
  2171.                     if ( $this->_anonymous_mode ) { 
  2172.                         // Simulate anonymous mode. 
  2173.                         $this->_is_anonymous = true; 
  2174.                     } 
  2175.                 } 
  2176.             } 
  2177.  
  2178.             // Check if Freemius is on for the current plugin. 
  2179.             // This MUST be executed after all the plugin variables has been loaded. 
  2180.             if ( ! $this->is_on() ) { 
  2181.                 return; 
  2182.             } 
  2183.         } 
  2184.  
  2185.         if ( $this->has_api_connectivity() ) { 
  2186.             if ( $this->is_cron() ) { 
  2187.                 $this->hook_callback_to_sync_cron(); 
  2188.             } else if ( $this->is_user_in_admin() ) { 
  2189.                 /** 
  2190.                  * Schedule daily data sync cron if: 
  2191.                  * 
  2192.                  *  1. User opted-in (for tracking). 
  2193.                  *  2. If skipped, but later upgraded (opted-in via upgrade). 
  2194.                  * 
  2195.                  * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  2196.                  * @since  1.1.7.3 
  2197.                  * 
  2198.                  */ 
  2199.                 if ( $this->is_registered() ) { 
  2200.                     if ( ! $this->is_sync_cron_on() && $this->is_tracking_allowed() ) { 
  2201.                         $this->schedule_sync_cron(); 
  2202.                     } 
  2203.                 } 
  2204.  
  2205.                 /** 
  2206.                  * Check if requested for manual blocking background sync. 
  2207.                  */ 
  2208.                 if ( fs_request_has( 'background_sync' ) ) { 
  2209.                     $this->run_manual_sync(); 
  2210.                 } 
  2211.             } 
  2212.         } 
  2213.  
  2214.         if ( $this->is_registered() ) { 
  2215.             $this->hook_callback_to_install_sync(); 
  2216.         } 
  2217.  
  2218.         if ( $this->is_addon() ) { 
  2219.             if ( $this->is_parent_plugin_installed() ) { 
  2220.                 // Link to parent FS. 
  2221.                 $this->_parent = self::get_instance_by_id( $this->_plugin->parent_plugin_id ); 
  2222.  
  2223.                 // Get parent plugin reference. 
  2224.                 $this->_parent_plugin = $this->_parent->get_plugin(); 
  2225.             } 
  2226.         } 
  2227.  
  2228.         if ( $this->is_user_in_admin() ) { 
  2229.             if ( $this->is_plugins_page() ) { 
  2230.                 $this->hook_plugin_action_links(); 
  2231.             } 
  2232.  
  2233.             if ( $this->is_addon() ) { 
  2234.                 if ( ! $this->is_parent_plugin_installed() ) { 
  2235.                     $parent_name = $this->get_option( $plugin_info, 'parent_name', null ); 
  2236.  
  2237.                     if ( isset( $plugin_info['parent'] ) ) { 
  2238.                         $parent_name = $this->get_option( $plugin_info['parent'], 'name', null ); 
  2239.                     } 
  2240.  
  2241.                     $this->_admin_notices->add( 
  2242.                         ( ! empty( $parent_name ) ? 
  2243.                             sprintf( __fs( 'addon-x-cannot-run-without-y', $this->_slug ), $this->get_plugin_name(), $parent_name ) : 
  2244.                             sprintf( __fs( 'addon-x-cannot-run-without-parent', $this->_slug ), $this->get_plugin_name() ) 
  2245.  ),  
  2246.                         __fs( 'oops', $this->_slug ) . '...',  
  2247.                         'error' 
  2248.  ); 
  2249.  
  2250.                     return; 
  2251.                 } else { 
  2252.                     if ( $this->_parent->is_registered() && ! $this->is_registered() ) { 
  2253.                         // If parent plugin activated, automatically install add-on for the user. 
  2254.                         $this->_activate_addon_account( $this->_parent ); 
  2255.                     } 
  2256.  
  2257.                     // @todo This should be only executed on activation. It should be migrated to register_activation_hook() together with other activation related logic. 
  2258.                     if ( $this->is_premium() ) { 
  2259.                         // Remove add-on download admin-notice. 
  2260.                         $this->_parent->_admin_notices->remove_sticky( array( 
  2261.                             'addon_plan_upgraded_' . $this->_slug,  
  2262.                             'no_addon_license_' . $this->_slug,  
  2263.  ) ); 
  2264.                     } 
  2265.  
  2266.                     $this->deactivate_premium_only_addon_without_license(); 
  2267.                 } 
  2268.             } else { 
  2269.                 add_action( 'admin_init', array( &$this, '_admin_init_action' ) ); 
  2270.  
  2271.                 if ( $this->has_addons() && 
  2272.                      'plugin-information' === fs_request_get( 'tab', false ) && 
  2273.                      $this->get_id() == fs_request_get( 'parent_plugin_id', false ) 
  2274.  ) { 
  2275.                     require_once WP_FS__DIR_INCLUDES . '/fs-plugin-info-dialog.php'; 
  2276.  
  2277.                     new FS_Plugin_Info_Dialog( $this ); 
  2278.                 } 
  2279.             } 
  2280.  
  2281.             if ( $this->is_premium() ) { 
  2282.                 new FS_Plugin_Updater( $this ); 
  2283.             } 
  2284.  
  2285. //                if ( $this->is_registered() || 
  2286. //                     $this->is_anonymous() || 
  2287. //                     $this->is_pending_activation() 
  2288. // ) { 
  2289. //                    $this->_init_admin(); 
  2290. //                } 
  2291.         } 
  2292.  
  2293.         $this->do_action( 'initiated' ); 
  2294.  
  2295.         if ( $this->_storage->prev_is_premium !== $this->_plugin->is_premium ) { 
  2296.             if ( isset( $this->_storage->prev_is_premium ) ) { 
  2297.                 $this->apply_filters( 
  2298.                     'after_code_type_change',  
  2299.                     // New code type. 
  2300.                     $this->_plugin->is_premium 
  2301.  ); 
  2302.             } else { 
  2303.                 // Set for code type for the first time. 
  2304.                 $this->_storage->prev_is_premium = $this->_plugin->is_premium; 
  2305.             } 
  2306.         } 
  2307.  
  2308.         if ( ! $this->is_addon() ) { 
  2309.             if ( $this->is_registered() ) { 
  2310.                 // Fix for upgrade from versions < 1.0.9. 
  2311.                 if ( ! isset( $this->_storage->activation_timestamp ) ) { 
  2312.                     $this->_storage->activation_timestamp = WP_FS__SCRIPT_START_TIME; 
  2313.                 } 
  2314.  
  2315.                 $this->do_action( 'after_init_plugin_registered' ); 
  2316.             } else if ( $this->is_anonymous() ) { 
  2317.                 $this->do_action( 'after_init_plugin_anonymous' ); 
  2318.             } else if ( $this->is_pending_activation() ) { 
  2319.                 $this->do_action( 'after_init_plugin_pending_activations' ); 
  2320.             } 
  2321.         } else { 
  2322.             if ( $this->is_registered() ) { 
  2323.                 $this->do_action( 'after_init_addon_registered' ); 
  2324.             } else if ( $this->is_anonymous() ) { 
  2325.                 $this->do_action( 'after_init_addon_anonymous' ); 
  2326.             } else if ( $this->is_pending_activation() ) { 
  2327.                 $this->do_action( 'after_init_addon_pending_activations' ); 
  2328.             } 
  2329.         } 
  2330.     } 
  2331.  
  2332.     /** 
  2333.      * @author Leo Fajardo (@leorw) 
  2334.      * 
  2335.      * @since  1.2.1.5 
  2336.      */ 
  2337.     function _stop_tracking_callback() { 
  2338.         $result = $this->stop_tracking(); 
  2339.  
  2340.         if ( true === $result ) { 
  2341.             $this->shoot_ajax_success(); 
  2342.         } 
  2343.  
  2344.         $this->_logger->api_error( $result ); 
  2345.  
  2346.         $this->shoot_ajax_failure( 
  2347.             __fs( 'unexpected-api-error', $this->_slug ) . 
  2348.             ( $this->is_api_error( $result ) && isset( $result->error ) ? 
  2349.                 $result->error->message : 
  2350.                 var_export( $result, true ) ) 
  2351.  ); 
  2352.     } 
  2353.  
  2354.     /** 
  2355.      * @author Leo Fajardo (@leorw) 
  2356.      * @since  1.2.1.5 
  2357.      */ 
  2358.     function _allow_tracking_callback() { 
  2359.         $result = $this->allow_tracking(); 
  2360.  
  2361.         if ( true === $result ) { 
  2362.             $this->shoot_ajax_success(); 
  2363.         } 
  2364.  
  2365.         $this->_logger->api_error( $result ); 
  2366.  
  2367.         $this->shoot_ajax_failure( 
  2368.             __fs( 'unexpected-api-error', $this->_slug ) . 
  2369.             ( $this->is_api_error( $result ) && isset( $result->error ) ? 
  2370.                 $result->error->message : 
  2371.                 var_export( $result, true ) ) 
  2372.  ); 
  2373.     } 
  2374.  
  2375.     /** 
  2376.      * Opt-out from usage tracking. 
  2377.      * 
  2378.      * Note: This will not delete the account information but will stop all tracking. 
  2379.      * 
  2380.      * Returns: 
  2381.      *  1. FALSE  - If the user never opted-in. 
  2382.      *  2. TRUE   - If successfully opted-out. 
  2383.      *  3. object - API result on failure. 
  2384.      * 
  2385.      * @author Leo Fajardo (@leorw) 
  2386.      * @since  1.2.1.5 
  2387.      * 
  2388.      * @return bool|object 
  2389.      */ 
  2390.     function stop_tracking() { 
  2391.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  2392.  
  2393.         if ( ! $this->is_registered() ) { 
  2394.             // User never opted-in. 
  2395.             return false; 
  2396.         } 
  2397.  
  2398.         if ( $this->is_tracking_prohibited() ) { 
  2399.             // Already disconnected. 
  2400.             return true; 
  2401.         } 
  2402.  
  2403.         // Send update to FS. 
  2404.         $result = $this->get_api_site_scope()->call( '/?fields=is_disconnected', 'put', array( 
  2405.             'is_disconnected' => true 
  2406.  ) ); 
  2407.  
  2408.         if ( ! $this->is_api_result_entity( $result ) || 
  2409.              ! isset( $result->is_disconnected ) || 
  2410.              ! $result->is_disconnected 
  2411.  ) { 
  2412.             $this->_logger->api_error( $result ); 
  2413.  
  2414.             return $result; 
  2415.         } 
  2416.  
  2417.         $this->_site->is_disconnected = $result->is_disconnected; 
  2418.         $this->_store_site(); 
  2419.  
  2420.         $this->clear_sync_cron(); 
  2421.  
  2422.         // Successfully disconnected. 
  2423.         return true; 
  2424.     } 
  2425.  
  2426.     /** 
  2427.      * Opt-in back into usage tracking. 
  2428.      * 
  2429.      * Note: This will only work if the user opted-in previously. 
  2430.      * 
  2431.      * Returns: 
  2432.      *  1. FALSE  - If the user never opted-in. 
  2433.      *  2. TRUE   - If successfully opted-in back to usage tracking. 
  2434.      *  3. object - API result on failure. 
  2435.      * 
  2436.      * @author Leo Fajardo (@leorw) 
  2437.      * @since  1.2.1.5 
  2438.      * 
  2439.      * @return bool|object 
  2440.      */ 
  2441.     function allow_tracking() { 
  2442.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  2443.  
  2444.         if ( ! $this->is_registered() ) { 
  2445.             // User never opted-in. 
  2446.             return false; 
  2447.         } 
  2448.  
  2449.         if ( $this->is_tracking_allowed() ) { 
  2450.             // Tracking already allowed. 
  2451.             return true; 
  2452.         } 
  2453.  
  2454.         $result = $this->get_api_site_scope()->call( '/?is_disconnected', 'put', array( 
  2455.             'is_disconnected' => false 
  2456.  ) ); 
  2457.  
  2458.         if ( ! $this->is_api_result_entity( $result ) || 
  2459.              ! isset( $result->is_disconnected ) || 
  2460.              $result->is_disconnected 
  2461.  ) { 
  2462.             $this->_logger->api_error( $result ); 
  2463.  
  2464.             return $result; 
  2465.         } 
  2466.  
  2467.         $this->_site->is_disconnected = $result->is_disconnected; 
  2468.         $this->_store_site(); 
  2469.  
  2470.         $this->schedule_sync_cron(); 
  2471.  
  2472.         // Successfully reconnected. 
  2473.         return true; 
  2474.     } 
  2475.  
  2476.     /** 
  2477.      * If user opted-in and later disabled usage-tracking,  
  2478.      * re-allow tracking for licensing and updates. 
  2479.      * 
  2480.      * @author Leo Fajardo (@leorw) 
  2481.      * 
  2482.      * @since  1.2.1.5 
  2483.      */ 
  2484.     private function reconnect_locally() { 
  2485.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  2486.  
  2487.         if ( $this->is_tracking_prohibited() && 
  2488.              $this->is_registered() 
  2489.  ) { 
  2490.             $this->_site->is_disconnected = false; 
  2491.             $this->_store_site(); 
  2492.         } 
  2493.     } 
  2494.  
  2495.     /** 
  2496.      * Parse plugin's settings (as defined by the plugin dev). 
  2497.      * 
  2498.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  2499.      * @since  1.1.7.3 
  2500.      * 
  2501.      * @param array $plugin_info 
  2502.      * 
  2503.      * @throws \Freemius_Exception 
  2504.      */ 
  2505.     private function parse_settings( &$plugin_info ) { 
  2506.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  2507.  
  2508.         $id = $this->get_numeric_option( $plugin_info, 'id', false ); 
  2509.         $public_key = $this->get_option( $plugin_info, 'public_key', false ); 
  2510.         $secret_key = $this->get_option( $plugin_info, 'secret_key', null ); 
  2511.         $parent_id = $this->get_numeric_option( $plugin_info, 'parent_id', null ); 
  2512.         $parent_name = $this->get_option( $plugin_info, 'parent_name', null ); 
  2513.  
  2514.         /** 
  2515.          * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  2516.          * @since  1.1.9 Try to pull secret key from external config. 
  2517.          */ 
  2518.         if ( is_null( $secret_key ) && defined( "WP_FS__{$this->_slug}_SECRET_KEY" ) ) { 
  2519.             $secret_key = constant( "WP_FS__{$this->_slug}_SECRET_KEY" ); 
  2520.         } 
  2521.  
  2522.         if ( isset( $plugin_info['parent'] ) ) { 
  2523.             $parent_id = $this->get_numeric_option( $plugin_info['parent'], 'id', null ); 
  2524. //                $parent_slug = $this->get_option( $plugin_info['parent'], 'slug', null ); 
  2525. //                $parent_public_key = $this->get_option( $plugin_info['parent'], 'public_key', null ); 
  2526. //                $parent_name = $this->get_option( $plugin_info['parent'], 'name', null ); 
  2527.         } 
  2528.  
  2529.         if ( false === $id ) { 
  2530.             throw new Freemius_Exception( 'Plugin id parameter is not set.' ); 
  2531.         } 
  2532.         if ( false === $public_key ) { 
  2533.             throw new Freemius_Exception( 'Plugin public_key parameter is not set.' ); 
  2534.         } 
  2535.  
  2536.         $plugin = ( $this->_plugin instanceof FS_Plugin ) ? 
  2537.             $this->_plugin : 
  2538.             new FS_Plugin(); 
  2539.  
  2540.         $plugin->update( array( 
  2541.             'id' => $id,  
  2542.             'public_key' => $public_key,  
  2543.             'slug' => $this->_slug,  
  2544.             'parent_plugin_id' => $parent_id,  
  2545.             'version' => $this->get_plugin_version(),  
  2546.             'title' => $this->get_plugin_name(),  
  2547.             'file' => $this->_plugin_basename,  
  2548.             'is_premium' => $this->get_bool_option( $plugin_info, 'is_premium', true ),  
  2549.             'is_live' => $this->get_bool_option( $plugin_info, 'is_live', true ),  
  2550. //                'secret_key' => $secret_key,  
  2551.  ) ); 
  2552.  
  2553.         if ( $plugin->is_updated() ) { 
  2554.             // Update plugin details. 
  2555.             $this->_plugin = FS_Plugin_Manager::instance( $this->_slug )->store( $plugin ); 
  2556.         } 
  2557.         // Set the secret key after storing the plugin, we don't want to store the key in the storage. 
  2558.         $this->_plugin->secret_key = $secret_key; 
  2559.  
  2560.         if ( ! isset( $plugin_info['menu'] ) ) { 
  2561.             // Back compatibility to 1.1.2 
  2562.             $plugin_info['menu'] = array( 
  2563.                 'slug' => isset( $plugin_info['menu_slug'] ) ? 
  2564.                     $plugin_info['menu_slug'] : 
  2565.                     $this->_slug 
  2566.  ); 
  2567.         } 
  2568.  
  2569.         $this->_menu = FS_Admin_Menu_Manager::instance( $this->_slug ); 
  2570.         $this->_menu->init( $plugin_info['menu'], $this->is_addon() ); 
  2571.  
  2572.         $this->_has_addons = $this->get_bool_option( $plugin_info, 'has_addons', false ); 
  2573.         $this->_has_paid_plans = $this->get_bool_option( $plugin_info, 'has_paid_plans', true ); 
  2574.         $this->_is_org_compliant = $this->get_bool_option( $plugin_info, 'is_org_compliant', true ); 
  2575.         $this->_is_premium_only = $this->get_bool_option( $plugin_info, 'is_premium_only', false ); 
  2576.         if ( $this->_is_premium_only ) { 
  2577.             // If premium only plugin, disable anonymous mode. 
  2578.             $this->_enable_anonymous = false; 
  2579.             $this->_anonymous_mode = false; 
  2580.         } else { 
  2581.             $this->_enable_anonymous = $this->get_bool_option( $plugin_info, 'enable_anonymous', true ); 
  2582.             $this->_anonymous_mode = $this->get_bool_option( $plugin_info, 'anonymous_mode', false ); 
  2583.         } 
  2584.         $this->_permissions = $this->get_option( $plugin_info, 'permissions', array() ); 
  2585.  
  2586.         if ( ! empty( $plugin_info['trial'] ) ) { 
  2587.             $this->_trial_days = $this->get_numeric_option( 
  2588.                 $plugin_info['trial'],  
  2589.                 'days',  
  2590.                 // Default to 0 - trial without days specification. 
  2591.                 0 
  2592.  ); 
  2593.  
  2594.             $this->_is_trial_require_payment = $this->get_bool_option( $plugin_info['trial'], 'is_require_payment', false ); 
  2595.         } 
  2596.     } 
  2597.  
  2598.     /** 
  2599.      * @param string[] $options 
  2600.      * @param string   $key 
  2601.      * @param mixed    $default 
  2602.      * 
  2603.      * @return bool 
  2604.      */ 
  2605.     private function get_option( &$options, $key, $default = false ) { 
  2606.         return ! empty( $options[ $key ] ) ? $options[ $key ] : $default; 
  2607.     } 
  2608.  
  2609.     private function get_bool_option( &$options, $key, $default = false ) { 
  2610.         return isset( $options[ $key ] ) && is_bool( $options[ $key ] ) ? $options[ $key ] : $default; 
  2611.     } 
  2612.  
  2613.     private function get_numeric_option( &$options, $key, $default = false ) { 
  2614.         return isset( $options[ $key ] ) && is_numeric( $options[ $key ] ) ? $options[ $key ] : $default; 
  2615.     } 
  2616.  
  2617.     /** 
  2618.      * Gate keeper. 
  2619.      * 
  2620.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  2621.      * @since  1.1.7.3 
  2622.      * 
  2623.      * @return bool 
  2624.      */ 
  2625.     private function should_stop_execution() { 
  2626.         if ( empty( $this->_storage->was_plugin_loaded ) ) { 
  2627.             /** 
  2628.              * Don't execute Freemius until plugin was fully loaded at least once,  
  2629.              * to give the opportunity for the activation hook to run before pinging 
  2630.              * the API for connectivity test. This logic is relevant for the 
  2631.              * identification of new plugin install vs. plugin update. 
  2632.              * 
  2633.              * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  2634.              * @since  1.1.9 
  2635.              */ 
  2636.             return true; 
  2637.         } 
  2638.  
  2639.         if ( $this->is_activation_mode() ) { 
  2640.             if ( ! is_admin() ) { 
  2641.                 /** 
  2642.                  * If in activation mode, don't execute Freemius outside of the 
  2643.                  * admin dashboard. 
  2644.                  * 
  2645.                  * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  2646.                  * @since  1.1.7.3 
  2647.                  */ 
  2648.                 return true; 
  2649.             } 
  2650.  
  2651.             if ( ! WP_FS__IS_HTTP_REQUEST ) { 
  2652.                 /** 
  2653.                  * If in activation and executed without HTTP context (e.g. CLI, Cronjob),  
  2654.                  * then don't start Freemius. 
  2655.                  * 
  2656.                  * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  2657.                  * @since  1.1.6.3 
  2658.                  * 
  2659.                  * @link   https://wordpress.org/support/topic/errors-in-the-freemius-class-when-running-in-wordpress-in-cli 
  2660.                  */ 
  2661.                 return true; 
  2662.             } 
  2663.  
  2664.             if ( $this->is_cron() ) { 
  2665.                 /** 
  2666.                  * If in activation mode, don't execute Freemius during wp crons 
  2667.                  * (wp crons have HTTP context - called as HTTP request). 
  2668.                  * 
  2669.                  * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  2670.                  * @since  1.1.7.3 
  2671.                  */ 
  2672.                 return true; 
  2673.             } 
  2674.  
  2675.             if ( $this->is_ajax() && 
  2676.                  ! $this->_admin_notices->has_sticky( 'failed_connect_api_first' ) && 
  2677.                  ! $this->_admin_notices->has_sticky( 'failed_connect_api' ) 
  2678.  ) { 
  2679.                 /** 
  2680.                  * During activation, if running in AJAX mode, unless there's a sticky 
  2681.                  * connectivity issue notice, don't run Freemius. 
  2682.                  * 
  2683.                  * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  2684.                  * @since  1.1.7.3 
  2685.                  */ 
  2686.                 return true; 
  2687.             } 
  2688.         } 
  2689.  
  2690.         return false; 
  2691.     } 
  2692.  
  2693.     /** 
  2694.      * Triggered after code type has changed. 
  2695.      * 
  2696.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  2697.      * @since  1.1.9.1 
  2698.      */ 
  2699.     function _after_code_type_change() { 
  2700.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  2701.  
  2702.         add_action( is_admin() ? 'admin_init' : 'init', array( 
  2703.             &$this,  
  2704.             '_plugin_code_type_changed' 
  2705.  ) ); 
  2706.     } 
  2707.  
  2708.     /** 
  2709.      * Handles plugin's code type change (free <--> premium). 
  2710.      * 
  2711.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  2712.      * @since  1.0.9 
  2713.      */ 
  2714.     function _plugin_code_type_changed() { 
  2715.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  2716.  
  2717.         if ( $this->is_premium() ) { 
  2718.             $this->reconnect_locally(); 
  2719.  
  2720.             // Activated premium code. 
  2721.             $this->do_action( 'after_premium_version_activation' ); 
  2722.  
  2723.             // Remove all sticky messages related to download of the premium version. 
  2724.             $this->_admin_notices->remove_sticky( array( 
  2725.                 'trial_started',  
  2726.                 'plan_upgraded',  
  2727.                 'plan_changed',  
  2728.                 'license_activated',  
  2729.  ) ); 
  2730.  
  2731.             $this->_admin_notices->add_sticky( 
  2732.                 __fs( 'premium-activated-message', $this->_slug ),  
  2733.                 'premium_activated',  
  2734.                 __fs( 'woot', $this->_slug ) . '!' 
  2735.  ); 
  2736.         } else { 
  2737.             // Remove sticky message related to premium code activation. 
  2738.             $this->_admin_notices->remove_sticky( 'premium_activated' ); 
  2739.  
  2740.             // Activated free code (after had the premium before). 
  2741.             $this->do_action( 'after_free_version_reactivation' ); 
  2742.  
  2743.             if ( $this->is_paying() && ! $this->is_premium() ) { 
  2744.                 $this->_admin_notices->add_sticky( 
  2745.                     sprintf( 
  2746.                         __fs( 'you-have-x-license', $this->_slug ),  
  2747.                         $this->_site->plan->title 
  2748.  ) . $this->get_complete_upgrade_instructions(),  
  2749.                     'plan_upgraded',  
  2750.                     __fs( 'yee-haw', $this->_slug ) . '!' 
  2751.  ); 
  2752.             } 
  2753.         } 
  2754.  
  2755.         // Schedule code type changes event. 
  2756.         $this->schedule_install_sync(); 
  2757.  
  2758.         /** 
  2759.          * Unregister the uninstall hook for the other version of the plugin (with different code type) to avoid 
  2760.          * triggering a fatal error when uninstalling that plugin. For example, after deactivating the "free" version 
  2761.          * of a specific plugin, its uninstall hook should be unregistered after the "premium" version has been 
  2762.          * activated. If we don't do that, a fatal error will occur when we try to uninstall the "free" version since 
  2763.          * the main file of the "free" version will be loaded first before calling the hooked callback. Since the 
  2764.          * free and premium versions are almost identical (same class or have same functions), a fatal error like 
  2765.          * "Cannot redeclare class MyClass" or "Cannot redeclare my_function()" will occur. 
  2766.          */ 
  2767.         $this->unregister_uninstall_hook(); 
  2768.  
  2769.         $this->clear_module_main_file_cache(); 
  2770.  
  2771.         // Update is_premium of latest version. 
  2772.         $this->_storage->prev_is_premium = $this->_plugin->is_premium; 
  2773.     } 
  2774.  
  2775.     #endregion 
  2776.

  2780.  
  2781.     /** 
  2782.      * Check if add-on installed and activated on site. 
  2783.      * 
  2784.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  2785.      * @since  1.0.6 
  2786.      * 
  2787.      * @param string|number $slug_or_id 
  2788.      * 
  2789.      * @return bool 
  2790.      */ 
  2791.     function is_addon_activated( $slug_or_id ) { 
  2792.         return self::has_instance( $slug_or_id ); 
  2793.     } 
  2794.  
  2795.     /** 
  2796.      * Check if add-on was connected to install 
  2797.      * 
  2798.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  2799.      * @since  1.1.7 
  2800.      * 
  2801.      * @param string $slug 
  2802.      * 
  2803.      * @return bool 
  2804.      */ 
  2805.     function is_addon_connected( $slug ) { 
  2806.         $sites = self::get_all_sites(); 
  2807.  
  2808.         if ( ! isset( $sites[ $slug ] ) ) { 
  2809.             return false; 
  2810.         } 
  2811.  
  2812.         $site = $sites[ $slug ]; 
  2813.  
  2814.         $plugin = FS_Plugin_Manager::instance( $slug )->get(); 
  2815.  
  2816.         if ( $plugin->parent_plugin_id != $this->_plugin->id ) { 
  2817.             // The given slug do NOT belong to any of the plugin's add-ons. 
  2818.             return false; 
  2819.         } 
  2820.  
  2821.         return ( is_object( $site ) && 
  2822.                  is_numeric( $site->id ) && 
  2823.                  is_numeric( $site->user_id ) && 
  2824.                  is_object( $site->plan ) 
  2825.  ); 
  2826.     } 
  2827.  
  2828.     /** 
  2829.      * Determines if add-on installed. 
  2830.      * 
  2831.      * NOTE: This is a heuristic and only works if the folder/file named as the slug. 
  2832.      * 
  2833.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  2834.      * @since  1.0.6 
  2835.      * 
  2836.      * @param string $slug 
  2837.      * 
  2838.      * @return bool 
  2839.      */ 
  2840.     function is_addon_installed( $slug ) { 
  2841.         return file_exists( fs_normalize_path( WP_PLUGIN_DIR . '/' . $this->get_addon_basename( $slug ) ) ); 
  2842.     } 
  2843.  
  2844.     /** 
  2845.      * Get add-on basename. 
  2846.      * 
  2847.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  2848.      * @since  1.0.6 
  2849.      * 
  2850.      * @param string $slug 
  2851.      * 
  2852.      * @return string 
  2853.      */ 
  2854.     function get_addon_basename( $slug ) { 
  2855.         if ( $this->is_addon_activated( $slug ) ) { 
  2856.             self::instance( $slug )->get_plugin_basename(); 
  2857.         } 
  2858.  
  2859.         $premium_basename = $slug . '-premium/' . $slug . '.php'; 
  2860.  
  2861.         if ( file_exists( fs_normalize_path( WP_PLUGIN_DIR . '/' . $premium_basename ) ) ) { 
  2862.             return $premium_basename; 
  2863.         } 
  2864.  
  2865.         $free_basename = $slug . '/' . $slug . '.php'; 
  2866.  
  2867.         return $free_basename; 
  2868.     } 
  2869.  
  2870.     /** 
  2871.      * Get installed add-ons instances. 
  2872.      * 
  2873.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  2874.      * @since  1.0.6 
  2875.      * 
  2876.      * @return Freemius[] 
  2877.      */ 
  2878.     function get_installed_addons() { 
  2879.         $installed_addons = array(); 
  2880.         foreach ( self::$_instances as $slug => $instance ) { 
  2881.             if ( $instance->is_addon() && is_object( $instance->_parent_plugin ) ) { 
  2882.                 if ( $this->_plugin->id == $instance->_parent_plugin->id ) { 
  2883.                     $installed_addons[] = $instance; 
  2884.                 } 
  2885.             } 
  2886.         } 
  2887.  
  2888.         return $installed_addons; 
  2889.     } 
  2890.  
  2891.     /** 
  2892.      * Check if any add-ons of the plugin are installed. 
  2893.      * 
  2894.      * @author Leo Fajardo (@leorw) 
  2895.      * @since  1.1.1 
  2896.      * 
  2897.      * @return bool 
  2898.      */ 
  2899.     function has_installed_addons() { 
  2900.         if ( ! $this->has_addons() ) { 
  2901.             return false; 
  2902.         } 
  2903.  
  2904.         foreach ( self::$_instances as $slug => $instance ) { 
  2905.             if ( $instance->is_addon() && is_object( $instance->_parent_plugin ) ) { 
  2906.                 if ( $this->_plugin->id == $instance->_parent_plugin->id ) { 
  2907.                     return true; 
  2908.                 } 
  2909.             } 
  2910.         } 
  2911.  
  2912.         return false; 
  2913.     } 
  2914.  
  2915.     /** 
  2916.      * Tell Freemius that the current plugin is an add-on. 
  2917.      * 
  2918.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  2919.      * @since  1.0.6 
  2920.      * 
  2921.      * @param number $parent_plugin_id The parent plugin ID 
  2922.      */ 
  2923.     function init_addon( $parent_plugin_id ) { 
  2924.         $this->_plugin->parent_plugin_id = $parent_plugin_id; 
  2925.     } 
  2926.  
  2927.     /** 
  2928.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  2929.      * @since  1.0.6 
  2930.      * 
  2931.      * @return bool 
  2932.      */ 
  2933.     function is_addon() { 
  2934.         return isset( $this->_plugin->parent_plugin_id ) && is_numeric( $this->_plugin->parent_plugin_id ); 
  2935.     } 
  2936.  
  2937.     /** 
  2938.      * Deactivate add-on if it's premium only and the user does't have a valid license. 
  2939.      * 
  2940.      * @param bool $is_after_trial_cancel 
  2941.      * 
  2942.      * @return bool If add-on was deactivated. 
  2943.      */ 
  2944.     private function deactivate_premium_only_addon_without_license( $is_after_trial_cancel = false ) { 
  2945.         if ( ! $this->has_free_plan() && 
  2946.              ! $this->has_features_enabled_license() && 
  2947.              ! $this->_has_premium_license() 
  2948.  ) { 
  2949.             // IF wrapper is turned off because activation_timestamp is currently only stored for plugins (not addons). 
  2950. //                if (empty($this->_storage->activation_timestamp) || 
  2951. //                    (WP_FS__SCRIPT_START_TIME - $this->_storage->activation_timestamp) > 30 
  2952. // ) { 
  2953.             /** 
  2954.              * @todo When it's first fail, there's no reason to try and re-sync because the licenses were just synced after initial activation. 
  2955.              * 
  2956.              * Retry syncing the user add-on licenses. 
  2957.              */ 
  2958.             // Sync licenses. 
  2959.             $this->_sync_licenses(); 
  2960. //                } 
  2961.  
  2962.             // Try to activate premium license. 
  2963.             $this->_activate_license( true ); 
  2964.  
  2965.             if ( ! $this->has_free_plan() && 
  2966.                  ! $this->has_features_enabled_license() && 
  2967.                  ! $this->_has_premium_license() 
  2968.  ) { 
  2969.                 // @todo Check if deactivate plugins also call the deactivation hook. 
  2970.  
  2971.                 deactivate_plugins( array( $this->_plugin_basename ), true ); 
  2972.  
  2973.                 $this->_parent->_admin_notices->add_sticky( 
  2974.                     sprintf( 
  2975.                         __fs( ( $is_after_trial_cancel ? 
  2976.                             'addon-trial-cancelled-message' : 
  2977.                             'addon-no-license-message' ),  
  2978.                             $this->_parent->_slug 
  2979.  ),  
  2980.                         '<b>' . $this->_plugin->title . '</b>' 
  2981.  ) . ' ' . sprintf( 
  2982.                         '<a href="%s" aria-label="%s" class="button button-primary" style="margin-left: 10px; vertical-align: middle;">%s  ➜</a>',  
  2983.                         $this->_parent->addon_url( $this->_slug ),  
  2984.                         esc_attr( sprintf( __fs( 'more-information-about-x', $this->_parent->_slug ), $this->_plugin->title ) ),  
  2985.                         __fs( 'purchase-license', $this->_parent->_slug ) 
  2986.  ),  
  2987.                     'no_addon_license_' . $this->_slug,  
  2988.                     ( $is_after_trial_cancel ? '' : __fs( 'oops', $this->_parent->_slug ) . '...' ),  
  2989.                     ( $is_after_trial_cancel ? 'success' : 'error' ) 
  2990.  ); 
  2991.  
  2992.                 return true; 
  2993.             } 
  2994.         } 
  2995.  
  2996.         return false; 
  2997.     } 
  2998.

  3020.     /**

  3034.     /**

  3039.      *

  3044.     } 
  3045.  
  3046.     /** 
  3047.      * Check if the user skipped connecting the account with Freemius. 
  3048.      * 
  3049.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  3050.      * @since  1.0.7 
  3051.      * 
  3052.      * @return bool 
  3053.      */ 
  3054.     function is_anonymous() { 
  3055.         if ( ! isset( $this->_is_anonymous ) ) { 
  3056.             if ( ! isset( $this->_storage->is_anonymous ) ) { 
  3057.                 // Not skipped. 
  3058.                 $this->_is_anonymous = false; 
  3059.             } else if ( is_bool( $this->_storage->is_anonymous ) ) { 
  3060.                 // For back compatibility, since the variable was boolean before. 
  3061.                 $this->_is_anonymous = $this->_storage->is_anonymous; 
  3062.  
  3063.                 // Upgrade stored data format to 1.1.3 format. 
  3064.                 $this->set_anonymous_mode( $this->_storage->is_anonymous ); 
  3065.             } else { 
  3066.                 // Version 1.1.3 and later. 
  3067.                 $this->_is_anonymous = $this->_storage->is_anonymous['is']; 
  3068.             } 
  3069.         } 
  3070.  
  3071.         return $this->_is_anonymous; 
  3072.     } 
  3073.  
  3074.     /** 
  3075.      * Check if user connected his account and install pending email activation.

  3079.      *

  3082.     function is_pending_activation() { 
  3083.         return $this->_storage->get( 'is_pending_activation', false ); 
  3084.     }

  3096.  
  3097.     #---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- 
  3098.     #region Daily Sync Cron 
  3099.     #---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- 
  3100.  
  3101.     /** 
  3102.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  3103.      * @since  1.1.7.3 
  3104.      */ 
  3105.     private function run_manual_sync() { 
  3106.         $this->require_pluggable_essentials(); 
  3107.  
  3108.         if ( ! current_user_can( 'activate_plugins' ) ) { 
  3109.             return; 
  3110.         } 
  3111.  
  3112.         // Run manual sync. 
  3113.         $this->_sync_cron(); 
  3114.  
  3115.         // Reschedule next cron to run 24 hours from now (performance optimization). 
  3116.         $this->clear_sync_cron(); 
  3117.  
  3118.         $this->schedule_sync_cron( time() + WP_FS__TIME_24_HOURS_IN_SEC, false ); 
  3119.     } 
  3120.  
  3121.     /** 
  3122.      * Data sync cron job. Replaces the background sync non blocking HTTP request 
  3123.      * that doesn't halt page loading. 
  3124.      * 
  3125.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  3126.      * @since  1.1.7.3 
  3127.      */ 
  3128.     function _sync_cron() { 
  3129.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  3130.  
  3131.         // Store the last time data sync was executed. 
  3132.         $this->_storage->sync_timestamp = time(); 
  3133.  
  3134.         // Check if API is temporary down. 
  3135.         if ( FS_Api::is_temporary_down() ) { 
  3136.             return; 
  3137.         } 
  3138.  
  3139.         // @todo Add logic that identifies API latency, and reschedule the next background sync randomly between 8-16 hours. 
  3140.  
  3141.         if ( $this->is_registered() ) { 
  3142.             if ( $this->has_paid_plan() ) { 
  3143.                 // Initiate background plan sync. 
  3144.                 $this->_sync_license( true ); 
  3145.  
  3146.                 if ( $this->is_paying() ) { 
  3147.                     // Check for premium plugin updates. 
  3148.                     $this->_check_updates( true ); 
  3149.                 } 
  3150.             } else { 
  3151.                 // Sync install (only if something changed locally). 
  3152.                 $this->sync_install(); 
  3153.             } 
  3154.         } 
  3155.  
  3156.         $this->do_action( 'after_sync_cron' ); 
  3157.     } 
  3158.  
  3159.     /** 
  3160.      * Check if sync was executed in the last $period of seconds. 
  3161.      * 
  3162.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  3163.      * @since  1.1.7.3 
  3164.      * 
  3165.      * @param int $period In seconds 
  3166.      * 
  3167.      * @return bool 
  3168.      */ 
  3169.     private function is_sync_executed( $period = WP_FS__TIME_24_HOURS_IN_SEC ) { 
  3170.         if ( ! isset( $this->_storage->sync_timestamp ) ) { 
  3171.             return false; 
  3172.         } 
  3173.  
  3174.         return ( $this->_storage->sync_timestamp > ( WP_FS__SCRIPT_START_TIME - $period ) ); 
  3175.     } 
  3176.  
  3177.     /** 
  3178.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  3179.      * @since  1.1.7.3 
  3180.      * 
  3181.      * @return bool 
  3182.      */ 
  3183.     private function is_sync_cron_on() { 
  3184.         /** 
  3185.          * @var object $sync_cron_data 
  3186.          */ 
  3187.         $sync_cron_data = $this->_storage->get( 'sync_cron', null ); 
  3188.  
  3189.         return ( ! is_null( $sync_cron_data ) && true === $sync_cron_data->on ); 
  3190.     } 
  3191.  
  3192.     /** 
  3193.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  3194.      * @since  1.1.7.3 
  3195.      * 
  3196.      * @param int  $start_at        Defaults to now. 
  3197.      * @param bool $randomize_start If true, schedule first job randomly during the next 12 hours. Otherwise,  
  3198.      *                              schedule job to start right away. 
  3199.      */ 
  3200.     private function schedule_sync_cron( $start_at = WP_FS__SCRIPT_START_TIME, $randomize_start = true ) { 
  3201.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  3202.  
  3203.         if ( $randomize_start ) { 
  3204.             // Schedule first sync with a random 12 hour time range from now. 
  3205.             $start_at += rand( 0, ( WP_FS__TIME_24_HOURS_IN_SEC / 2 ) ); 
  3206.         } 
  3207.  
  3208.         // Schedule daily WP cron. 
  3209.         wp_schedule_event( 
  3210.             $start_at,  
  3211.             'daily',  
  3212.             $this->get_action_tag( 'data_sync' ) 
  3213.  ); 
  3214.  
  3215.         $this->_storage->store( 'sync_cron', (object) array( 
  3216.             'version' => $this->get_plugin_version(),  
  3217.             'sdk_version' => $this->version,  
  3218.             'timestamp' => WP_FS__SCRIPT_START_TIME,  
  3219.             'on' => true,  
  3220.  ) ); 
  3221.     } 
  3222.  
  3223.     /** 
  3224.      * Add the actual sync function to the cron job hook. 
  3225.      * 
  3226.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  3227.      * @since  1.1.7.3 
  3228.      */ 
  3229.     private function hook_callback_to_sync_cron() { 
  3230.         $this->add_action( 'data_sync', array( &$this, '_sync_cron' ) ); 
  3231.     } 
  3232.  
  3233.     /** 
  3234.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  3235.      * @since  1.1.7.3 
  3236.      */ 
  3237.     private function clear_sync_cron() { 
  3238.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  3239.  
  3240.         if ( ! $this->is_sync_cron_on() ) { 
  3241.             return; 
  3242.         } 
  3243.  
  3244.         $this->_storage->remove( 'sync_cron' ); 
  3245.  
  3246.         wp_clear_scheduled_hook( $this->get_action_tag( 'data_sync' ) ); 
  3247.     } 
  3248.  
  3249.     /** 
  3250.      * Unix timestamp for next sync cron execution or false if not scheduled. 
  3251.      * 
  3252.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  3253.      * @since  1.1.7.3 
  3254.      * 
  3255.      * @return int|false 
  3256.      */ 
  3257.     function next_sync_cron() { 
  3258.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  3259.  
  3260.         if ( ! $this->is_sync_cron_on() ) { 
  3261.             return false; 
  3262.         } 
  3263.  
  3264.         return wp_next_scheduled( $this->get_action_tag( 'data_sync' ) ); 
  3265.     } 
  3266.  
  3267.     /** 
  3268.      * Unix timestamp for previous sync cron execution or false if never executed. 
  3269.      * 
  3270.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  3271.      * @since  1.1.7.3 
  3272.      * 
  3273.      * @return int|false 
  3274.      */ 
  3275.     function last_sync_cron() { 
  3276.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  3277.  
  3278.         return $this->_storage->get( 'sync_timestamp' ); 
  3279.     } 
  3280.  
  3281.     #endregion Daily Sync Cron ------------------------------------------------------------------ 
  3282.  
  3283.     #---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- 
  3284.     #region Async Install Sync 
  3285.     #---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- 
  3286.  
  3287.     /** 
  3288.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  3289.      * @since  1.1.7.3 
  3290.      * 
  3291.      * @return bool 
  3292.      */ 
  3293.     private function is_install_sync_scheduled() { 
  3294.         /** 
  3295.          * @var object $cron_data 
  3296.          */ 
  3297.         $cron_data = $this->_storage->get( 'install_sync_cron', null ); 
  3298.  
  3299.         return ( ! is_null( $cron_data ) && true === $cron_data->on ); 
  3300.     } 
  3301.  
  3302.     /** 
  3303.      * Instead of running blocking install sync event, execute non blocking scheduled wp-cron. 
  3304.      * 
  3305.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  3306.      * @since  1.1.7.3 
  3307.      */ 
  3308.     private function schedule_install_sync() { 
  3309.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  3310.  
  3311.         $this->clear_install_sync_cron(); 
  3312.  
  3313.         // Schedule immediate install sync. 
  3314.         wp_schedule_single_event( 
  3315.             WP_FS__SCRIPT_START_TIME,  
  3316.             $this->get_action_tag( 'install_sync' ) 
  3317.  ); 
  3318.  
  3319.         $this->_storage->store( 'install_sync_cron', (object) array( 
  3320.             'version' => $this->get_plugin_version(),  
  3321.             'sdk_version' => $this->version,  
  3322.             'timestamp' => WP_FS__SCRIPT_START_TIME,  
  3323.             'on' => true,  
  3324.  ) ); 
  3325.     } 
  3326.  
  3327.     /** 
  3328.      * Unix timestamp for previous install sync cron execution or false if never executed. 
  3329.      * 
  3330.      * @todo   There's some very strange bug that $this->_storage->install_sync_timestamp value is not being 
  3331.      *         updated. But for sure the sync event is working. 
  3332.      * 
  3333.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  3334.      * @since  1.1.7.3 
  3335.      * 
  3336.      * @return int|false 
  3337.      */ 
  3338.     function last_install_sync() { 
  3339.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  3340.  
  3341.         return $this->_storage->get( 'install_sync_timestamp' ); 
  3342.     } 
  3343.  
  3344.     /** 
  3345.      * Unix timestamp for next install sync cron execution or false if not scheduled. 
  3346.      * 
  3347.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  3348.      * @since  1.1.7.3 
  3349.      * 
  3350.      * @return int|false 
  3351.      */ 
  3352.     function next_install_sync() { 
  3353.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  3354.  
  3355.         if ( ! $this->is_install_sync_scheduled() ) { 
  3356.             return false; 
  3357.         } 
  3358.  
  3359.         return wp_next_scheduled( $this->get_action_tag( 'install_sync' ) ); 
  3360.     } 
  3361.  
  3362.     /** 
  3363.      * Add the actual install sync function to the cron job hook. 
  3364.      * 
  3365.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  3366.      * @since  1.1.7.3 
  3367.      */ 
  3368.     private function hook_callback_to_install_sync() { 
  3369.         $this->add_action( 'install_sync', array( &$this, '_run_sync_install' ) ); 
  3370.     } 
  3371.  
  3372.     /** 
  3373.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  3374.      * @since  1.1.7.3 
  3375.      */ 
  3376.     private function clear_install_sync_cron() { 
  3377.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  3378.  
  3379.         if ( ! $this->is_install_sync_scheduled() ) { 
  3380.             return; 
  3381.         } 
  3382.  
  3383.         $this->_storage->remove( 'install_sync_cron' ); 
  3384.  
  3385.         wp_clear_scheduled_hook( $this->get_action_tag( 'install_sync' ) ); 
  3386.     } 
  3387.  
  3388.     /** 
  3389.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  3390.      * @since  1.1.7.3 
  3391.      */ 
  3392.     public function _run_sync_install() { 
  3393.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  3394.  
  3395.         // Update last install sync timestamp. 
  3396.         $this->_storage->install_sync_timestamp = time(); 
  3397.  
  3398.         $this->sync_install( array(), true ); 
  3399.     }

  3593.     /** 
  3594.      * Return current page's URL. 
  3595.      * 
  3596.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  3597.      * @since  1.0.7 
  3598.      * 
  3599.      * @return string 
  3600.      */ 
  3601.     function current_page_url() { 
  3602.         $url = 'http'; 
  3603.  
  3604.         if ( isset( $_SERVER["HTTPS"] ) ) { 
  3605.             if ( $_SERVER["HTTPS"] == "on" ) { 
  3606.                 $url .= "s"; 
  3607.             } 
  3608.         } 
  3609.         $url .= "://"; 
  3610.         if ( $_SERVER["SERVER_PORT"] != "80" ) { 
  3611.             $url .= $_SERVER["SERVER_NAME"] . ":" . $_SERVER["SERVER_PORT"] . $_SERVER["REQUEST_URI"]; 
  3612.         } else { 
  3613.             $url .= $_SERVER["SERVER_NAME"] . $_SERVER["REQUEST_URI"]; 
  3614.         } 
  3615.  
  3616.         return esc_url( $url ); 
  3617.     } 
  3618.

  3650.     }

  3692.  
  3693.     /** 
  3694.      * Check if Freemius was added on new plugin installation. 
  3695.      * 
  3696.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  3697.      * @since  1.1.5 
  3698.      * 
  3699.      * @return bool 
  3700.      */ 
  3701.     function is_plugin_new_install() { 
  3702.         return isset( $this->_storage->is_plugin_new_install ) && 
  3703.                $this->_storage->is_plugin_new_install; 
  3704.     } 
  3705.  
  3706.     /** 
  3707.      * Check if it's the first plugin release that is running Freemius. 
  3708.      * 
  3709.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  3710.      * @since  1.2.1.5 
  3711.      * 
  3712.      * @return bool 
  3713.      */ 
  3714.     function is_first_freemius_powered_version() { 
  3715.         return empty( $this->_storage->plugin_last_version ); 
  3716.     } 
  3717.  
  3718.     /** 
  3719.      * Plugin activated hook. 
  3720.      * 
  3721.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  3722.      * @since  1.0.1 
  3723.      * 
  3724.      * @uses   FS_Api 
  3725.      */ 
  3726.     function _activate_plugin_event_hook() { 
  3727.         $this->_logger->entrance( 'slug = ' . $this->_slug ); 
  3728.  
  3729.         if ( ! current_user_can( 'activate_plugins' ) ) { 
  3730.             return; 
  3731.         } 
  3732.  
  3733.         $this->unregister_uninstall_hook(); 
  3734.  
  3735.         // Clear API cache on activation. 
  3736.         FS_Api::clear_cache(); 
  3737.  
  3738.         if ( $this->is_registered() ) { 
  3739.             $this->reconnect_locally(); 
  3740.  
  3741.             // Schedule re-activation event and sync. 
  3742. //                $this->sync_install( array(), true ); 
  3743.             $this->schedule_install_sync(); 
  3744.  
  3745.             $is_premium_version_activation = ( current_filter() !== ( 'activate_' . $this->_free_plugin_basename ) ); 
  3746.  
  3747.             // 1. If running in the activation of the FREE module, get the basename of the PREMIUM. 
  3748.             // 2. If running in the activation of the PREMIUM module, get the basename of the FREE. 
  3749.             $other_version_basename = $is_premium_version_activation ? 
  3750.                 $this->_free_plugin_basename : 
  3751.                 $this->premium_plugin_basename(); 
  3752.  
  3753.             /** 
  3754.              * If the other module version is activate, deactivate it. 
  3755.              * 
  3756.              * @author Leo Fajardo (@leorw) 
  3757.              * @since  1.2.2 
  3758.              */ 
  3759.             if ( is_plugin_active( $other_version_basename ) ) { 
  3760.                 deactivate_plugins( $other_version_basename ); 
  3761.             } 
  3762.  
  3763.             // If activating the premium module version, add an admin noitce to congratulate for an upgrade completion. 
  3764.             if ( $is_premium_version_activation ) { 
  3765.                 $this->_admin_notices->add( 
  3766.                     sprintf( __fs( 'successful-version-upgrade-message', $this->_slug ), sprintf( '<b>%s</b>', $this->_plugin->title ) ),  
  3767.                     __fs( 'woot', $this->_slug ) . '!' 
  3768.  ); 
  3769.             } 
  3770.         } else if ( $this->is_anonymous() ) { 
  3771.             /** 
  3772.              * Reset "skipped" click cache on the following: 
  3773.              *  1. Development mode. 
  3774.              *  2. If the user skipped the exact same version before. 
  3775.              * 
  3776.              * @todo 3. If explicitly asked to retry after every activation. 
  3777.              */ 
  3778.             if ( WP_FS__DEV_MODE || 
  3779.                  $this->get_plugin_version() == $this->_storage->is_anonymous['version'] 
  3780.  ) { 
  3781.                 $this->reset_anonymous_mode(); 
  3782.             } 
  3783.         } 
  3784.  
  3785.         if ( ! isset( $this->_storage->is_plugin_new_install ) ) { 
  3786.             /** 
  3787.              * If no previous version of plugin's version exist, it means that it's either 
  3788.              * the first time that the plugin installed on the site, or the plugin was installed 
  3789.              * before but didn't have Freemius integrated. 
  3790.              * 
  3791.              * Since register_activation_hook() do NOT fires on updates since 3.1, and only fires 
  3792.              * on manual activation via the dashboard, is_plugin_activation() is TRUE 
  3793.              * only after immediate activation. 
  3794.              * 
  3795.              * @since 1.1.4 
  3796.              * @link  https://make.wordpress.org/core/2010/10/27/plugin-activation-hooks-no-longer-fire-for-updates/ 
  3797.              */ 
  3798.             $this->_storage->is_plugin_new_install = empty( $this->_storage->plugin_last_version ); 
  3799.         } 
  3800.  
  3801.         if ( ! $this->_anonymous_mode && $this->has_api_connectivity( WP_FS__DEV_MODE ) ) { 
  3802.             // Store hint that the plugin was just activated to enable auto-redirection to settings. 
  3803.             add_option( "fs_{$this->_slug}_activated", true ); 
  3804.         } 
  3805.  
  3806.         /** 
  3807.          * Activation hook is executed after the plugin's main file is loaded, therefore,  
  3808.          * after the plugin was loaded. The logic is located at activate_plugin() 
  3809.          * ./wp-admin/includes/plugin.php. 
  3810.          * 
  3811.          * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  3812.          * @since  1.1.9 
  3813.          */ 
  3814.         $this->_storage->was_plugin_loaded = true; 
  3815.     } 
  3816.  
  3817.     /** 
  3818.      * Delete account. 
  3819.      * 
  3820.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  3821.      * @since  1.0.3 
  3822.      * 
  3823.      * @param bool $check_user Enforce checking if user have plugins activation privileges. 
  3824.      */ 
  3825.     function delete_account_event( $check_user = true ) { 
  3826.         $this->_logger->entrance( 'slug = ' . $this->_slug ); 
  3827.  
  3828.         if ( $check_user && ! current_user_can( 'activate_plugins' ) ) { 
  3829.             return; 
  3830.         } 
  3831.  
  3832.         $this->do_action( 'before_account_delete' ); 
  3833.  
  3834.         // Clear all admin notices. 
  3835.         $this->_admin_notices->clear_all_sticky(); 
  3836.  
  3837.         $this->_delete_site( false ); 
  3838.  
  3839.         $this->_delete_plans( false ); 
  3840.  
  3841.         $this->_delete_licenses( false ); 
  3842.  
  3843.         // Delete add-ons related to plugin's account. 
  3844.         $this->_delete_account_addons( false ); 
  3845.  
  3846.         // @todo Delete plans and licenses of add-ons. 
  3847.  
  3848.         self::$_accounts->store(); 
  3849.  
  3850.         /** 
  3851.          * IMPORTANT: 
  3852.          *  Clear crons must be executed before clearing all storage. 
  3853.          *  Otherwise, the cron will not be cleared. 
  3854.          */ 
  3855.         $this->clear_sync_cron(); 
  3856.         $this->clear_install_sync_cron(); 
  3857.  
  3858.         // Clear all storage data. 
  3859.         $this->_storage->clear_all( true, array( 
  3860.             'connectivity_test',  
  3861.             'is_on',  
  3862.  ) ); 
  3863.  
  3864.         // Send delete event. 
  3865.         $this->get_api_site_scope()->call( '/', 'delete' ); 
  3866.  
  3867.         $this->do_action( 'after_account_delete' ); 
  3868.     } 
  3869.  
  3870.     /** 
  3871.      * Plugin deactivation hook. 
  3872.      * 
  3873.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  3874.      * @since  1.0.1 
  3875.      */ 
  3876.     function _deactivate_plugin_hook() { 
  3877.         $this->_logger->entrance( 'slug = ' . $this->_slug ); 
  3878.  
  3879.         if ( ! current_user_can( 'activate_plugins' ) ) { 
  3880.             return; 
  3881.         } 
  3882.  
  3883.         $this->_admin_notices->clear_all_sticky(); 
  3884.         if ( isset( $this->_storage->sticky_optin_added ) ) { 
  3885.             unset( $this->_storage->sticky_optin_added ); 
  3886.         } 
  3887.  
  3888.         if ( ! isset( $this->_storage->is_plugin_new_install ) ) { 
  3889.             // Remember that plugin was already installed. 
  3890.             $this->_storage->is_plugin_new_install = false; 
  3891.         } 
  3892.  
  3893.         // Hook to plugin uninstall. 
  3894.         register_uninstall_hook( $this->_plugin_main_file_path, array( 'Freemius', '_uninstall_plugin_hook' ) ); 
  3895.  
  3896.         $this->clear_module_main_file_cache(); 
  3897.         $this->clear_sync_cron(); 
  3898.         $this->clear_install_sync_cron(); 
  3899.  
  3900.         if ( $this->is_registered() ) { 
  3901.             // Send deactivation event. 
  3902.             $this->sync_install( array( 
  3903.                 'is_active' => false,  
  3904.  ) ); 
  3905.         } else { 
  3906.             if ( ! $this->has_api_connectivity() ) { 
  3907.                 // Reset connectivity test cache. 
  3908.                 unset( $this->_storage->connectivity_test ); 
  3909.             } 
  3910.         } 
  3911.  
  3912.         // Clear API cache on deactivation. 
  3913.         FS_Api::clear_cache(); 
  3914.  
  3915.         $this->remove_sdk_reference(); 
  3916.     } 
  3917.  
  3918.     /** 
  3919.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  3920.      * @since  1.1.6 
  3921.      */ 
  3922.     private function remove_sdk_reference() { 
  3923.         global $fs_active_plugins; 
  3924.  
  3925.         foreach ( $fs_active_plugins->plugins as $sdk_path => &$data ) { 
  3926.             if ( $this->_plugin_basename == $data->plugin_path ) { 
  3927.                 unset( $fs_active_plugins->plugins[ $sdk_path ] ); 
  3928.                 break; 
  3929.             } 
  3930.         } 
  3931.  
  3932.         fs_fallback_to_newest_active_sdk(); 
  3933.     }

  3948.  ); 
  3949.

  3952.     }

  3990.

  4000.      *

  4004.     private function update_plugin_version_event() { 
  4005.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  4006.  
  4007.         if ( ! $this->is_registered() ) { 
  4008.             return; 
  4009.         } 
  4010.

  4012. //            $this->sync_install( array(), true );
