  4015.     /** 
  4016.      * Return a list of modified plugins since the last sync. 
  4017.      * 
  4018.      * Note: 
  4019.      *  There's no point to store a plugins counter since even if the number of 
  4020.      *  plugins didn't change, we still need to check if the versions are all the 
  4021.      *  same and the activity state is similar. 
  4022.      * 
  4023.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  4024.      * @since  1.1.8 
  4025.      * 
  4026.      * @return array|false 
  4027.      */ 
  4028.     private function get_plugins_data_for_api() { 
  4029.         // Alias. 
  4030.         $option_name = 'all_plugins'; 
  4031.  
  4032.         $all_cached_plugins = self::$_accounts->get_option( $option_name ); 
  4033.  
  4034.         if ( ! is_object( $all_cached_plugins ) ) { 
  4035.             $all_cached_plugins = (object) array( 
  4036.                 'timestamp' => '',  
  4037.                 'md5' => '',  
  4038.                 'plugins' => array(),  
  4039.  ); 
  4040.         } 
  4041.  
  4042.         $time = time(); 
  4043.  
  4044.         if ( ! empty( $all_cached_plugins->timestamp ) && 
  4045.              ( $time - $all_cached_plugins->timestamp ) < WP_FS__TIME_5_MIN_IN_SEC 
  4046.  ) { 
  4047.             // Don't send plugin updates if last update was in the past 5 min. 
  4048.             return false; 
  4049.         } 
  4050.  
  4051.         // Write timestamp to lock the logic. 
  4052.         $all_cached_plugins->timestamp = $time; 
  4053.         self::$_accounts->set_option( $option_name, $all_cached_plugins, true ); 
  4054.  
  4055.         // Reload options from DB. 
  4056.         self::$_accounts->load( true ); 
  4057.         $all_cached_plugins = self::$_accounts->get_option( $option_name ); 
  4058.  
  4059.         if ( $time != $all_cached_plugins->timestamp ) { 
  4060.             // If timestamp is different, then another thread captured the lock. 
  4061.             return false; 
  4062.         } 
  4063.  
  4064.         // Check if there's a change in plugins. 
  4065.         $all_plugins = self::get_all_plugins(); 
  4066.  
  4067.         // Check if plugins changed. 
  4068.         ksort( $all_plugins ); 
  4069.  
  4070.         $plugins_signature = ''; 
  4071.         foreach ( $all_plugins as $basename => $data ) { 
  4072.             $plugins_signature .= $data['slug'] . ', ' . 
  4073.                                   $data['Version'] . ', ' . 
  4074.                                   ( $data['is_active'] ? '1' : '0' ) . ';'; 
  4075.         } 
  4076.  
  4077.         // Check if plugins status changed (version or active/inactive). 
  4078.         $plugins_changed = ( $all_cached_plugins->md5 !== md5( $plugins_signature ) ); 
  4079.  
  4080.         $plugins_update_data = array(); 
  4081.  
  4082.         if ( $plugins_changed ) { 
  4083.             // Change in plugins, report changes. 
  4084.  
  4085.             // Update existing plugins info. 
  4086.             foreach ( $all_cached_plugins->plugins as $basename => $data ) { 
  4087.                 if ( ! isset( $all_plugins[ $basename ] ) ) { 
  4088.                     // Plugin uninstalled. 
  4089.                     $uninstalled_plugin_data = $data; 
  4090.                     $uninstalled_plugin_data['is_active'] = false; 
  4091.                     $uninstalled_plugin_data['is_uninstalled'] = true; 
  4092.                     $plugins_update_data[] = $uninstalled_plugin_data; 
  4093.  
  4094.                     unset( $all_plugins[ $basename ] ); 
  4095.                     unset( $all_cached_plugins->plugins[ $basename ] ); 
  4096.                 } else if ( $data['is_active'] !== $all_plugins[ $basename ]['is_active'] || 
  4097.                             $data['version'] !== $all_plugins[ $basename ]['Version'] 
  4098.  ) { 
  4099.                     // Plugin activated or deactivated, or version changed. 
  4100.                     $all_cached_plugins->plugins[ $basename ]['is_active'] = $all_plugins[ $basename ]['is_active']; 
  4101.                     $all_cached_plugins->plugins[ $basename ]['version'] = $all_plugins[ $basename ]['Version']; 
  4102.  
  4103.                     $plugins_update_data[] = $all_cached_plugins->plugins[ $basename ]; 
  4104.                 } 
  4105.             } 
  4106.  
  4107.             // Find new plugins that weren't yet seen before. 
  4108.             foreach ( $all_plugins as $basename => $data ) { 
  4109.                 if ( ! isset( $all_cached_plugins->plugins[ $basename ] ) ) { 
  4110.                     // New plugin. 
  4111.                     $new_plugin = array( 
  4112.                         'slug' => $data['slug'],  
  4113.                         'version' => $data['Version'],  
  4114.                         'title' => $data['Name'],  
  4115.                         'is_active' => $data['is_active'],  
  4116.                         'is_uninstalled' => false,  
  4117.  ); 
  4118.  
  4119.                     $plugins_update_data[] = $new_plugin; 
  4120.                     $all_cached_plugins->plugins[ $basename ] = $new_plugin; 
  4121.                 } 
  4122.             } 
  4123.  
  4124.             $all_cached_plugins->md5 = md5( $plugins_signature ); 
  4125.             $all_cached_plugins->timestamp = $time; 
  4126.             self::$_accounts->set_option( $option_name, $all_cached_plugins, true ); 
  4127.         } 
  4128.  
  4129.         return $plugins_update_data; 
  4130.     } 
  4131.  
  4132.     /** 
  4133.      * Return a list of modified themes since the last sync. 
  4134.      * 
  4135.      * Note: 
  4136.      *  There's no point to store a themes counter since even if the number of 
  4137.      *  themes didn't change, we still need to check if the versions are all the 
  4138.      *  same and the activity state is similar. 
  4139.      * 
  4140.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  4141.      * @since  1.1.8 
  4142.      * 
  4143.      * @return array|false 
  4144.      */ 
  4145.     private function get_themes_data_for_api() { 
  4146.         // Alias. 
  4147.         $option_name = 'all_themes'; 
  4148.  
  4149.         $all_cached_themes = self::$_accounts->get_option( $option_name ); 
  4150.  
  4151.         if ( ! is_object( $all_cached_themes ) ) { 
  4152.             $all_cached_themes = (object) array( 
  4153.                 'timestamp' => '',  
  4154.                 'md5' => '',  
  4155.                 'themes' => array(),  
  4156.  ); 
  4157.         } 
  4158.  
  4159.         $time = time(); 
  4160.  
  4161.         if ( ! empty( $all_cached_themes->timestamp ) && 
  4162.              ( $time - $all_cached_themes->timestamp ) < WP_FS__TIME_5_MIN_IN_SEC 
  4163.  ) { 
  4164.             // Don't send theme updates if last update was in the past 5 min. 
  4165.             return false; 
  4166.         } 
  4167.  
  4168.         // Write timestamp to lock the logic. 
  4169.         $all_cached_themes->timestamp = $time; 
  4170.         self::$_accounts->set_option( $option_name, $all_cached_themes, true ); 
  4171.  
  4172.         // Reload options from DB. 
  4173.         self::$_accounts->load( true ); 
  4174.         $all_cached_themes = self::$_accounts->get_option( $option_name ); 
  4175.  
  4176.         if ( $time != $all_cached_themes->timestamp ) { 
  4177.             // If timestamp is different, then another thread captured the lock. 
  4178.             return false; 
  4179.         } 
  4180.  
  4181.         // Get active theme. 
  4182.         $active_theme = wp_get_theme(); 
  4183.         $active_theme_stylesheet = $active_theme->get_stylesheet(); 
  4184.  
  4185.         // Check if there's a change in themes. 
  4186.         $all_themes = wp_get_themes(); 
  4187.  
  4188.         // Check if themes changed. 
  4189.         ksort( $all_themes ); 
  4190.  
  4191.         $themes_signature = ''; 
  4192.         foreach ( $all_themes as $slug => $data ) { 
  4193.             $is_active = ( $slug === $active_theme_stylesheet ); 
  4194.             $themes_signature .= $slug . ', ' . 
  4195.                                  $data->version . ', ' . 
  4196.                                  ( $is_active ? '1' : '0' ) . ';'; 
  4197.         } 
  4198.  
  4199.         // Check if themes status changed (version or active/inactive). 
  4200.         $themes_changed = ( $all_cached_themes->md5 !== md5( $themes_signature ) ); 
  4201.  
  4202.         $themes_update_data = array(); 
  4203.  
  4204.         if ( $themes_changed ) { 
  4205.             // Change in themes, report changes. 
  4206.  
  4207.             // Update existing themes info. 
  4208.             foreach ( $all_cached_themes->themes as $slug => $data ) { 
  4209.                 $is_active = ( $slug === $active_theme_stylesheet ); 
  4210.  
  4211.                 if ( ! isset( $all_themes[ $slug ] ) ) { 
  4212.                     // Plugin uninstalled. 
  4213.                     $uninstalled_theme_data = $data; 
  4214.                     $uninstalled_theme_data['is_active'] = false; 
  4215.                     $uninstalled_theme_data['is_uninstalled'] = true; 
  4216.                     $themes_update_data[] = $uninstalled_theme_data; 
  4217.  
  4218.                     unset( $all_themes[ $slug ] ); 
  4219.                     unset( $all_cached_themes->themes[ $slug ] ); 
  4220.                 } else if ( $data['is_active'] !== $is_active || 
  4221.                             $data['version'] !== $all_themes[ $slug ]->version 
  4222.  ) { 
  4223.                     // Plugin activated or deactivated, or version changed. 
  4224.  
  4225.                     $all_cached_themes->themes[ $slug ]['is_active'] = $is_active; 
  4226.                     $all_cached_themes->themes[ $slug ]['version'] = $all_themes[ $slug ]->version; 
  4227.  
  4228.                     $themes_update_data[] = $all_cached_themes->themes[ $slug ]; 
  4229.                 } 
  4230.             } 
  4231.  
  4232.             // Find new themes that weren't yet seen before. 
  4233.             foreach ( $all_themes as $slug => $data ) { 
  4234.                 if ( ! isset( $all_cached_themes->themes[ $slug ] ) ) { 
  4235.                     $is_active = ( $slug === $active_theme_stylesheet ); 
  4236.  
  4237.                     // New plugin. 
  4238.                     $new_plugin = array( 
  4239.                         'slug' => $slug,  
  4240.                         'version' => $data->version,  
  4241.                         'title' => $data->name,  
  4242.                         'is_active' => $is_active,  
  4243.                         'is_uninstalled' => false,  
  4244.  ); 
  4245.  
  4246.                     $themes_update_data[] = $new_plugin; 
  4247.                     $all_cached_themes->themes[ $slug ] = $new_plugin; 
  4248.                 } 
  4249.             } 
  4250.  
  4251.             $all_cached_themes->md5 = md5( $themes_signature ); 
  4252.             $all_cached_themes->timestamp = time(); 
  4253.             self::$_accounts->set_option( $option_name, $all_cached_themes, true ); 
  4254.         } 
  4255.  
  4256.         return $themes_update_data; 
  4257.     } 
  4258.  
  4259.     /** 
  4260.      * Update install details. 
  4261.      * 
  4262.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  4263.      * @since  1.1.2 
  4264.      * 
  4265.      * @param string[] string           $override 
  4266.      * @param bool     $include_plugins Since 1.1.8 by default include plugin changes. 
  4267.      * @param bool     $include_themes  Since 1.1.8 by default include plugin changes. 
  4268.      * 
  4269.      * @return array 
  4270.      */ 
  4271.     private function get_install_data_for_api( 
  4272.         array $override,  
  4273.         $include_plugins = true,  
  4274.         $include_themes = true 
  4275.  ) { 
  4276.         /** 
  4277.          * @since 1.1.8 Also send plugin updates. 
  4278.          */ 
  4279.         if ( $include_plugins && ! isset( $override['plugins'] ) ) { 
  4280.             $plugins = $this->get_plugins_data_for_api(); 
  4281.             if ( ! empty( $plugins ) ) { 
  4282.                 $override['plugins'] = $plugins; 
  4283.             } 
  4284.         } 
  4285.         /** 
  4286.          * @since 1.1.8 Also send themes updates. 
  4287.          */ 
  4288.         if ( $include_themes && ! isset( $override['themes'] ) ) { 
  4289.             $themes = $this->get_themes_data_for_api(); 
  4290.             if ( ! empty( $themes ) ) { 
  4291.                 $override['themes'] = $themes; 
  4292.             } 
  4293.         } 
  4294.  
  4295.         return array_merge( array( 
  4296.             'version' => $this->get_plugin_version(),  
  4297.             'is_premium' => $this->is_premium(),  
  4298.             'language' => get_bloginfo( 'language' ),  
  4299.             'charset' => get_bloginfo( 'charset' ),  
  4300.             'platform_version' => get_bloginfo( 'version' ),  
  4301.             'sdk_version' => $this->version,  
  4302.             'programming_language_version' => phpversion(),  
  4303.             'title' => get_bloginfo( 'name' ),  
  4304.             'url' => get_site_url(),  
  4305.             // Special params. 
  4306.             'is_active' => true,  
  4307.             'is_disconnected' => $this->is_tracking_prohibited(),  
  4308.             'is_uninstalled' => false,  
  4309.  ), $override ); 
  4310.     } 
  4311.  
  4312.     /** 
  4313.      * Update install only if changed. 
  4314.      * 
  4315.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  4316.      * @since  1.0.9 
  4317.      * 
  4318.      * @param string[] string $override 
  4319.      * @param bool     $flush 
  4320.      * 
  4321.      * @return false|object|string 
  4322.      */ 
  4323.     private function send_install_update( $override = array(), $flush = false ) { 
  4324.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  4325.  
  4326.         $check_properties = $this->get_install_data_for_api( $override ); 
  4327.  
  4328.         if ( $flush ) { 
  4329.             $params = $check_properties; 
  4330.         } else { 
  4331.             $params = array(); 
  4332.             $special = array(); 
  4333.             $special_override = false; 
  4334.  
  4335.             foreach ( $check_properties as $p => $v ) { 
  4336.                 if ( property_exists( $this->_site, $p ) ) { 
  4337.                     if ( ( is_bool( $this->_site->{$p} ) || ! empty( $this->_site->{$p} ) ) && 
  4338.                          $this->_site->{$p} != $v 
  4339.  ) { 
  4340.                         $this->_site->{$p} = $v; 
  4341.                         $params[ $p ]      = $v; 
  4342.                     } 
  4343.                 } else { 
  4344.                     $special[ $p ] = $v; 
  4345.  
  4346.                     if ( isset( $override[ $p ] ) || 
  4347.                          'plugins' === $p || 
  4348.                          'themes' === $p 
  4349.  ) { 
  4350.                         $special_override = true; 
  4351.                     } 
  4352.                 } 
  4353.             } 
  4354.  
  4355.             if ( $special_override || 0 < count( $params ) ) { 
  4356.                 // Add special params only if has at least one 
  4357.                 // standard param, or if explicitly requested to 
  4358.                 // override a special param or a param which is not exist 
  4359.                 // in the install object. 
  4360.                 $params = array_merge( $params, $special ); 
  4361.             } 
  4362.         } 
  4363.  
  4364.         if ( 0 < count( $params ) ) { 
  4365.             // Update last install sync timestamp. 
  4366.             $this->_storage->install_sync_timestamp = time(); 
  4367.  
  4368.             $params['uid'] = $this->get_anonymous_id(); 
  4369.  
  4370.             // Send updated values to FS. 
  4371.             $site = $this->get_api_site_scope()->call( '/', 'put', $params ); 
  4372.  
  4373.             if ( $this->is_api_result_entity( $site ) ) { 
  4374.                 // I successfully sent install update, clear scheduled sync if exist. 
  4375.                 $this->clear_install_sync_cron(); 
  4376.             } 
  4377.  
  4378.             return $site; 
  4379.         } 
  4380.  
  4381.         return false; 
  4382.     } 
  4383.  
  4384.     /** 
  4385.      * Update install only if changed. 
  4386.      * 
  4387.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  4388.      * @since  1.0.9 
  4389.      * 
  4390.      * @param string[] string $override 
  4391.      * @param bool     $flush 
  4392.      */ 
  4393.     private function sync_install( $override = array(), $flush = false ) { 
  4394.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  4395.  
  4396.         $site = $this->send_install_update( $override, $flush ); 
  4397.  
  4398.         if ( false === $site ) { 
  4399.             // No sync required. 
  4400.             return; 
  4401.         } 
  4402.  
  4403.         if ( ! $this->is_api_result_entity( $site ) ) { 
  4404.             // Failed to sync, don't update locally. 
  4405.             return; 
  4406.         } 
  4407.  
  4408.         $plan = $this->get_plan(); 
  4409.         $this->_site = new FS_Site( $site ); 
  4410.         $this->_site->plan = $plan; 
  4411.  
  4412.         $this->_store_site( true ); 
  4413.     } 
  4414.  
  4415.     /** 
  4416.      * Track install's custom event. 
  4417.      * 
  4418.      * IMPORTANT: 
  4419.      *      Custom event tracking is currently only supported for specific clients. 
  4420.      *      If you are not one of them, please don't use this method. If you will,  
  4421.      *      the API will simply ignore your request based on the plugin ID. 
  4422.      * 
  4423.      * Need custom tracking for your plugin or theme? 
  4424.      *      If you are interested in custom event tracking please contact yo@freemius.com 
  4425.      *      for further details. 
  4426.      * 
  4427.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  4428.      * @since  1.2.1 
  4429.      * 
  4430.      * @param string $name       Event name. 
  4431.      * @param array  $properties Associative key/value array with primitive values only 
  4432.      * @param bool   $process_at A valid future date-time in the following format Y-m-d H:i:s. 
  4433.      * @param bool   $once       If true, event will be tracked only once. IMPORTANT: Still trigger the API call. 
  4434.      * 
  4435.      * @return object|false Event data or FALSE on failure. 
  4436.      * 
  4437.      * @throws \Freemius_InvalidArgumentException 
  4438.      */ 
  4439.     public function track_event( $name, $properties = array(), $process_at = false, $once = false ) { 
  4440.         $this->_logger->entrance( http_build_query( array( 'name' => $name, 'once' => $once ) ) ); 
  4441.  
  4442.         if ( ! $this->is_registered() ) { 
  4443.             return false; 
  4444.         } 
  4445.  
  4446.         $event = array( 'type' => $name ); 
  4447.  
  4448.         if ( is_numeric( $process_at ) && $process_at > time() ) { 
  4449.             $event['process_at'] = $process_at; 
  4450.         } 
  4451.  
  4452.         if ( $once ) { 
  4453.             $event['once'] = true; 
  4454.         } 
  4455.  
  4456.         if ( ! empty( $properties ) ) { 
  4457.             // Verify associative array values are primitive. 
  4458.             foreach ( $properties as $k => $v ) { 
  4459.                 if ( ! is_scalar( $v ) ) { 
  4460.                     throw new Freemius_InvalidArgumentException( 'The $properties argument must be an associative key/value array with primitive values only.' ); 
  4461.                 } 
  4462.             } 
  4463.  
  4464.             $event['properties'] = $properties; 
  4465.         } 
  4466.  
  4467.         $result = $this->get_api_site_scope()->call( 'events.json', 'post', $event ); 
  4468.  
  4469.         return $this->is_api_error( $result ) ? 
  4470.             false : 
  4471.             $result; 
  4472.     } 
  4473.  
  4474.     /** 
  4475.      * Track install's custom event only once, but it still triggers the API call. 
  4476.      * 
  4477.      * IMPORTANT: 
  4478.      *      Custom event tracking is currently only supported for specific clients. 
  4479.      *      If you are not one of them, please don't use this method. If you will,  
  4480.      *      the API will simply ignore your request based on the plugin ID. 
  4481.      * 
  4482.      * Need custom tracking for your plugin or theme? 
  4483.      *      If you are interested in custom event tracking please contact yo@freemius.com 
  4484.      *      for further details. 
  4485.      * 
  4486.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  4487.      * @since  1.2.1 
  4488.      * 
  4489.      * @param string $name       Event name. 
  4490.      * @param array  $properties Associative key/value array with primitive values only 
  4491.      * @param bool   $process_at A valid future date-time in the following format Y-m-d H:i:s. 
  4492.      * 
  4493.      * @return object|false Event data or FALSE on failure. 
  4494.      * 
  4495.      * @throws \Freemius_InvalidArgumentException 
  4496.      * 
  4497.      * @user   Freemius::track_event() 
  4498.      */ 
  4499.     public function track_event_once( $name, $properties = array(), $process_at = false ) { 
  4500.         return $this->track_event( $name, $properties, $process_at, true ); 
  4501.     } 
  4502.  
  4503.     /** 
  4504.      * Plugin uninstall hook. 
  4505.      * 
  4506.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  4507.      * @since  1.0.1 
  4508.      * 
  4509.      * @param bool $check_user Enforce checking if user have plugins activation privileges. 
  4510.      */ 
  4511.     function _uninstall_plugin_event( $check_user = true ) { 
  4512.         $this->_logger->entrance( 'slug = ' . $this->_slug ); 
  4513.  
  4514.         if ( $check_user && ! current_user_can( 'activate_plugins' ) ) { 
  4515.             return; 
  4516.         } 
  4517.  
  4518.         $params = array(); 
  4519.         $uninstall_reason = null; 
  4520.         if ( isset( $this->_storage->uninstall_reason ) ) { 
  4521.             $uninstall_reason = $this->_storage->uninstall_reason; 
  4522.             $params['reason_id'] = $uninstall_reason->id; 
  4523.             $params['reason_info'] = $uninstall_reason->info; 
  4524.         } 
  4525.  
  4526.         if ( ! $this->is_registered() && isset( $uninstall_reason ) ) { 
  4527.             // Send anonymous uninstall event only if user submitted a feedback. 
  4528.             if ( isset( $uninstall_reason->is_anonymous ) && ! $uninstall_reason->is_anonymous ) { 
  4529.                 $this->opt_in( false, false, false, false, true ); 
  4530.             } else { 
  4531.                 $params['uid'] = $this->get_anonymous_id(); 
  4532.                 $this->get_api_plugin_scope()->call( 'uninstall.json', 'put', $params ); 
  4533.             } 
  4534.         } else { 
  4535.             // Send uninstall event. 
  4536.             $this->send_install_update( array_merge( $params, array( 
  4537.                 'is_active' => false,  
  4538.                 'is_uninstalled' => true,  
  4539.  ) ) ); 
  4540.         } 
  4541.  
  4542.         // @todo Decide if we want to delete plugin information from db. 
  4543.     } 
  4544.  
  4545.     /** 
  4546.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  4547.      * @since  1.1.1 
  4548.      * 
  4549.      * @return string 
  4550.      */ 
  4551.     private function premium_plugin_basename() { 
  4552.         return preg_replace( '/\//', '-premium/', $this->_free_plugin_basename, 1 ); 
  4553.     } 
  4554.  
  4555.     /** 
  4556.      * Uninstall plugin hook. Called only when connected his account with Freemius for active sites tracking. 
  4557.      * 
  4558.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  4559.      * @since  1.0.2 
  4560.      */ 
  4561.     public static function _uninstall_plugin_hook() { 
  4562.         self::_load_required_static(); 
  4563.  
  4564.         self::$_static_logger->entrance(); 
  4565.  
  4566.         if ( ! current_user_can( 'activate_plugins' ) ) { 
  4567.             return; 
  4568.         } 
  4569.  
  4570.         $plugin_file = substr( current_filter(), strlen( 'uninstall_' ) ); 
  4571.  
  4572.         self::$_static_logger->info( 'plugin = ' . $plugin_file ); 
  4573.  
  4574.         define( 'WP_FS__UNINSTALL_MODE', true ); 
  4575.  
  4576.         $fs = self::get_instance_by_file( $plugin_file ); 
  4577.  
  4578.         if ( is_object( $fs ) ) { 
  4579.             self::require_plugin_essentials(); 
  4580.  
  4581.             if ( is_plugin_active( $fs->_free_plugin_basename ) || 
  4582.                  is_plugin_active( $fs->premium_plugin_basename() ) 
  4583.  ) { 
  4584.                 // Deleting Free or Premium plugin version while the other version still installed. 
  4585.                 return; 
  4586.             } 
  4587.  
  4588.             $fs->_uninstall_plugin_event(); 
  4589.  
  4590.             $fs->do_action( 'after_uninstall' ); 
  4591.         } 
  4592.     }

  4631.      */ 
  4632.     function get_plugin_data() { 
  4633.         if ( ! isset( $this->_plugin_data ) ) { 
  4634.             self::require_plugin_essentials(); 
  4635.  
  4636.             /** 
  4637.              * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  4638.              * @since  1.2.0 When using get_plugin_data() do NOT translate plugin data.

  4640.              * @link   https://github.com/Freemius/wordpress-sdk/issues/77 
  4641.              */ 
  4642.             $this->_plugin_data = get_plugin_data( 
  4643.                 $this->_plugin_main_file_path,  
  4644.                 false,  
  4645.                 false 
  4646.  ); 
  4647.         } 
  4648.  
  4649.         return $this->_plugin_data; 
  4650.     }

  4726.     /**

  4728.      * @since  1.0.9 
  4729.      * 
  4730.      * @return string 
  4731.      */ 
  4732.     function get_plugin_name() { 
  4733.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  4734.  
  4735.         if ( ! isset( $this->_plugin_name ) ) { 
  4736.             $plugin_data = $this->get_plugin_data(); 
  4737.  
  4738.             // Get name. 
  4739.             $this->_plugin_name = $plugin_data['Name']; 
  4740.  
  4741.             // Check if plugin name contains [Premium] suffix and remove it. 
  4742.             $suffix = '[premium]'; 
  4743.             $suffix_len = strlen( $suffix ); 
  4744.  
  4745.             if ( strlen( $plugin_data['Name'] ) > $suffix_len && 
  4746.                  $suffix === substr( strtolower( $plugin_data['Name'] ), - $suffix_len ) 
  4747.  ) { 
  4748.                 $this->_plugin_name = substr( $plugin_data['Name'], 0, - $suffix_len ); 
  4749.             } 
  4750.  
  4751.             $this->_logger->departure( 'Name = ' . $this->_plugin_name ); 
  4752.         } 
  4753.  
  4754.         return $this->_plugin_name; 
  4755.     } 
  4756.

  4759.      * @since  1.0.0 
  4760.      *

  4762.      */ 
  4763.     function get_plugin_version() { 
  4764.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  4765.  
  4766.         $plugin_data = $this->get_plugin_data(); 
  4767.  
  4768.         $this->_logger->departure( 'Version = ' . $plugin_data['Version'] ); 
  4769.  
  4770.         return $this->apply_filters( 'plugin_version', $plugin_data['Version'] ); 
  4771.     }

  4783.     function get_plugin_folder_name() { 
  4784.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  4785.  
  4786.         $plugin_folder = $this->_plugin_basename; 
  4787.  
  4788.         while ( '.' !== dirname( $plugin_folder ) ) { 
  4789.             $plugin_folder = dirname( $plugin_folder ); 
  4790.         } 
  4791.  
  4792.         $this->_logger->departure( 'Folder Name = ' . $plugin_folder ); 
  4793.  
  4794.         return $plugin_folder; 
  4795.     }

  4802.     /** 
  4803.      * Find plugin's slug by plugin's basename. 
  4804.      * 
  4805.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  4806.      * @since  1.0.9 
  4807.      * 
  4808.      * @param string $plugin_base_name 
  4809.      * 
  4810.      * @return false|string 
  4811.      */ 
  4812.     private static function find_slug_by_basename( $plugin_base_name ) { 
  4813.         $file_slug_map = self::$_accounts->get_option( 'file_slug_map', array() ); 
  4814.  
  4815.         if ( ! array( $file_slug_map ) || ! isset( $file_slug_map[ $plugin_base_name ] ) ) { 
  4816.             return false; 
  4817.         } 
  4818.  
  4819.         return $file_slug_map[ $plugin_base_name ]; 
  4820.     } 
  4821.  
  4822.     /** 
  4823.      * Store the map between the plugin's basename to the slug. 
  4824.      * 
  4825.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  4826.      * @since  1.0.9 
  4827.      */ 
  4828.     private function store_file_slug_map() { 
  4829.         $file_slug_map = self::$_accounts->get_option( 'file_slug_map', array() ); 
  4830.  
  4831.         if ( ! array( $file_slug_map ) ) { 
  4832.             $file_slug_map = array(); 
  4833.         } 
  4834.  
  4835.         if ( ! isset( $file_slug_map[ $this->_plugin_basename ] ) || 
  4836.              $file_slug_map[ $this->_plugin_basename ] !== $this->_slug 
  4837.  ) { 
  4838.             $file_slug_map[ $this->_plugin_basename ] = $this->_slug; 
  4839.             self::$_accounts->set_option( 'file_slug_map', $file_slug_map, true ); 
  4840.         } 
  4841.     }

  4979.     /**

  5333.     /**

  5402.     /**

  5409.      * 
  5410.      * @return FS_Plugin_License[]|object 
  5411.      */ 
  5412.     function _sync_licenses( $site_license_id = false ) { 
  5413.         $licenses = $this->_fetch_licenses( false, $site_license_id ); 
  5414.  
  5415.         if ( $this->is_array_instanceof( $licenses, 'FS_Plugin_License' ) ) { 
  5416.             $this->_licenses = $licenses; 
  5417.             $this->_store_licenses(); 
  5418.         } 
  5419.  
  5420.         // Update current license. 
  5421.         if ( is_object( $this->_license ) ) { 
  5422.             $this->_license = $this->_get_license_by_id( $this->_license->id ); 
  5423.         } 
  5424.  
  5425.         return $this->_licenses; 
  5426.     } 
  5427.  
  5428.     /**

  5430.      * @since  1.0.5 
  5431.      * 
  5432.      * @param number $id 
  5433.      * 
  5434.      * @return FS_Plugin_License|false 
  5435.      */ 
  5436.     function _get_license_by_id( $id ) { 
  5437.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  5438.  
  5439.         if ( ! is_numeric( $id ) ) { 
  5440.             return false; 
  5441.         } 
  5442.  
  5443.         if ( ! $this->has_any_license() ) { 
  5444.             $this->_sync_licenses(); 
  5445.         } 
  5446.  
  5447.         foreach ( $this->_licenses as $license ) { 
  5448.             if ( $id == $license->id ) { 
  5449.                 return $license; 
  5450.             } 
  5451.         } 
  5452.  
  5453.         return false; 
  5454.     } 
  5455.  
  5456.     /** 
  5457.      * Sync site's license with user licenses. 
  5458.      * 
  5459.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  5460.      * @since  1.0.6 
  5461.      * 
  5462.      * @param FS_Plugin_License|null $new_license 
  5463.      */ 
  5464.     function _update_site_license( $new_license ) { 
  5465.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  5466.  
  5467.         $this->_license = $new_license; 
  5468.  
  5469.         if ( ! is_object( $new_license ) ) { 
  5470.             $this->_site->license_id = null; 
  5471.             $this->_sync_site_subscription( null ); 
  5472.  
  5473.             return; 
  5474.         } 
  5475.  
  5476.         $this->_site->license_id = $this->_license->id; 
  5477.  
  5478.         if ( ! is_array( $this->_licenses ) ) { 
  5479.             $this->_licenses = array(); 
  5480.         } 
  5481.  
  5482.         $is_license_found = false; 
  5483.         for ( $i = 0, $len = count( $this->_licenses ); $i < $len; $i ++ ) { 
  5484.             if ( $new_license->id == $this->_licenses[ $i ]->id ) { 
  5485.                 $this->_licenses[ $i ] = $new_license; 
  5486.  
  5487.                 $is_license_found = true; 
  5488.                 break; 
  5489.             } 
  5490.         } 
  5491.  
  5492.         // If new license just append. 
  5493.         if ( ! $is_license_found ) { 
  5494.             $this->_licenses[] = $new_license; 
  5495.         } 
  5496.  
  5497.         $this->_sync_site_subscription( $new_license ); 
  5498.     } 
  5499.  
  5500.     /** 
  5501.      * Sync site's subscription. 
  5502.      * 
  5503.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  5504.      * @since  1.0.9 
  5505.      * 
  5506.      * @param FS_Plugin_License|null $license 
  5507.      * 
  5508.      * @return bool|\FS_Subscription 
  5509.      */ 
  5510.     private function _sync_site_subscription( $license ) { 
  5511.         if ( ! is_object( $license ) ) { 
  5512.             unset( $this->_storage->subscription ); 
  5513.  
  5514.             return false; 
  5515.         } 
  5516.  
  5517.         // Load subscription details if not lifetime. 
  5518.         $subscription = $license->is_lifetime() ? 
  5519.             false : 
  5520.             $this->_fetch_site_license_subscription(); 
  5521.  
  5522.         if ( is_object( $subscription ) && ! isset( $subscription->error ) ) { 
  5523.             $this->_storage->subscription = $subscription; 
  5524.         } else { 
  5525.             unset( $this->_storage->subscription ); 
  5526.         } 
  5527.  
  5528.         return $subscription; 
  5529.     } 
  5530.  
  5531.     /** 
  5532.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  5533.      * @since  1.0.6 
  5534.      *

  5536.      */ 
  5537.     function _get_license() { 
  5538.         return $this->_license; 
  5539.     } 
  5540.  
  5541.     /** 
  5542.      * @return bool|\FS_Subscription 
  5543.      */ 
  5544.     function _get_subscription() { 
  5545.         return isset( $this->_storage->subscription ) ? 
  5546.             $this->_storage->subscription : 
  5547.             false; 
  5548.     } 
  5549.  
  5550.     /** 
  5551.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  5552.      * @since  1.0.2 
  5553.      * 
  5554.      * @param string $plan  Plan name 
  5555.      * @param bool   $exact If true, looks for exact plan. If false, also check "higher" plans. 
  5556.      * 
  5557.      * @return bool 
  5558.      */ 
  5559.     function is_plan( $plan, $exact = false ) { 
  5560.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  5561.  
  5562.         if ( ! $this->is_registered() ) { 
  5563.             return false; 
  5564.         } 
  5565.  
  5566.         $plan = strtolower( $plan ); 
  5567.  
  5568.         if ( $this->_site->plan->name === $plan ) // Exact plan. 
  5569.         { 
  5570.             return true; 
  5571.         } else if ( $exact ) // Required exact, but plans are different. 
  5572.         { 
  5573.             return false; 
  5574.         } 
  5575.  
  5576.         $current_plan_order = - 1; 
  5577.         $required_plan_order = - 1; 
  5578.         for ( $i = 0, $len = count( $this->_plans ); $i < $len; $i ++ ) { 
  5579.             if ( $plan === $this->_plans[ $i ]->name ) { 
  5580.                 $required_plan_order = $i; 
  5581.             } else if ( $this->_site->plan->name === $this->_plans[ $i ]->name ) { 
  5582.                 $current_plan_order = $i; 
  5583.             } 
  5584.         } 
  5585.  
  5586.         return ( $current_plan_order > $required_plan_order ); 
  5587.     } 
  5588.  
  5589.     /** 
  5590.      * Check if plan based on trial. If not in trial mode, should return false. 
  5591.      * 
  5592.      * @since  1.0.9 
  5593.      * 
  5594.      * @param string $plan  Plan name 
  5595.      * @param bool   $exact If true, looks for exact plan. If false, also check "higher" plans. 
  5596.      * 
  5597.      * @return bool 
  5598.      */ 
  5599.     function is_trial_plan( $plan, $exact = false ) { 
  5600.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  5601.  
  5602.         if ( ! $this->is_registered() ) { 
  5603.             return false; 
  5604.         } 
  5605.  
  5606.         if ( ! $this->is_trial() ) { 
  5607.             return false; 
  5608.         } 
  5609.  
  5610.         if ( ! isset( $this->_storage->trial_plan ) ) { 
  5611.             // Store trial plan information. 
  5612.             $this->_enrich_site_trial_plan( true ); 
  5613.         } 
  5614.  
  5615.         if ( $this->_storage->trial_plan->name === $plan ) // Exact plan. 
  5616.         { 
  5617.             return true; 
  5618.         } else if ( $exact ) // Required exact, but plans are different. 
  5619.         { 
  5620.             return false; 
  5621.         } 
  5622.  
  5623.         $current_plan_order = - 1; 
  5624.         $required_plan_order = - 1; 
  5625.         for ( $i = 0, $len = count( $this->_plans ); $i < $len; $i ++ ) { 
  5626.             if ( $plan === $this->_plans[ $i ]->name ) { 
  5627.                 $required_plan_order = $i; 
  5628.             } else if ( $this->_storage->trial_plan->name === $this->_plans[ $i ]->name ) { 
  5629.                 $current_plan_order = $i; 
  5630.             } 
  5631.         } 
  5632.  
  5633.         return ( $current_plan_order > $required_plan_order ); 
  5634.     } 
  5635.  
  5636.     /** 
  5637.      * Check if plugin has any paid plans. 
  5638.      * 
  5639.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  5640.      * @since  1.0.7 
  5641.      * 
  5642.      * @return bool 
  5643.      */ 
  5644.     function has_paid_plan() { 
  5645.         return $this->_has_paid_plans || 
  5646.                FS_Plan_Manager::instance()->has_paid_plan( $this->_plans ); 
  5647.     } 
  5648.  
  5649.     /** 
  5650.      * Check if plugin has any plan with a trail. 
  5651.      * 
  5652.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  5653.      * @since  1.0.9 
  5654.      * 
  5655.      * @return bool 
  5656.      */ 
  5657.     function has_trial_plan() { 
  5658.         if ( ! $this->is_registered() ) { 
  5659.             /** 
  5660.              * @author Vova Feldman(@svovaf) 
  5661.              * @since  1.2.1.5 
  5662.              * 
  5663.              * Allow setting a trial from the SDK without calling the API. 
  5664.              * But, if the user did opt-in, continue using the real data from the API. 
  5665.              */ 
  5666.             if ( $this->_trial_days >= 0 ) { 
  5667.                 return true; 
  5668.             } 
  5669.  
  5670.             return false; 
  5671.         } 
  5672.  
  5673.         return $this->_storage->get( 'has_trial_plan', false ); 
  5674.     } 
  5675.  
  5676.     /** 
  5677.      * Check if plugin has any free plan, or is it premium only. 
  5678.      * 
  5679.      * Note: If no plans configured, assume plugin is free. 
  5680.      * 
  5681.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  5682.      * @since  1.0.7 
  5683.      * 
  5684.      * @return bool 
  5685.      */ 
  5686.     function has_free_plan() { 
  5687.         return ! $this->is_only_premium(); 
  5688.     } 
  5689.  
  5690.     /** 
  5691.      * Displays a license activation dialog box when the user clicks on the "Activate License" 
  5692.      * or "Change License" link on the plugins 
  5693.      * page. 
  5694.      * 
  5695.      * @author Leo Fajardo (@leorw) 
  5696.      * @since  1.1.9 
  5697.      */ 
  5698.     function _add_license_activation_dialog_box() { 
  5699.         $vars = array( 
  5700.             'slug' => $this->_slug,  
  5701.  ); 
  5702.  
  5703.         fs_require_template( 'forms/license-activation.php', $vars ); 
  5704.         fs_require_template( 'forms/resend-key.php', $vars ); 
  5705.     } 
  5706.  
  5707.     /** 
  5708.      * Displays the opt-out dialog box when the user clicks on the "Opt Out" link on the "Plugins"

  5714.     function _add_optout_dialog() { 
  5715.         $vars = array(

  5717.  ); 
  5718.  
  5719.         fs_require_template( 'forms/optout.php', $vars ); 
  5720.     } 
  5721.  
  5722.     /** 
  5723.      * Prepare page to include all required UI and logic for the license activation dialog. 
  5724.      * 
  5725.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  5726.      * @since  1.2.0 
  5727.      */ 
  5728.     function _add_license_activation() { 
  5729.         if ( ! current_user_can( 'activate_plugins' ) ) { 
  5730.             // Only admins can activate a license. 
  5731.             return; 
  5732.         } 
  5733.  
  5734.         if ( ! $this->has_paid_plan() ) { 
  5735.             // Module doesn't have any paid plans. 
  5736.             return; 
  5737.         } 
  5738.  
  5739.         if ( ! $this->is_premium() ) { 
  5740.             // Only add license activation logic to the premium version. 
  5741.             return; 
  5742.         } 
  5743.  
  5744.         // Add license activation link and AJAX request handler. 
  5745.         if ( $this->is_plugins_page() ) { 
  5746.             /** 
  5747.              * @since 1.2.0 Add license action link only on plugins page. 
  5748.              */ 
  5749.             $this->_add_license_action_link(); 
  5750.         } 
  5751.  
  5752.         // Add license activation AJAX callback. 
  5753.         $this->add_ajax_action( 'activate_license', array( &$this, '_activate_license_ajax_action' ) ); 
  5754.  
  5755.         // Add resend license AJAX callback. 
  5756.         $this->add_ajax_action( 'resend_license_key', array( &$this, '_resend_license_key_ajax_action' ) ); 
  5757.     } 
  5758.  
  5759.     /** 
  5760.      * @author Leo Fajardo (@leorw) 
  5761.      * @since  1.1.9 
  5762.      */ 
  5763.     function _activate_license_ajax_action() { 
  5764.         $license_key = trim( fs_request_get( 'license_key' ) ); 
  5765.  
  5766.         if ( empty( $license_key ) ) { 
  5767.             exit; 
  5768.         } 
  5769.  
  5770.         $slug = $_POST['slug']; 
  5771.         $fs = ( ( $slug === $this->_slug ) ? $this : self::instance( $slug ) ); 
  5772.         $error = false; 
  5773.         $next_page = false; 
  5774.  
  5775.         if ( $this->is_registered() ) { 
  5776.             $api = $fs->get_api_site_scope(); 
  5777.             $install = $api->call( '/', 'put', array( 
  5778.                 'license_key' => $this->apply_filters( 'license_key', $license_key ) 
  5779.  ) ); 
  5780.  
  5781.             if ( isset( $install->error ) ) { 
  5782.                 $error = $install->error->message; 
  5783.             } else { 
  5784.                 $fs = $this->is_addon() ? 
  5785.                     $this->get_parent_instance() : 
  5786.                     $this; 
  5787.  
  5788.                 $next_page = $fs->_get_sync_license_url( $this->get_id(), true ); 
  5789.  
  5790.                 $this->reconnect_locally(); 
  5791.             } 
  5792.         } else { 
  5793.             $next_page = $this->opt_in( false, false, false, $license_key ); 
  5794.  
  5795.             if ( isset( $next_page->error ) ) { 
  5796.                 $error = $next_page->error; 
  5797.             } 
  5798.         } 
  5799.  
  5800.         $result = array( 
  5801.             'success' => ( false === $error ) 
  5802.  ); 
  5803.  
  5804.         if ( false !== $error ) { 
  5805.             $result['error'] = $error; 
  5806.         } else { 
  5807.             $result['next_page'] = $next_page; 
  5808.         } 
  5809.  
  5810.         echo json_encode( $result ); 
  5811.  
  5812.         exit; 
  5813.     } 
  5814.  
  5815.     /** 
  5816.      * Billing update AJAX callback. 
  5817.      * 
  5818.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  5819.      * @since  1.2.1.5 
  5820.      */ 
  5821.     function _update_billing_ajax_action() { 
  5822.         check_ajax_referer( $this->get_action_tag( 'update_billing' ), 'security' ); 
  5823.  
  5824.         if ( ! current_user_can( 'activate_plugins' ) ) { 
  5825.             // Only for admins. 
  5826.             $this->shoot_ajax_failure(); 
  5827.         } 
  5828.  
  5829.         $billing = fs_request_get( 'billing' ); 
  5830.  
  5831.         $api = $this->get_api_user_scope(); 
  5832.         $result = $api->call( '/billing.json', 'put', array_merge( $billing, array( 
  5833.             'plugin_id' => $this->get_parent_id(),  
  5834.  ) ) ); 
  5835.  
  5836.         if ( ! $this->is_api_result_entity( $result ) ) { 
  5837.             $this->shoot_ajax_failure(); 
  5838.         } 
  5839.  
  5840.         // Purge cached billing. 
  5841.         $this->get_api_user_scope()->purge_cache( 'billing.json' ); 
  5842.  
  5843.         $this->shoot_ajax_success(); 
  5844.     } 
  5845.  
  5846.     /** 
  5847.      * Trial start for anonymous users (AJAX callback). 
  5848.      * 
  5849.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  5850.      * @since  1.2.1.5 
  5851.      */ 
  5852.     function _start_trial_ajax_action() { 
  5853.         check_ajax_referer( $this->get_action_tag( 'start_trial' ), 'security' ); 
  5854.  
  5855.         if ( ! current_user_can( 'activate_plugins' ) ) { 
  5856.             // Only for admins. 
  5857.             $this->shoot_ajax_failure(); 
  5858.         } 
  5859.  
  5860.         $trial_data = fs_request_get( 'trial' ); 
  5861.  
  5862.         $next_page = $this->opt_in( 
  5863.             false,  
  5864.             false,  
  5865.             false,  
  5866.             false,  
  5867.             false,  
  5868.             $trial_data['plan_id'] 
  5869.  ); 
  5870.  
  5871.         if ( is_object( $next_page ) && $this->is_api_error( $next_page ) ) { 
  5872.             $this->shoot_ajax_failure( 
  5873.                 isset( $next_page->error ) ? 
  5874.                     $next_page->error->message : 
  5875.                     var_export( $next_page, true ) 
  5876.  ); 
  5877.         } 
  5878.  
  5879.         $this->shoot_ajax_success( array( 
  5880.             'next_page' => $next_page,  
  5881.  ) ); 
  5882.     } 
  5883.  
  5884.     /** 
  5885.      * @author Leo Fajardo (@leorw) 
  5886.      * @since  1.2.0 
  5887.      */ 
  5888.     function _resend_license_key_ajax_action() { 
  5889.         if ( ! isset( $_POST['email'] ) ) { 
  5890.             exit; 
  5891.         } 
  5892.  
  5893.         $email_address = trim( $_POST['email'] ); 
  5894.         if ( empty( $email_address ) ) { 
  5895.             exit; 
  5896.         } 
  5897.  
  5898.         $error = false; 
  5899.  
  5900.         $api = $this->get_api_plugin_scope(); 
  5901.         $result = $api->call( '/licenses/resend.json', 'post',  
  5902.             array( 
  5903.                 'email' => $email_address,  
  5904.                 'is_localhost' => WP_FS__IS_LOCALHOST 
  5905.  ) 
  5906.  ); 
  5907.  
  5908.         if ( is_object( $result ) && isset( $result->error ) ) { 
  5909.             $error = $result->error; 
  5910.  
  5911.             if ( in_array( $error->code, array( 'invalid_email', 'no_user' ) ) ) { 
  5912.                 $error = __fs( 'email-not-found' ); 
  5913.             } else if ( 'no_license' === $error->code ) { 
  5914.                 $error = __fs( 'no-active-licenses' ); 
  5915.             } else { 
  5916.                 $error = $error->message; 
  5917.             } 
  5918.         } 
  5919.  
  5920.         $licenses = array( 
  5921.             'success' => ( false === $error ) 
  5922.  ); 
  5923.  
  5924.         if ( false !== $error ) { 
  5925.             $licenses['error'] = sprintf( '%s... %s', __fs( 'oops', $this->_slug ), strtolower( $error ) ); 
  5926.         } 
  5927.  
  5928.         echo json_encode( $licenses ); 
  5929.  
  5930.         exit; 
  5931.     } 
  5932.  
  5933.     /** 
  5934.      * Helper method to check if user in the plugins page.

  5936.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  5937.      * @since  1.2.1.5 
  5938.      * 
  5939.      * @return bool 
  5940.      */ 
  5941.     private function is_plugins_page() { 
  5942.         global $pagenow; 
  5943.  
  5944.         return ( 'plugins.php' === $pagenow ); 
  5945.     }

  5980.     /** 
  5981.      * Plugin's pricing URL. 
  5982.      * 
  5983.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  5984.      * @since  1.0.4 
  5985.      * 
  5986.      * @param string $billing_cycle Billing cycle 
  5987.      * 
  5988.      * @param bool   $is_trial 
  5989.      * 
  5990.      * @return string 
  5991.      */ 
  5992.     function pricing_url( $billing_cycle = WP_FS__PERIOD_ANNUALLY, $is_trial = false ) { 
  5993.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  5994.  
  5995.         $params = array( 
  5996.             'billing_cycle' => $billing_cycle 
  5997.  ); 
  5998.  
  5999.         if ( $is_trial ) { 
  6000.             $params['trial'] = 'true'; 
  6001.         } 
  6002.  
  6003.         return $this->_get_admin_page_url( 'pricing', $params ); 
  6004.     }

  6013.      * @param bool   $is_trial 
  6014.      * @param array  $extra         (optional) Extra parameters, override other query params. 
  6015.      * 
  6016.      * @return string 
  6017.      */ 
  6018.     function checkout_url( 
  6019.         $billing_cycle = WP_FS__PERIOD_ANNUALLY,  
  6020.         $is_trial = false,  
  6021.         $extra = array() 
  6022.  ) { 
  6023.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  6024.  
  6025.         $params = array( 
  6026.             'checkout' => 'true',  
  6027.             'billing_cycle' => $billing_cycle,  
  6028.  ); 
  6029.  
  6030.         if ( $is_trial ) { 
  6031.             $params['trial'] = 'true'; 
  6032.         }

  6034.         /** 
  6035.          * Params in extra override other params. 
  6036.          */ 
  6037.         $params = array_merge( $params, $extra ); 
  6038.  
  6039.         return $this->_get_admin_page_url( 'pricing', $params ); 
  6040.     }

  6141.     /**

  6151.     /** 
  6152.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  6153.      * @since  1.0.9 
  6154.      * 
  6155.      * @return bool Is running in AJAX call. 
  6156.      * 
  6157.      * @link   http://wordpress.stackexchange.com/questions/70676/how-to-check-if-i-am-in-admin-ajax 
  6158.      */ 
  6159.     function is_ajax() { 
  6160.         return ( defined( 'DOING_AJAX' ) && DOING_AJAX ); 
  6161.     } 
  6162.  
  6163.     /** 
  6164.      * Check if it's an AJAX call targeted for the current module. 
  6165.      * 
  6166.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  6167.      * @since  1.2.0 
  6168.      * 
  6169.      * @param array|string $actions Collection of AJAX actions. 
  6170.      * 
  6171.      * @return bool 
  6172.      */ 
  6173.     function is_ajax_action( $actions ) { 
  6174.         // Verify it's an ajax call. 
  6175.         if ( ! $this->is_ajax() ) { 
  6176.             return false; 
  6177.         } 
  6178.  
  6179.         // Verify the call is relevant for the plugin. 
  6180.         if ( $this->_slug !== fs_request_get( 'slug' ) ) { 
  6181.             return false; 
  6182.         } 
  6183.  
  6184.         // Verify it's one of the specified actions. 
  6185.         if ( is_string( $actions ) ) { 
  6186.             $actions = explode( ', ', $actions ); 
  6187.         } 
  6188.  
  6189.         if ( is_array( $actions ) && 0 < count( $actions ) ) { 
  6190.             $ajax_action = fs_request_get( 'action' ); 
  6191.  
  6192.             foreach ( $actions as $action ) { 
  6193.                 if ( $ajax_action === $this->get_action_tag( $action ) ) { 
  6194.                     return true; 
  6195.                 } 
  6196.             } 
  6197.         } 
  6198.  
  6199.         return false; 
  6200.     } 
  6201.  
  6202.     /** 
  6203.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  6204.      * @since  1.1.7 
  6205.      * 
  6206.      * @return bool 
  6207.      */ 
  6208.     function is_cron() { 
  6209.         return ( defined( 'DOING_CRON' ) && DOING_CRON ); 
  6210.     } 
  6211.  
  6212.     /** 
  6213.      * Check if a real user is visiting the admin dashboard. 
  6214.      * 
  6215.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  6216.      * @since  1.1.7 
  6217.      * 
  6218.      * @return bool 
  6219.      */ 
  6220.     function is_user_in_admin() { 
  6221.         return is_admin() && ! $this->is_ajax() && ! $this->is_cron(); 
  6222.     } 
  6223.  
  6224.     /** 
  6225.      * Check if running in HTTPS and if site's plan matching the specified plan. 
  6226.      * 
  6227.      * @param string $plan 
  6228.      * @param bool   $exact 
  6229.      * 
  6230.      * @return bool 
  6231.      */ 
  6232.     function is_ssl_and_plan( $plan, $exact = false ) { 
  6233.         return ( $this->is_ssl() && $this->is_plan( $plan, $exact ) ); 
  6234.     } 
  6235.  
  6236.     /** 
  6237.      * Construct plugin's settings page URL. 
  6238.      * 
  6239.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  6240.      * @since  1.0.4 
  6241.      * 
  6242.      * @param string $page 
  6243.      * @param array  $params 
  6244.      * 
  6245.      * @return string 
  6246.      */ 
  6247.     function _get_admin_page_url( $page = '', $params = array() ) { 
  6248.         if ( 0 < count( $params ) ) { 
  6249.             foreach ( $params as $k => $v ) { 
  6250.                 $params[ $k ] = urlencode( $v ); 
  6251.             } 
  6252.         } 
  6253.  
  6254.         if ( ! $this->_menu->is_top_level() ) { 
  6255.             $parent_slug = $this->_menu->get_parent_slug(); 
  6256.             $menu_file = ( false !== strpos( $parent_slug, '.php' ) ) ? 
  6257.                 $parent_slug : 
  6258.                 'admin.php'; 
  6259.  
  6260.             return add_query_arg( array_merge( $params, array( 
  6261.                 'page' => $this->_menu->get_slug( $page ),  
  6262.  ) ), admin_url( $menu_file, 'admin' ) ); 
  6263.         } 
  6264.  
  6265.         if ( $this->_menu->is_cpt() ) { 
  6266.             if ( empty( $page ) && $this->is_activation_mode() ) { 
  6267.                 return add_query_arg( array_merge( $params, array( 
  6268.                     'page' => $this->_menu->get_slug() 
  6269.  ) ), admin_url( 'admin.php', 'admin' ) ); 
  6270.             } else { 
  6271.                 if ( ! empty( $page ) ) { 
  6272.                     $params['page'] = $this->_menu->get_slug( $page ); 
  6273.                 } 
  6274.  
  6275.                 return add_query_arg( $params, admin_url( $this->_menu->get_raw_slug(), 'admin' ) ); 
  6276.             } 
  6277.         } else { 
  6278.             return add_query_arg( array_merge( $params, array( 
  6279.                 'page' => $this->_menu->get_slug( $page ),  
  6280.  ) ), admin_url( 'admin.php', 'admin' ) ); 
  6281.         } 
  6282.     } 
  6283.  
  6284.     /**

  6299.             $params['plugin_id'] = $plugin_id; 
  6300.         }

  6302.         return $this->get_account_url( 
  6303.             $this->_slug . '_sync_license',  
  6304.             $params,  
  6305.             $add_action_nonce 
  6306.  );

  6309.     /**
