  6420.  
  6421.     /** Security 
  6422.     ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------*/ 
  6423.     private function _encrypt( $str ) { 
  6424.         if ( is_null( $str ) ) { 
  6425.             return null; 
  6426.         } 
  6427.  
  6428.         return base64_encode( $str ); 
  6429.     } 
  6430.  
  6431.     private function _decrypt( $str ) { 
  6432.         if ( is_null( $str ) ) { 
  6433.             return null; 
  6434.         } 
  6435.  
  6436.         return base64_decode( $str ); 
  6437.     } 
  6438.  
  6439.     /** 
  6440.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  6441.      * @since  1.0.5 
  6442.      * 
  6443.      * @param FS_Entity $entity 
  6444.      * 
  6445.      * @return FS_Entity Return an encrypted clone entity. 
  6446.      */ 
  6447.     private function _encrypt_entity( FS_Entity $entity ) { 
  6448.         $clone = clone $entity; 
  6449.         $props = get_object_vars( $entity ); 
  6450.  
  6451.         foreach ( $props as $key => $val ) { 
  6452.             $clone->{$key} = $this->_encrypt( $val ); 
  6453.         } 
  6454.  
  6455.         return $clone; 
  6456.     } 
  6457.  
  6458.     /** 
  6459.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  6460.      * @since  1.0.5 
  6461.      * 
  6462.      * @param FS_Entity $entity 
  6463.      * 
  6464.      * @return FS_Entity Return an decrypted clone entity. 
  6465.      */ 
  6466.     private function _decrypt_entity( FS_Entity $entity ) { 
  6467.         $clone = clone $entity; 
  6468.         $props = get_object_vars( $entity ); 
  6469.  
  6470.         foreach ( $props as $key => $val ) { 
  6471.             $clone->{$key} = $this->_decrypt( $val ); 
  6472.         } 
  6473.  
  6474.         return $clone; 
  6475.     } 
  6476.  
  6477.     /** 
  6478.      * Tries to activate account based on POST params. 
  6479.      * 
  6480.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  6481.      * @since  1.0.2 
  6482.      */ 
  6483.     function _activate_account() { 
  6484.         if ( $this->is_registered() ) { 
  6485.             // Already activated. 
  6486.             return; 
  6487.         } 
  6488.  
  6489.         self::_clean_admin_content_section(); 
  6490.  
  6491.         if ( fs_request_is_action( 'activate' ) && fs_request_is_post() ) { 
  6492. //                check_admin_referer( 'activate_' . $this->_plugin->public_key ); 
  6493.  
  6494.             // Verify matching plugin details. 
  6495.             if ( $this->_plugin->id != fs_request_get( 'plugin_id' ) || $this->_slug != fs_request_get( 'plugin_slug' ) ) { 
  6496.                 return; 
  6497.             } 
  6498.  
  6499.             $user = new FS_User(); 
  6500.             $user->id = fs_request_get( 'user_id' ); 
  6501.             $user->public_key = fs_request_get( 'user_public_key' ); 
  6502.             $user->secret_key = fs_request_get( 'user_secret_key' ); 
  6503.             $user->email = fs_request_get( 'user_email' ); 
  6504.             $user->first = fs_request_get( 'user_first' ); 
  6505.             $user->last = fs_request_get( 'user_last' ); 
  6506.             $user->is_verified = fs_request_get_bool( 'user_is_verified' ); 
  6507.  
  6508.             $site = new FS_Site(); 
  6509.             $site->id = fs_request_get( 'install_id' ); 
  6510.             $site->public_key = fs_request_get( 'install_public_key' ); 
  6511.             $site->secret_key = fs_request_get( 'install_secret_key' ); 
  6512.             $site->plan->id = fs_request_get( 'plan_id' ); 
  6513.             $site->plan->title = fs_request_get( 'plan_title' ); 
  6514.             $site->plan->name = fs_request_get( 'plan_name' ); 
  6515.  
  6516.             $plans = array(); 
  6517.             $plans_data = json_decode( urldecode( fs_request_get( 'plans' ) ) ); 
  6518.             foreach ( $plans_data as $p ) { 
  6519.                 $plans[] = new FS_Plugin_Plan( $p ); 
  6520.             } 
  6521.  
  6522.             $this->_set_account( $user, $site, $plans ); 
  6523.  
  6524.             // Reload the page with the keys. 
  6525.             fs_redirect( $this->_get_admin_page_url() ); 
  6526.         } 
  6527.     } 
  6528.  
  6529.     /** 
  6530.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  6531.      * @since  1.0.7 
  6532.      * 
  6533.      * @param string $email 
  6534.      * 
  6535.      * @return FS_User|bool 
  6536.      */ 
  6537.     static function _get_user_by_email( $email ) { 
  6538.         self::$_static_logger->entrance(); 
  6539.  
  6540.         $email = trim( strtolower( $email ) ); 
  6541.         $users = self::get_all_users(); 
  6542.         if ( is_array( $users ) ) { 
  6543.             foreach ( $users as $u ) { 
  6544.                 if ( $email === trim( strtolower( $u->email ) ) ) { 
  6545.                     return $u; 
  6546.                 } 
  6547.             } 
  6548.         } 
  6549.  
  6550.         return false; 
  6551.     } 
  6552.  
  6553.     #---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- 
  6554.     #region Account (Loading, Updates & Activation) 
  6555.     #---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- 
  6556.  
  6557.     /*** 
  6558.      * Load account information (user + site). 
  6559.      * 
  6560.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  6561.      * @since  1.0.1 
  6562.      */ 
  6563.     private function _load_account() { 
  6564.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  6565.  
  6566.         $this->do_action( 'before_account_load' ); 
  6567.  
  6568.         $sites = self::get_all_sites(); 
  6569.         $users = self::get_all_users(); 
  6570.         $plans = self::get_all_plans(); 
  6571.         $licenses = self::get_all_licenses(); 
  6572.  
  6573.         if ( $this->_logger->is_on() && is_admin() ) { 
  6574.             $this->_logger->log( 'sites = ' . var_export( $sites, true ) ); 
  6575.             $this->_logger->log( 'users = ' . var_export( $users, true ) ); 
  6576.             $this->_logger->log( 'plans = ' . var_export( $plans, true ) ); 
  6577.             $this->_logger->log( 'licenses = ' . var_export( $licenses, true ) ); 
  6578.         } 
  6579.  
  6580.         $site = isset( $sites[ $this->_slug ] ) ? $sites[ $this->_slug ] : false; 
  6581.  
  6582.         if ( is_object( $site ) && 
  6583.              is_numeric( $site->id ) && 
  6584.              is_numeric( $site->user_id ) && 
  6585.              is_object( $site->plan ) 
  6586.  ) { 
  6587.             // Load site. 
  6588.             $this->_site = clone $site; 
  6589.             $this->_site->plan = $this->_decrypt_entity( $this->_site->plan ); 
  6590.  
  6591.             // Load relevant user. 
  6592.             $this->_user = clone $users[ $this->_site->user_id ]; 
  6593.  
  6594.             // Load plans. 
  6595.             $this->_plans = $plans[ $this->_slug ]; 
  6596.             if ( ! is_array( $this->_plans ) || empty( $this->_plans ) ) { 
  6597.                 $this->_sync_plans(); 
  6598.             } else { 
  6599.                 for ( $i = 0, $len = count( $this->_plans ); $i < $len; $i ++ ) { 
  6600.                     if ( $this->_plans[ $i ] instanceof FS_Plugin_Plan ) { 
  6601.                         $this->_plans[ $i ] = $this->_decrypt_entity( $this->_plans[ $i ] ); 
  6602.                     } else { 
  6603.                         unset( $this->_plans[ $i ] ); 
  6604.                     } 
  6605.                 } 
  6606.             } 
  6607.  
  6608.             // Load licenses. 
  6609.             $this->_licenses = array(); 
  6610.             if ( is_array( $licenses ) && 
  6611.                  isset( $licenses[ $this->_slug ] ) && 
  6612.                  isset( $licenses[ $this->_slug ][ $this->_user->id ] ) 
  6613.  ) { 
  6614.                 $this->_licenses = $licenses[ $this->_slug ][ $this->_user->id ]; 
  6615.             } 
  6616.  
  6617.             $this->_license = $this->_get_license_by_id( $this->_site->license_id ); 
  6618.  
  6619.             if ( $this->_site->version != $this->get_plugin_version() ) { 
  6620.                 // If stored install version is different than current installed plugin version,  
  6621.                 // then update plugin version event. 
  6622.                 $this->update_plugin_version_event(); 
  6623.             } 
  6624.         } 
  6625.  
  6626.         $this->_register_account_hooks(); 
  6627.     } 
  6628.  
  6629.     /** 
  6630.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  6631.      * @since  1.0.1 
  6632.      * 
  6633.      * @param FS_User    $user 
  6634.      * @param FS_Site    $site 
  6635.      * @param bool|array $plans 
  6636.      */ 
  6637.     private function _set_account( FS_User $user, FS_Site $site, $plans = false ) { 
  6638.         $site->slug = $this->_slug; 
  6639.         $site->user_id = $user->id; 
  6640.  
  6641.         $this->_site = $site; 
  6642.         $this->_user = $user; 
  6643.         if ( false !== $plans ) { 
  6644.             $this->_plans = $plans; 
  6645.         } 
  6646.  
  6647.         $this->send_install_update(); 
  6648.  
  6649.         $this->_store_account(); 
  6650.  
  6651.     } 
  6652.  
  6653.     /** 
  6654.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  6655.      * @since  1.1.7.4 
  6656.      * 
  6657.      * @param array $override_with 
  6658.      * 
  6659.      * @return array 
  6660.      */ 
  6661.     function get_opt_in_params( $override_with = array() ) { 
  6662.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  6663.  
  6664.         $current_user = self::_get_current_wp_user(); 
  6665.  
  6666.         $activation_action = $this->_slug . '_activate_new'; 
  6667.         $return_url = $this->is_anonymous() ? 
  6668.             // If skipped already, then return to the account page. 
  6669.             $this->get_account_url( $activation_action, array(), false ) : 
  6670.             // Return to the module's main page. 
  6671.             $this->_get_admin_page_url( 
  6672.                 '',  
  6673.                 array( 'fs_action' => $activation_action ) 
  6674.  ); 
  6675.  
  6676.         $params = array( 
  6677.             'user_firstname' => $current_user->user_firstname,  
  6678.             'user_lastname' => $current_user->user_lastname,  
  6679.             'user_nickname' => $current_user->user_nicename,  
  6680.             'user_email' => $current_user->user_email,  
  6681.             'user_ip' => WP_FS__REMOTE_ADDR,  
  6682.             'plugin_slug' => $this->_slug,  
  6683.             'plugin_id' => $this->get_id(),  
  6684.             'plugin_public_key' => $this->get_public_key(),  
  6685.             'plugin_version' => $this->get_plugin_version(),  
  6686.             'return_url' => fs_nonce_url( $return_url, $activation_action ),  
  6687.             'account_url' => fs_nonce_url( $this->_get_admin_page_url( 
  6688.                 'account',  
  6689.                 array( 'fs_action' => 'sync_user' ) 
  6690.  ), 'sync_user' ),  
  6691.             'site_uid' => $this->get_anonymous_id(),  
  6692.             'site_url' => get_site_url(),  
  6693.             'site_name' => get_bloginfo( 'name' ),  
  6694.             'platform_version' => get_bloginfo( 'version' ),  
  6695.             'sdk_version' => $this->version,  
  6696.             'programming_language_version' => phpversion(),  
  6697.             'language' => get_bloginfo( 'language' ),  
  6698.             'charset' => get_bloginfo( 'charset' ),  
  6699.             'is_premium' => $this->is_premium(),  
  6700.             'is_active' => true,  
  6701.             'is_uninstalled' => false,  
  6702.  ); 
  6703.  
  6704.         if ( $this->is_pending_activation() && 
  6705.              ! empty( $this->_storage->pending_license_key ) 
  6706.  ) { 
  6707.             $params['license_key'] = $this->_storage->pending_license_key; 
  6708.         } 
  6709.  
  6710.         if ( WP_FS__SKIP_EMAIL_ACTIVATION && $this->has_secret_key() ) { 
  6711.             // Even though rand() is known for its security issues,  
  6712.             // the timestamp adds another layer of protection. 
  6713.             // It would be very hard for an attacker to get the secret key form here. 
  6714.             // Plus, this should never run in production since the secret should never 
  6715.             // be included in the production version. 
  6716.             $params['ts'] = WP_FS__SCRIPT_START_TIME; 
  6717.             $params['salt'] = md5( uniqid( rand() ) ); 
  6718.             $params['secure'] = md5( 
  6719.                 $params['ts'] . 
  6720.                 $params['salt'] . 
  6721.                 $this->get_secret_key() 
  6722.  ); 
  6723.         } 
  6724.  
  6725.         return array_merge( $params, $override_with ); 
  6726.     } 
  6727.  
  6728.     /** 
  6729.      * 1. If successful opt-in or pending activation returns the next page that the user should be redirected to. 
  6730.      * 2. If there was an API error, return the API result. 
  6731.      * 
  6732.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  6733.      * @since  1.1.7.4 
  6734.      * 
  6735.      * @param string|bool $email 
  6736.      * @param string|bool $first 
  6737.      * @param string|bool $last 
  6738.      * @param string|bool $license_key 
  6739.      * @param bool        $is_uninstall       If "true", this means that the module is currently being uninstalled. 
  6740.      *                                        In this case, the user and site info will be sent to the server but no 
  6741.      *                                        data will be saved to the WP installation's database. 
  6742.      * @param number|bool $trial_plan_id 
  6743.      * 
  6744.      * @return string|object 
  6745.      * @use    WP_Error 
  6746.      */ 
  6747.     function opt_in( 
  6748.         $email = false,  
  6749.         $first = false,  
  6750.         $last = false,  
  6751.         $license_key = false,  
  6752.         $is_uninstall = false,  
  6753.         $trial_plan_id = false 
  6754.  ) { 
  6755.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  6756.  
  6757.         if ( false === $email ) { 
  6758.             $current_user = self::_get_current_wp_user(); 
  6759.             $email = $current_user->user_email; 
  6760.         } 
  6761.  
  6762.         /** 
  6763.          * @since 1.2.1 If activating with license key, ignore the context-user 
  6764.          *              since the user will be automatically loaded from the license. 
  6765.          */ 
  6766.         if ( empty( $license_key ) ) { 
  6767.             // Clean up pending license if opt-ing in again. 
  6768.             $this->_storage->remove( 'pending_license_key' ); 
  6769.  
  6770.             if ( ! $is_uninstall ) { 
  6771.                 $fs_user = Freemius::_get_user_by_email( $email ); 
  6772.                 if ( is_object( $fs_user ) && ! $this->is_pending_activation() ) { 
  6773.                     return $this->install_with_current_user( false, $trial_plan_id ); 
  6774.                 } 
  6775.             } 
  6776.         } 
  6777.  
  6778.         $user_info = array(); 
  6779.         if ( ! empty( $email ) ) { 
  6780.             $user_info['user_email'] = $email; 
  6781.         } 
  6782.         if ( ! empty( $first ) ) { 
  6783.             $user_info['user_firstname'] = $first; 
  6784.         } 
  6785.         if ( ! empty( $last ) ) { 
  6786.             $user_info['user_lastname'] = $last; 
  6787.         } 
  6788.  
  6789.         $params = $this->get_opt_in_params( $user_info ); 
  6790.  
  6791.         $filtered_license_key = false; 
  6792.         if ( is_string( $license_key ) ) { 
  6793.             $filtered_license_key = $this->apply_filters( 'license_key', $license_key ); 
  6794.             $params['license_key'] = $filtered_license_key; 
  6795.         } else if ( FS_Plugin_Plan::is_valid_id( $trial_plan_id ) ) { 
  6796.             $params['trial_plan_id'] = $trial_plan_id; 
  6797.         } 
  6798.  
  6799.         if ( $is_uninstall ) { 
  6800.             $params['uninstall_params'] = array( 
  6801.                 'reason_id' => $this->_storage->uninstall_reason->id,  
  6802.                 'reason_info' => $this->_storage->uninstall_reason->info 
  6803.  ); 
  6804.         } 
  6805.  
  6806.         $params['format'] = 'json'; 
  6807.  
  6808.         $url = WP_FS__ADDRESS . '/action/service/user/install/'; 
  6809.         if ( isset( $_COOKIE['XDEBUG_SESSION'] ) ) { 
  6810.             $url = add_query_arg( 'XDEBUG_SESSION', 'PHPSTORM', $url ); 
  6811.         } 
  6812.  
  6813.         $response = wp_remote_post( $url, array( 
  6814.             'method' => 'POST',  
  6815.             'body' => $params,  
  6816.             'timeout' => 15,  
  6817.  ) ); 
  6818.  
  6819.         if ( $response instanceof WP_Error ) { 
  6820.             if ( 'https://' === substr( $url, 0, 8 ) && 
  6821.                  isset( $response->errors ) && 
  6822.                  isset( $response->errors['http_request_failed'] ) 
  6823.  ) { 
  6824.                 $http_error = strtolower( $response->errors['http_request_failed'][0] ); 
  6825.  
  6826.                 if ( false !== strpos( $http_error, 'ssl' ) ) { 
  6827.                     // Failed due to old version of cURL or Open SSL (SSLv3 is not supported by CloudFlare). 
  6828.                     $url = 'http://' . substr( $url, 8 ); 
  6829.  
  6830.                     $response = wp_remote_post( $url, array( 
  6831.                         'method' => 'POST',  
  6832.                         'body' => $params,  
  6833.                         'timeout' => 15,  
  6834.  ) ); 
  6835.                 } 
  6836.             } 
  6837.         } 
  6838.  
  6839.         if ( is_wp_error( $response ) ) { 
  6840.             /** 
  6841.              * @var WP_Error $response 
  6842.              */ 
  6843.             $result = new stdClass(); 
  6844.  
  6845.             $error_code = $response->get_error_code(); 
  6846.             $error_type = str_replace( ' ', '', ucwords( str_replace( '_', ' ', $error_code ) ) ); 
  6847.  
  6848.             $result->error = (object) array( 
  6849.                 'type' => $error_type,  
  6850.                 'message' => $response->get_error_message(),  
  6851.                 'code' => $error_code,  
  6852.                 'http' => 402 
  6853.  ); 
  6854.  
  6855.             return $result; 
  6856.         } 
  6857.  
  6858.         // Module is being uninstalled, don't handle the returned data. 
  6859.         if ( $is_uninstall ) { 
  6860.             return true; 
  6861.         } 
  6862.  
  6863.         $decoded = @json_decode( $response['body'] ); 
  6864.  
  6865.         if ( empty( $decoded ) ) { 
  6866.             return false; 
  6867.         } 
  6868.  
  6869.         if ( ! $this->is_api_result_object( $decoded ) ) { 
  6870.             if ( ! empty( $params['license_key'] ) ) { 
  6871.                 // Pass the fully entered license key to the failure handler. 
  6872.                 $params['license_key'] = $license_key; 
  6873.             } 
  6874.  
  6875.             return $is_uninstall ? 
  6876.                 $decoded : 
  6877.                 $this->apply_filters( 'after_install_failure', $decoded, $params ); 
  6878.         } else if ( isset( $decoded->pending_activation ) && $decoded->pending_activation ) { 
  6879.             // Pending activation, add message. 
  6880.             return $this->set_pending_confirmation( 
  6881.                 true,  
  6882.                 false,  
  6883.                 $filtered_license_key,  
  6884.                 ! empty( $params['trial_plan_id'] ) 
  6885.  ); 
  6886.         } else if ( isset( $decoded->install_secret_key ) ) { 
  6887.             return $this->install_with_new_user( 
  6888.                 $decoded->user_id,  
  6889.                 $decoded->user_public_key,  
  6890.                 $decoded->user_secret_key,  
  6891.                 $decoded->install_id,  
  6892.                 $decoded->install_public_key,  
  6893.                 $decoded->install_secret_key,  
  6894.                 false 
  6895.  ); 
  6896.         } 
  6897.  
  6898.         return $decoded; 
  6899.     } 
  6900.  
  6901.     /** 
  6902.      * Set user and site identities. 
  6903.      * 
  6904.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  6905.      * @since  1.0.9 
  6906.      * 
  6907.      * @param FS_User $user 
  6908.      * @param FS_Site $site 
  6909.      * @param bool    $redirect 
  6910.      * 
  6911.      * @return string If redirect is `false`, returns the next page the user should be redirected to. 
  6912.      */ 
  6913.     function setup_account( FS_User $user, FS_Site $site, $redirect = true ) { 
  6914.         $this->_user = $user; 
  6915.         $this->_site = $site; 
  6916.  
  6917.         $this->_sync_plans(); 
  6918.  
  6919.         $this->_enrich_site_plan( false ); 
  6920.  
  6921.         $this->_set_account( $user, $site ); 
  6922.  
  6923.         if ( $this->is_trial() ) { 
  6924.             // Store trial plan information. 
  6925.             $this->_enrich_site_trial_plan( true ); 
  6926.         } 
  6927.  
  6928.         // If Freemius was OFF before, turn it on. 
  6929.         $this->turn_on(); 
  6930.  
  6931.         $this->do_action( 'after_account_connection', $user, $site ); 
  6932.  
  6933.         if ( is_numeric( $site->license_id ) ) { 
  6934.             $this->_license = $this->_get_license_by_id( $site->license_id ); 
  6935.         } 
  6936.  
  6937.         $this->_admin_notices->remove_sticky( 'connect_account' ); 
  6938.  
  6939.         if ( $this->is_pending_activation() ) { 
  6940.             // Remove pending activation sticky notice (if still exist). 
  6941.             $this->_admin_notices->remove_sticky( 'activation_pending' ); 
  6942.  
  6943.             // Remove plugin from pending activation mode. 
  6944.             unset( $this->_storage->is_pending_activation ); 
  6945.  
  6946.             if ( ! $this->is_paying_or_trial() ) { 
  6947.                 $this->_admin_notices->add_sticky( 
  6948.                     sprintf( __fs( 'plugin-x-activation-message', $this->_slug ), '<b>' . $this->get_plugin_name() . '</b>' ),  
  6949.                     'activation_complete' 
  6950.  ); 
  6951.             } 
  6952.         } 
  6953.  
  6954.         if ( $this->is_paying_or_trial() && ! $this->is_premium() ) { 
  6955.             if ( $this->is_paying() ) { 
  6956.                 $this->_admin_notices->add_sticky( 
  6957.                     sprintf( 
  6958.                         __fs( 'activation-with-plan-x-message', $this->_slug ),  
  6959.                         $this->_site->plan->title 
  6960.  ) . $this->get_complete_upgrade_instructions(),  
  6961.                     'plan_upgraded',  
  6962.                     __fs( 'yee-haw', $this->_slug ) . '!' 
  6963.  ); 
  6964.             } else { 
  6965.                 $this->_admin_notices->add_sticky( 
  6966.                     sprintf( 
  6967.                         __fs( 'trial-started-message', $this->_slug ),  
  6968.                         '<i>' . $this->get_plugin_name() . '</i>' 
  6969.  ) . $this->get_complete_upgrade_instructions( $this->_storage->trial_plan->title ),  
  6970.                     'trial_started',  
  6971.                     __fs( 'yee-haw', $this->_slug ) . '!' 
  6972.  ); 
  6973.             } 
  6974.  
  6975.             $this->_admin_notices->remove_sticky( array( 
  6976.                 'trial_promotion',  
  6977.  ) ); 
  6978.         } 
  6979.  
  6980.         $plugin_id = fs_request_get( 'plugin_id', false ); 
  6981.  
  6982.         // Store activation time ONLY for plugins (not add-ons). 
  6983.         if ( ! is_numeric( $plugin_id ) || ( $plugin_id == $this->_plugin->id ) ) { 
  6984.             $this->_storage->activation_timestamp = WP_FS__SCRIPT_START_TIME; 
  6985.         } 
  6986.  
  6987.         $next_page = ''; 
  6988.  
  6989.         if ( is_numeric( $plugin_id ) ) { 
  6990.             if ( $plugin_id != $this->_plugin->id ) { 
  6991.                 // Add-on was installed - sync license right after install. 
  6992.                 $next_page = $this->_get_sync_license_url( $plugin_id ); 
  6993.             } 
  6994.         } else { 
  6995.             /** 
  6996.              * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  6997.              * @since  1.1.9 If site installed with a valid license, sync license. 
  6998.              */ 
  6999.             if ( $this->is_paying() ) { 
  7000.                 $this->_sync_plugin_license( true ); 
  7001.             } 
  7002.  
  7003.             // Reload the page with the keys. 
  7004.             $next_page = $this->is_anonymous() ? 
  7005.                 // If user previously skipped, redirect to account page. 
  7006.                 $this->get_account_url() : 
  7007.                 $this->get_after_activation_url( 'after_connect_url' ); 
  7008.         } 
  7009.  
  7010.         if ( ! empty( $next_page ) && $redirect ) { 
  7011.             fs_redirect( $next_page ); 
  7012.         } 
  7013.  
  7014.         return $next_page; 
  7015.     } 
  7016.  
  7017.     /** 
  7018.      * Install plugin with new user information after approval. 
  7019.      * 
  7020.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  7021.      * @since  1.0.7 
  7022.      */ 
  7023.     function _install_with_new_user() { 
  7024.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  7025.  
  7026.         if ( $this->is_registered() ) { 
  7027.             return; 
  7028.         } 
  7029.  
  7030.         if ( fs_request_is_action( $this->_slug . '_activate_new' ) ) { 
  7031. //                check_admin_referer( $this->_slug . '_activate_new' ); 
  7032.  
  7033.             if ( fs_request_has( 'user_secret_key' ) ) { 
  7034.                 $this->install_with_new_user( 
  7035.                     fs_request_get( 'user_id' ),  
  7036.                     fs_request_get( 'user_public_key' ),  
  7037.                     fs_request_get( 'user_secret_key' ),  
  7038.                     fs_request_get( 'install_id' ),  
  7039.                     fs_request_get( 'install_public_key' ),  
  7040.                     fs_request_get( 'install_secret_key' ) 
  7041.  ); 
  7042.             } else if ( fs_request_has( 'pending_activation' ) ) { 
  7043.                 $this->set_pending_confirmation( fs_request_get( 'user_email' ), true ); 
  7044.             } 
  7045.         } 
  7046.     } 
  7047.  
  7048.     /** 
  7049.      * Install plugin with new user. 
  7050.      * 
  7051.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  7052.      * @since  1.1.7.4 
  7053.      * 
  7054.      * @param number $user_id 
  7055.      * @param string $user_public_key 
  7056.      * @param string $user_secret_key 
  7057.      * @param number $install_id 
  7058.      * @param string $install_public_key 
  7059.      * @param string $install_secret_key 
  7060.      * @param bool   $redirect 
  7061.      * 
  7062.      * @return string If redirect is `false`, returns the next page the user should be redirected to. 
  7063.      */ 
  7064.     private function install_with_new_user( 
  7065.         $user_id,  
  7066.         $user_public_key,  
  7067.         $user_secret_key,  
  7068.         $install_id,  
  7069.         $install_public_key,  
  7070.         $install_secret_key,  
  7071.         $redirect = true 
  7072.  ) { 
  7073.         $user = new FS_User(); 
  7074.         $user->id = $user_id; 
  7075.         $user->public_key = $user_public_key; 
  7076.         $user->secret_key = $user_secret_key; 
  7077.  
  7078.         $this->_user = $user; 
  7079.         $user_result = $this->get_api_user_scope()->get(); 
  7080.         $user = new FS_User( $user_result ); 
  7081.         $this->_user = $user; 
  7082.  
  7083.         $site = new FS_Site(); 
  7084.         $site->id = $install_id; 
  7085.         $site->public_key = $install_public_key; 
  7086.         $site->secret_key = $install_secret_key; 
  7087.  
  7088.         $this->_site = $site; 
  7089.         $site_result = $this->get_api_site_scope()->get(); 
  7090.         $site = new FS_Site( $site_result ); 
  7091.         $this->_site = $site; 
  7092.  
  7093.         return $this->setup_account( $this->_user, $this->_site, $redirect ); 
  7094.     } 
  7095.  
  7096.     /** 
  7097.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  7098.      * @since  1.1.7.4 
  7099.      * 
  7100.      * @param string|bool $email 
  7101.      * @param bool        $redirect 
  7102.      * @param string|bool $license_key      Since 1.2.1.5 
  7103.      * @param bool        $is_pending_trial Since 1.2.1.5 
  7104.      * 
  7105.      * @return string Since 1.2.1.5 if $redirect is `false`, return the pending activation page. 
  7106.      */ 
  7107.     private function set_pending_confirmation( 
  7108.         $email = false,  
  7109.         $redirect = true,  
  7110.         $license_key = false,  
  7111.         $is_pending_trial = false 
  7112.  ) { 
  7113.         // Install must be activated via email since 
  7114.         // user with the same email already exist. 
  7115.         $this->_storage->is_pending_activation = true; 
  7116.         $this->_add_pending_activation_notice( $email, $is_pending_trial ); 
  7117.  
  7118.         if ( ! empty( $license_key ) ) { 
  7119.             $this->_storage->pending_license_key = $license_key; 
  7120.         } 
  7121.  
  7122.         // Remove the opt-in sticky notice. 
  7123.         $this->_admin_notices->remove_sticky( array( 
  7124.             'connect_account',  
  7125.             'trial_promotion',  
  7126.  ) ); 
  7127.  
  7128.         $next_page = $this->get_after_activation_url( 'after_pending_connect_url' ); 
  7129.  
  7130.         // Reload the page with with pending activation message. 
  7131.         if ( $redirect ) { 
  7132.             fs_redirect( $next_page ); 
  7133.         } 
  7134.  
  7135.         return $next_page; 
  7136.     } 
  7137.  
  7138.     /** 
  7139.      * Install plugin with current logged WP user info. 
  7140.      * 
  7141.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  7142.      * @since  1.0.7 
  7143.      */ 
  7144.     function _install_with_current_user() { 
  7145.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  7146.  
  7147.         if ( $this->is_registered() ) { 
  7148.             return; 
  7149.         } 
  7150.  
  7151.         if ( fs_request_is_action( $this->_slug . '_activate_existing' ) && fs_request_is_post() ) { 
  7152. //                check_admin_referer( 'activate_existing_' . $this->_plugin->public_key ); 
  7153.  
  7154.             /** 
  7155.              * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  7156.              * @since  1.1.9 Add license key if given. 
  7157.              */ 
  7158.             $license_key = fs_request_get( 'license_secret_key' ); 
  7159.  
  7160.             $this->install_with_current_user( $license_key ); 
  7161.         } 
  7162.     } 
  7163.  
  7164.  
  7165.     /** 
  7166.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  7167.      * @since  1.1.7.4 
  7168.      * 
  7169.      * @param string|bool $license_key 
  7170.      * @param number|bool $trial_plan_id 
  7171.      * @param bool        $redirect 
  7172.      * 
  7173.      * @return string|object If redirect is `false`, returns the next page the user should be redirected to, or the 
  7174.      *                       API error object if failed to install. 
  7175.      */ 
  7176.     private function install_with_current_user( 
  7177.         $license_key = false,  
  7178.         $trial_plan_id = false,  
  7179.         $redirect = true 
  7180.  ) { 
  7181.         // Get current logged WP user. 
  7182.         $current_user = self::_get_current_wp_user(); 
  7183.  
  7184.         // Find the relevant FS user by the email. 
  7185.         $user = self::_get_user_by_email( $current_user->user_email ); 
  7186.  
  7187.         // We have to set the user before getting user scope API handler. 
  7188.         $this->_user = $user; 
  7189.  
  7190.         $extra_install_params = array( 
  7191.             'uid' => $this->get_anonymous_id(),  
  7192.  ); 
  7193.  
  7194.         if ( ! empty( $license_key ) ) { 
  7195.             $filtered_license_key = $this->apply_filters( 'license_key', $license_key ); 
  7196.             $extra_install_params['license_key'] = $filtered_license_key; 
  7197.         } else if ( FS_Plugin_Plan::is_valid_id( $trial_plan_id ) ) { 
  7198.             $extra_install_params['trial_plan_id'] = $trial_plan_id; 
  7199.         } 
  7200.  
  7201.         $args = $this->get_install_data_for_api( $extra_install_params, false, false ); 
  7202.  
  7203.         // Install the plugin. 
  7204.         $install = $this->get_api_user_scope()->call( 
  7205.             "/plugins/{$this->get_id()}/installs.json",  
  7206.             'post',  
  7207.             $args 
  7208.  ); 
  7209.  
  7210.         if ( ! $this->is_api_result_entity( $install ) ) { 
  7211.             if ( ! empty( $args['license_key'] ) ) { 
  7212.                 // Pass full the fully entered license key to the failure handler. 
  7213.                 $args['license_key'] = $license_key; 
  7214.             } 
  7215.  
  7216.             $install = $this->apply_filters( 'after_install_failure', $install, $args ); 
  7217.  
  7218.             $this->_admin_notices->add( 
  7219.                 sprintf( __fs( 'could-not-activate-x', $this->_slug ), $this->get_plugin_name() ) . ' ' . 
  7220.                 __fs( 'contact-us-with-error-message', $this->_slug ) . ' ' . '<b>' . $install->error->message . '</b>',  
  7221.                 __fs( 'oops', $this->_slug ) . '...',  
  7222.                 'error' 
  7223.  ); 
  7224.  
  7225.             if ( $redirect ) { 
  7226.                 fs_redirect( $this->get_activation_url( array( 'error' => $install->error->message ) ) ); 
  7227.             } 
  7228.  
  7229.             return $install; 
  7230.         } 
  7231.  
  7232.         $site = new FS_Site( $install ); 
  7233.         $this->_site = $site; 
  7234.  
  7235.         return $this->setup_account( $this->_user, $this->_site, $redirect ); 
  7236.     } 
  7237.  
  7238.     /** 
  7239.      * Tries to activate add-on account based on parent plugin info. 
  7240.      * 
  7241.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  7242.      * @since  1.0.6 
  7243.      * 
  7244.      * @param Freemius $parent_fs 
  7245.      */ 
  7246.     private function _activate_addon_account( Freemius $parent_fs ) { 
  7247.         if ( $this->is_registered() ) { 
  7248.             // Already activated. 
  7249.             return; 
  7250.         } 
  7251.  
  7252.         // Activate add-on with parent plugin credentials. 
  7253.         $addon_install = $parent_fs->get_api_site_scope()->call( 
  7254.             "/addons/{$this->_plugin->id}/installs.json",  
  7255.             'post',  
  7256.             $this->get_install_data_for_api( array( 
  7257.                 'uid' => $this->get_anonymous_id(),  
  7258.  ), false, false ) 
  7259.  ); 
  7260.  
  7261.         if ( isset( $addon_install->error ) ) { 
  7262.             $this->_admin_notices->add( 
  7263.                 sprintf( __fs( 'could-not-activate-x', $this->_slug ), $this->get_plugin_name() ) . ' ' . 
  7264.                 __fs( 'contact-us-with-error-message', $this->_slug ) . ' ' . '<b>' . $addon_install->error->message . '</b>',  
  7265.                 __fs( 'oops', $this->_slug ) . '...',  
  7266.                 'error' 
  7267.  ); 
  7268.  
  7269.             return; 
  7270.         } 
  7271.  
  7272.         // First of all, set site info - otherwise we won't 
  7273.         // be able to invoke API calls. 
  7274.         $this->_site = new FS_Site( $addon_install ); 
  7275.  
  7276.         // Sync add-on plans. 
  7277.         $this->_sync_plans(); 
  7278.  
  7279.         // Get site's current plan. 
  7280.         $this->_site->plan = $this->_get_plan_by_id( $this->_site->plan->id ); 
  7281.  
  7282.         // Get user information based on parent's plugin. 
  7283.         $user = $parent_fs->get_user(); 
  7284.  
  7285.         $this->_set_account( $user, $this->_site ); 
  7286.  
  7287.         // Sync licenses. 
  7288.         $this->_sync_licenses(); 
  7289.  
  7290.         // Try to activate premium license. 
  7291.         $this->_activate_license( true ); 
  7292.     } 
  7293.  
  7294.     #endregion 
  7295.  
  7296.     #---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- 
  7297.     #region Admin Menu Items 
  7298.     #---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- 
  7299.  
  7300.     private $_menu_items = array(); 
  7301.  
  7302.     /** 
  7303.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  7304.      * @since  1.0.7 
  7305.      * 
  7306.      * @return string 
  7307.      */ 
  7308.     function get_menu_slug() { 
  7309.         return $this->_menu->get_slug(); 
  7310.     } 
  7311.  
  7312.     /** 
  7313.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  7314.      * @since  1.0.9 
  7315.      */ 
  7316.     function _prepare_admin_menu() { 
  7317. //            if ( ! $this->is_on() ) { 
  7318. //                return; 
  7319. //            } 
  7320.  
  7321.         if ( ! $this->has_api_connectivity() && ! $this->is_enable_anonymous() ) { 
  7322.             $this->_menu->remove_menu_item(); 
  7323.         } else { 
  7324.             $this->do_action( 'before_admin_menu_init' ); 
  7325.  
  7326.             $this->add_menu_action(); 
  7327.             $this->add_submenu_items(); 
  7328.         } 
  7329.     } 
  7330.  
  7331.     /** 
  7332.      * Admin dashboard menu items modifications. 
  7333.      * 
  7334.      * NOTE: admin_menu action executed before admin_init. 
  7335.      * 
  7336.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  7337.      * @since  1.0.7 
  7338.      * 
  7339.      */ 
  7340.     private function add_menu_action() { 
  7341.         if ( $this->is_activation_mode() ) { 
  7342.             $this->override_plugin_menu_with_activation(); 
  7343.         } else { 
  7344.             // If not registered try to install user. 
  7345.             if ( ! $this->is_registered() && 
  7346.                  fs_request_is_action( $this->_slug . '_activate_new' ) 
  7347.  ) { 
  7348.                 $this->_install_with_new_user(); 
  7349.             } 
  7350.         } 
  7351.     } 
  7352.  
  7353.     /** 
  7354.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  7355.      * @since  1.0.1 
  7356.      */ 
  7357.     function _redirect_on_clicked_menu_link() { 
  7358.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  7359.  
  7360.         $page = strtolower( isset( $_REQUEST['page'] ) ? $_REQUEST['page'] : '' ); 
  7361.  
  7362.         $this->_logger->log( 'page = ' . $page ); 
  7363.  
  7364.         foreach ( $this->_menu_items as $priority => $items ) { 
  7365.             foreach ( $items as $item ) { 
  7366.                 if ( isset( $item['url'] ) ) { 
  7367.                     if ( $page === $this->_menu->get_slug( strtolower( $item['menu_slug'] ) ) ) { 
  7368.                         $this->_logger->log( 'Redirecting to ' . $item['url'] ); 
  7369.  
  7370.                         fs_redirect( $item['url'] ); 
  7371.                     } 
  7372.                 } 
  7373.             } 
  7374.         } 
  7375.     } 
  7376.  
  7377.     /** 
  7378.      * Remove plugin's all admin menu items & pages, and replace with activation page. 
  7379.      * 
  7380.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  7381.      * @since  1.0.1 
  7382.      */ 
  7383.     private function override_plugin_menu_with_activation() { 
  7384.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  7385.  
  7386.         $hook = false; 
  7387.  
  7388.         if ( $this->_menu->is_top_level() ) { 
  7389.             $hook = $this->_menu->override_menu_item( array( &$this, '_connect_page_render' ) ); 
  7390.  
  7391.             if ( false === $hook ) { 
  7392.                 // Create new menu item just for the opt-in. 
  7393.                 $hook = add_menu_page( 
  7394.                     $this->get_plugin_name(),  
  7395.                     $this->get_plugin_name(),  
  7396.                     'manage_options',  
  7397.                     $this->_menu->get_slug(),  
  7398.                     array( &$this, '_connect_page_render' ) 
  7399.  ); 
  7400.             } 
  7401.         } else { 
  7402.             $menus = array( $this->_menu->get_parent_slug() ); 
  7403.  
  7404.             if ( $this->_menu->is_override_exact() ) { 
  7405.                 // Make sure the current page is matching the activation page. 
  7406.                 $activation_url = strtolower( $this->get_activation_url() ); 
  7407.                 $request_url = strtolower( $_SERVER['REQUEST_URI'] ); 
  7408.  
  7409.                 if ( parse_url( $activation_url, PHP_URL_PATH ) !== parse_url( $request_url, PHP_URL_PATH ) ) { 
  7410.                     // Different path - DO NOT OVERRIDE PAGE. 
  7411.                     return; 
  7412.                 } 
  7413.  
  7414.                 $activation_url_params = array(); 
  7415.                 parse_str( parse_url( $activation_url, PHP_URL_QUERY ), $activation_url_params ); 
  7416.  
  7417.                 $request_url_params = array(); 
  7418.                 parse_str( parse_url( $request_url, PHP_URL_QUERY ), $request_url_params ); 
  7419.  
  7420.  
  7421.                 foreach ( $activation_url_params as $key => $val ) { 
  7422.                     if ( ! isset( $request_url_params[ $key ] ) || $val != $request_url_params[ $key ] ) { 
  7423.                         // Not matching query string - DO NOT OVERRIDE PAGE. 
  7424.                         return; 
  7425.                     } 
  7426.                 } 
  7427.             } 
  7428.  
  7429.             foreach ( $menus as $parent_slug ) { 
  7430.                 $hook = $this->_menu->override_submenu_action( 
  7431.                     $parent_slug,  
  7432.                     $this->_menu->get_raw_slug(),  
  7433.                     array( &$this, '_connect_page_render' ) 
  7434.  ); 
  7435.  
  7436.                 if ( false !== $hook ) { 
  7437.                     // Found plugin's submenu item. 
  7438.                     break; 
  7439.                 } 
  7440.             } 
  7441.         } 
  7442.  
  7443.         if ( $this->_menu->is_activation_page() ) { 
  7444.             // Clean admin page from distracting content. 
  7445.             self::_clean_admin_content_section(); 
  7446.         } 
  7447.  
  7448.         if ( false !== $hook ) { 
  7449.             if ( fs_request_is_action( $this->_slug . '_activate_existing' ) ) { 
  7450.                 add_action( "load-$hook", array( &$this, '_install_with_current_user' ) ); 
  7451.             } else if ( fs_request_is_action( $this->_slug . '_activate_new' ) ) { 
  7452.                 add_action( "load-$hook", array( &$this, '_install_with_new_user' ) ); 
  7453.             } 
  7454.         } 
  7455.     } 
  7456.  
  7457.     /** 
  7458.      * @author Leo Fajardo (leorw) 
  7459.      * @since  1.2.1 
  7460.      * 
  7461.      * return string 
  7462.      */ 
  7463.     function get_top_level_menu_capability() { 
  7464.         global $menu; 
  7465.  
  7466.         $top_level_menu_slug = $this->get_top_level_menu_slug(); 
  7467.  
  7468.         foreach ( $menu as $menu_info ) { 
  7469.             /** 
  7470.              * The second element in the menu info array is the capability/role that has access to the menu and the 
  7471.              * third element is the menu slug. 
  7472.              */ 
  7473.             if ( $menu_info[2] === $top_level_menu_slug ) { 
  7474.                 return $menu_info[1]; 
  7475.             } 
  7476.         } 
  7477.  
  7478.         return 'read'; 
  7479.     } 
  7480.  
  7481.     /** 
  7482.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  7483.      * @since  1.0.0 
  7484.      * 
  7485.      * @return string 
  7486.      */ 
  7487.     private function get_top_level_menu_slug() { 
  7488.         return ( $this->is_addon() ? 
  7489.             $this->get_parent_instance()->_menu->get_top_level_menu_slug() : 
  7490.             $this->_menu->get_top_level_menu_slug() ); 
  7491.     } 
  7492.  
  7493.     /** 
  7494.      * Add default Freemius menu items. 
  7495.      * 
  7496.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  7497.      * @since  1.0.0 
  7498.      */ 
  7499.     private function add_submenu_items() { 
  7500.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  7501.  
  7502.         if ( ! $this->is_addon() ) { 
  7503.             if ( ! $this->is_activation_mode() ) { 
  7504.                 if ( $this->is_registered() ) { 
  7505.                     // Add user account page. 
  7506.                     $this->add_submenu_item( 
  7507.                         __fs( 'account', $this->_slug ),  
  7508.                         array( &$this, '_account_page_render' ),  
  7509.                         $this->get_plugin_name() . ' – ' . __fs( 'account', $this->_slug ),  
  7510.                         'manage_options',  
  7511.                         'account',  
  7512.                         array( &$this, '_account_page_load' ),  
  7513.                         WP_FS__DEFAULT_PRIORITY,  
  7514.                         $this->_menu->is_submenu_item_visible( 'account' ) 
  7515.  ); 
  7516.                 } 
  7517.  
  7518.                 // Add contact page. 
  7519.                 $this->add_submenu_item( 
  7520.                     __fs( 'contact-us', $this->_slug ),  
  7521.                     array( &$this, '_contact_page_render' ),  
  7522.                     $this->get_plugin_name() . ' – ' . __fs( 'contact-us', $this->_slug ),  
  7523.                     'manage_options',  
  7524.                     'contact',  
  7525.                     'Freemius::_clean_admin_content_section',  
  7526.                     WP_FS__DEFAULT_PRIORITY,  
  7527.                     $this->_menu->is_submenu_item_visible( 'contact' ) 
  7528.  ); 
  7529.  
  7530.                 if ( $this->has_addons() ) { 
  7531.                     $this->add_submenu_item( 
  7532.                         __fs( 'add-ons', $this->_slug ),  
  7533.                         array( &$this, '_addons_page_render' ),  
  7534.                         $this->get_plugin_name() . ' – ' . __fs( 'add-ons', $this->_slug ),  
  7535.                         'manage_options',  
  7536.                         'addons',  
  7537.                         array( &$this, '_addons_page_load' ),  
  7538.                         WP_FS__LOWEST_PRIORITY - 1,  
  7539.                         $this->_menu->is_submenu_item_visible( 'addons' ) 
  7540.  ); 
  7541.                 } 
  7542.  
  7543.                 $show_pricing = ( $this->has_paid_plan() && $this->_menu->is_submenu_item_visible( 'pricing' ) ); 
  7544.                 // If user don't have paid plans, add pricing page 
  7545.                 // to support add-ons checkout but don't add the submenu item. 
  7546.                 // || (isset( $_GET['page'] ) && $this->_menu->get_slug( 'pricing' ) == $_GET['page']); 
  7547.  
  7548.                 $pricing_cta_slug = 'upgrade'; 
  7549.                 $pricing_class = 'upgrade-mode'; 
  7550.                 if ( $show_pricing ) { 
  7551.                     if ( $this->_admin_notices->has_sticky( 'trial_promotion' ) && 
  7552.                          ! $this->is_paying_or_trial() 
  7553.  ) { 
  7554.                         // If running a trial promotion, modify the pricing to load the trial. 
  7555.                         $pricing_cta_slug = 'start-trial'; 
  7556.                         $pricing_class = 'trial-mode'; 
  7557.                     } else if ( $this->is_paying() ) { 
  7558.                         $pricing_cta_slug = 'pricing'; 
  7559.                         $pricing_class = ''; 
  7560.                     } 
  7561.                 } 
  7562.  
  7563.                 // Add upgrade/pricing page. 
  7564.                 $this->add_submenu_item( 
  7565.                     __fs( $pricing_cta_slug, $this->_slug ) . '  ➤',  
  7566.                     array( &$this, '_pricing_page_render' ),  
  7567.                     $this->get_plugin_name() . ' – ' . __fs( 'pricing', $this->_slug ),  
  7568.                     'manage_options',  
  7569.                     'pricing',  
  7570.                     'Freemius::_clean_admin_content_section',  
  7571.                     WP_FS__LOWEST_PRIORITY,  
  7572.                     $show_pricing,  
  7573.                     $pricing_class 
  7574.  ); 
  7575.             } 
  7576.         } 
  7577.  
  7578.  
  7579.         if ( 0 < count( $this->_menu_items ) ) { 
  7580.             if ( ! $this->_menu->is_top_level() ) { 
  7581.                 fs_enqueue_local_style( 'fs_common', '/admin/common.css' ); 
  7582.  
  7583.                 // Append submenu items right after the plugin's submenu item. 
  7584.                 $this->order_sub_submenu_items(); 
  7585.             } else { 
  7586.                 // Append submenu items. 
  7587.                 $this->embed_submenu_items(); 
  7588.             } 
  7589.         } 
  7590.     } 
  7591.  
  7592.     /** 
  7593.      * Moved the actual submenu item additions to a separated function,  
  7594.      * in order to support sub-submenu items when the plugin's settings 
  7595.      * only have a submenu and not top-level menu item. 
  7596.      * 
  7597.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  7598.      * @since  1.1.4 
  7599.      */ 
  7600.     private function embed_submenu_items() { 
  7601.         $item_template = $this->_menu->is_top_level() ? 
  7602.             '<span class="fs-submenu-item %s %s %s">%s</span>' : 
  7603.             '<span class="fs-submenu-item fs-sub %s %s %s">%s</span>'; 
  7604.  
  7605.         $top_level_menu_capability = $this->get_top_level_menu_capability(); 
  7606.  
  7607.         ksort( $this->_menu_items ); 
  7608.  
  7609.         foreach ( $this->_menu_items as $priority => $items ) { 
  7610.             foreach ( $items as $item ) { 
  7611.                 $capability = ( ! empty( $item['capability'] ) ? $item['capability'] : $top_level_menu_capability ); 
  7612.  
  7613.                 $menu_item = sprintf( 
  7614.                     $item_template,  
  7615.                     $this->_slug,  
  7616.                     $item['menu_slug'],  
  7617.                     ! empty( $item['class'] ) ? $item['class'] : '',  
  7618.                     $item['menu_title'] 
  7619.  ); 
  7620.  
  7621.                 $menu_slug = $this->_menu->get_slug( $item['menu_slug'] ); 
  7622.  
  7623.                 if ( ! isset( $item['url'] ) ) { 
  7624.                     $hook = add_submenu_page( 
  7625.                         $item['show_submenu'] ? 
  7626.                             $this->get_top_level_menu_slug() : 
  7627.                             null,  
  7628.                         $item['page_title'],  
  7629.                         $menu_item,  
  7630.                         $capability,  
  7631.                         $menu_slug,  
  7632.                         $item['render_function'] 
  7633.  ); 
  7634.  
  7635.                     if ( false !== $item['before_render_function'] ) { 
  7636.                         add_action( "load-$hook", $item['before_render_function'] ); 
  7637.                     } 
  7638.                 } else { 
  7639.                     add_submenu_page( 
  7640.                         $this->get_top_level_menu_slug(),  
  7641.                         $item['page_title'],  
  7642.                         $menu_item,  
  7643.                         $capability,  
  7644.                         $menu_slug,  
  7645.                         array( $this, '' ) 
  7646.  ); 
  7647.                 } 
  7648.             } 
  7649.         } 
  7650.     } 
  7651.  
  7652.     /** 
  7653.      * Re-order the submenu items so all Freemius added new submenu items 
  7654.      * are added right after the plugin's settings submenu item. 
  7655.      * 
  7656.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  7657.      * @since  1.1.4 
  7658.      */ 
  7659.     private function order_sub_submenu_items() { 
  7660.         global $submenu; 
  7661.  
  7662.         $menu_slug = $this->_menu->get_top_level_menu_slug(); 
  7663.  
  7664.         /** 
  7665.          * Before "admin_menu" fires, WordPress will loop over the default submenus and remove pages for which the user 
  7666.          * does not have permissions. So in case a plugin does not have top-level menu but does have submenus under any 
  7667.          * of the default menus, only users that have the right role can access its sub-submenus (Account, Contact Us,  
  7668.          * Support Forum, etc.) since $submenu[ $menu_slug ] will be empty if the user doesn't have permission. 
  7669.          * 
  7670.          * In case a plugin does not have submenus under any of the default menus but does have submenus under the menu 
  7671.          * of another plugin, only users that have the right role can access its sub-submenus since we will use the 
  7672.          * capability needed to access the parent menu as the capability for the submenus that we will add. 
  7673.          */ 
  7674.         if ( empty( $submenu[ $menu_slug ] ) ) { 
  7675.             return; 
  7676.         } 
  7677.  
  7678.         $top_level_menu = &$submenu[ $menu_slug ]; 
  7679.  
  7680.         $all_submenu_items_after = array(); 
  7681.  
  7682.         $found_submenu_item = false; 
  7683.  
  7684.         foreach ( $top_level_menu as $submenu_id => $meta ) { 
  7685.             if ( $found_submenu_item ) { 
  7686.                 // Remove all submenu items after the plugin's submenu item. 
  7687.                 $all_submenu_items_after[] = $meta; 
  7688.                 unset( $top_level_menu[ $submenu_id ] ); 
  7689.             } 
  7690.  
  7691.             if ( $this->_menu->get_raw_slug() === $meta[2] ) { 
  7692.                 // Found the submenu item, put all below. 
  7693.                 $found_submenu_item = true; 
  7694.                 continue; 
  7695.             } 
  7696.         } 
  7697.  
  7698.         // Embed all plugin's new submenu items. 
  7699.         $this->embed_submenu_items(); 
  7700.  
  7701.         // Start with specially high number to make sure it's appended. 
  7702.         $i = max( 10000, max( array_keys( $top_level_menu ) ) + 1 ); 
  7703.         foreach ( $all_submenu_items_after as $meta ) { 
  7704.             $top_level_menu[ $i ] = $meta; 
  7705.             $i ++; 
  7706.         } 
  7707.  
  7708.         // Sort submenu items. 
  7709.         ksort( $top_level_menu ); 
  7710.     } 
  7711.  
  7712.     /** 
  7713.      * Displays the Support Forum link when enabled. 
  7714.      * 
  7715.      * Can be filtered like so: 
  7716.      * 
  7717.      *  function _fs_show_support_menu( $is_visible, $menu_id ) { 
  7718.      *      if ( 'support' === $menu_id ) { 
  7719.      *            return _fs->is_registered(); 
  7720.      *        } 
  7721.      *        return $is_visible; 
  7722.      *    } 
  7723.      *    _fs()->add_filter('is_submenu_visible', '_fs_show_support_menu', 10, 2); 
  7724.      * 
  7725.      */ 
  7726.     function _add_default_submenu_items() { 
  7727.         if ( ! $this->is_on() ) { 
  7728.             return; 
  7729.         } 
  7730.  
  7731.         if ( ! $this->is_activation_mode() ) { 
  7732.             if ( $this->_menu->is_submenu_item_visible( 'support' ) ) { 
  7733.                 $this->add_submenu_link_item( 
  7734.                     $this->apply_filters( 'support_forum_submenu', __fs( 'support-forum', $this->_slug ) ),  
  7735.                     $this->apply_filters( 'support_forum_url', 'https://wordpress.org/support/plugin/' . $this->_slug ),  
  7736.                     'wp-support-forum',  
  7737.                     null,  
  7738.                     50 
  7739.  ); 
  7740.             } 
  7741.         } 
  7742.     } 
  7743.  
  7744.     /** 
  7745.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  7746.      * @since  1.0.1 
  7747.      * 
  7748.      * @param string        $menu_title 
  7749.      * @param callable      $render_function 
  7750.      * @param bool|string   $page_title 
  7751.      * @param string        $capability 
  7752.      * @param bool|string   $menu_slug 
  7753.      * @param bool|callable $before_render_function 
  7754.      * @param int           $priority 
  7755.      * @param bool          $show_submenu 
  7756.      * @param string        $class Since 1.2.1.5 can add custom classes to menu items. 
  7757.      */ 
  7758.     function add_submenu_item( 
  7759.         $menu_title,  
  7760.         $render_function,  
  7761.         $page_title = false,  
  7762.         $capability = 'manage_options',  
  7763.         $menu_slug = false,  
  7764.         $before_render_function = false,  
  7765.         $priority = WP_FS__DEFAULT_PRIORITY,  
  7766.         $show_submenu = true,  
  7767.         $class = '' 
  7768.  ) { 
  7769.         $this->_logger->entrance( 'Title = ' . $menu_title ); 
  7770.  
  7771.         if ( $this->is_addon() ) { 
  7772.             $parent_fs = $this->get_parent_instance(); 
  7773.  
  7774.             if ( is_object( $parent_fs ) ) { 
  7775.                 $parent_fs->add_submenu_item( 
  7776.                     $menu_title,  
  7777.                     $render_function,  
  7778.                     $page_title,  
  7779.                     $capability,  
  7780.                     $menu_slug,  
  7781.                     $before_render_function,  
  7782.                     $priority,  
  7783.                     $show_submenu,  
  7784.                     $class 
  7785.  ); 
  7786.  
  7787.                 return; 
  7788.             } 
  7789.         } 
  7790.  
  7791.         if ( ! isset( $this->_menu_items[ $priority ] ) ) { 
  7792.             $this->_menu_items[ $priority ] = array(); 
  7793.         } 
  7794.  
  7795.         $this->_menu_items[ $priority ][] = array( 
  7796.             'page_title' => is_string( $page_title ) ? $page_title : $menu_title,  
  7797.             'menu_title' => $menu_title,  
  7798.             'capability' => $capability,  
  7799.             'menu_slug' => is_string( $menu_slug ) ? $menu_slug : strtolower( $menu_title ),  
  7800.             'render_function' => $render_function,  
  7801.             'before_render_function' => $before_render_function,  
  7802.             'show_submenu' => $show_submenu,  
  7803.             'class' => $class,  
  7804.  ); 
  7805.     } 
  7806.  
  7807.     /** 
  7808.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  7809.      * @since  1.0.1 
  7810.      * 
  7811.      * @param string $menu_title 
  7812.      * @param string $url 
  7813.      * @param bool   $menu_slug 
  7814.      * @param string $capability 
  7815.      * @param int    $priority 
  7816.      * 
  7817.      */ 
  7818.     function add_submenu_link_item( 
  7819.         $menu_title,  
  7820.         $url,  
  7821.         $menu_slug = false,  
  7822.         $capability = 'read',  
  7823.         $priority = WP_FS__DEFAULT_PRIORITY 
  7824.  ) { 
  7825.         $this->_logger->entrance( 'Title = ' . $menu_title . '; Url = ' . $url ); 
  7826.  
  7827.         if ( $this->is_addon() ) { 
  7828.             $parent_fs = $this->get_parent_instance(); 
  7829.  
  7830.             if ( is_object( $parent_fs ) ) { 
  7831.                 $parent_fs->add_submenu_link_item( 
  7832.                     $menu_title,  
  7833.                     $url,  
  7834.                     $menu_slug,  
  7835.                     $capability,  
  7836.                     $priority 
  7837.  ); 
  7838.  
  7839.                 return; 
  7840.             } 
  7841.         } 
  7842.  
  7843.         if ( ! isset( $this->_menu_items[ $priority ] ) ) { 
  7844.             $this->_menu_items[ $priority ] = array(); 
  7845.         } 
  7846.  
  7847.         $this->_menu_items[ $priority ][] = array( 
  7848.             'menu_title' => $menu_title,  
  7849.             'capability' => $capability,  
  7850.             'menu_slug' => is_string( $menu_slug ) ? $menu_slug : strtolower( $menu_title ),  
  7851.             'url' => $url,  
  7852.             'page_title' => $menu_title,  
  7853.             'render_function' => 'fs_dummy',  
  7854.             'before_render_function' => '',  
  7855.  ); 
  7856.     } 
  7857.  
  7858.     #endregion ------------------------------------------------------------------ 
  7859.  
  7860.     /** Actions / Hooks / Filters 
  7861.     ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------*/ 
  7862.     /** 
  7863.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  7864.      * @since  1.1.7 
  7865.      * 
  7866.      * @param string $tag 
  7867.      * 
  7868.      * @return string 
  7869.      */ 
  7870.     public function get_action_tag( $tag ) { 
  7871.         return "fs_{$tag}_{$this->_slug}"; 
  7872.     } 
  7873.  
  7874.     /** 
  7875.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  7876.      * @since  1.2.1 
  7877.      * 
  7878.      * @param string $tag 
  7879.      * 
  7880.      * @return string 
  7881.      */ 
  7882.     private function get_ajax_action_tag( $tag ) { 
  7883.         return 'wp_ajax_' . $this->get_action_tag( $tag ); 
  7884.     } 
  7885.  
  7886.     /** 
  7887.      * Do action, specific for the current context plugin. 
  7888.      * 
  7889.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  7890.      * @since  1.0.1 
  7891.      * 
  7892.      * @param string $tag     The name of the action to be executed. 
  7893.      * @param mixed  $arg, ... Optional. Additional arguments which are passed on to the 
  7894.      *                        functions hooked to the action. Default empty. 
  7895.      * 
  7896.      * @uses   do_action() 
  7897.      */ 
  7898.     function do_action( $tag, $arg = '' ) { 
  7899.         $this->_logger->entrance( $tag ); 
  7900.  
  7901.         $args = func_get_args(); 
  7902.  
  7903.         call_user_func_array( 'do_action', array_merge( 
  7904.                 array( $this->get_action_tag( $tag ) ),  
  7905.                 array_slice( $args, 1 ) ) 
  7906.  ); 
  7907.     } 
  7908.  
  7909.     /** 
  7910.      * Add action, specific for the current context plugin. 
  7911.      * 
  7912.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  7913.      * @since  1.0.1 
  7914.      * 
  7915.      * @param string   $tag 
  7916.      * @param callable $function_to_add 
  7917.      * @param int      $priority 
  7918.      * @param int      $accepted_args 
  7919.      * 
  7920.      * @uses   add_action() 
  7921.      */ 
  7922.     function add_action( $tag, $function_to_add, $priority = WP_FS__DEFAULT_PRIORITY, $accepted_args = 1 ) { 
  7923.         $this->_logger->entrance( $tag ); 
  7924.  
  7925.         add_action( $this->get_action_tag( $tag ), $function_to_add, $priority, $accepted_args ); 
  7926.     } 
  7927.  
  7928.     /** 
  7929.      * Add AJAX action, specific for the current context plugin. 
  7930.      * 
  7931.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  7932.      * @since  1.2.1 
  7933.      * 
  7934.      * @param string   $tag 
  7935.      * @param callable $function_to_add 
  7936.      * @param int      $priority 
  7937.      * @param int      $accepted_args 
  7938.      * 
  7939.      * @uses   add_action() 
  7940.      * 
  7941.      * @return bool True if action added, false if no need to add the action since the AJAX call isn't matching. 
  7942.      */ 
  7943.     function add_ajax_action( $tag, $function_to_add, $priority = WP_FS__DEFAULT_PRIORITY, $accepted_args = 1 ) { 
  7944.         $this->_logger->entrance( $tag ); 
  7945.  
  7946.         if ( ! $this->is_ajax_action( $tag ) ) { 
  7947.             return false; 
  7948.         } 
  7949.  
  7950.         add_action( $this->get_ajax_action_tag( $tag ), $function_to_add, $priority, $accepted_args ); 
  7951.  
  7952.         $this->_logger->info( "$tag AJAX callback action added." ); 
  7953.  
  7954.         return true; 
  7955.     } 
  7956.  
  7957.     /** 
  7958.      * Send a JSON response back to an Ajax request. 
  7959.      * 
  7960.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  7961.      * @since  1.2.1.5 
  7962.      * 
  7963.      * @param mixed $response 
  7964.      */ 
  7965.     function shoot_ajax_response( $response ) { 
  7966.         wp_send_json( $response ); 
  7967.     } 
  7968.  
  7969.     /** 
  7970.      * Send a JSON response back to an Ajax request, indicating success. 
  7971.      * 
  7972.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  7973.      * @since  1.2.1.5 
  7974.      * 
  7975.      * @param mixed $data Data to encode as JSON, then print and exit. 
  7976.      */ 
  7977.     function shoot_ajax_success( $data = null ) { 
  7978.         wp_send_json_success( $data ); 
  7979.     } 
  7980.  
  7981.     /** 
  7982.      * Send a JSON response back to an Ajax request, indicating failure. 
  7983.      * 
  7984.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  7985.      * @since  1.2.1.5 
  7986.      * 
  7987.      * @param mixed $error Optional error message. 
  7988.      */ 
  7989.     function shoot_ajax_failure( $error = '' ) { 
  7990.         $result = array( 'success' => false ); 
  7991.         if ( ! empty( $error ) ) { 
  7992.             $result['error'] = $error; 
  7993.         } 
  7994.  
  7995.         wp_send_json( $result ); 
  7996.     } 
  7997.  
  7998.     /** 
  7999.      * Apply filter, specific for the current context plugin. 
  8000.      * 
  8001.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  8002.      * @since  1.0.9 
  8003.      * 
  8004.      * @param string $tag   The name of the filter hook. 
  8005.      * @param mixed  $value The value on which the filters hooked to `$tag` are applied on. 
  8006.      * 
  8007.      * @return mixed The filtered value after all hooked functions are applied to it. 
  8008.      * 
  8009.      * @uses   apply_filters() 
  8010.      */ 
  8011.     function apply_filters( $tag, $value ) { 
  8012.         $this->_logger->entrance( $tag ); 
  8013.  
  8014.         $args = func_get_args(); 
  8015.         array_unshift( $args, $this->_slug ); 
  8016.  
  8017.         return call_user_func_array( 'fs_apply_filter', $args ); 
  8018.     } 
  8019.  
  8020.     /** 
  8021.      * Add filter, specific for the current context plugin. 
  8022.      * 
  8023.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  8024.      * @since  1.0.9 
  8025.      * 
  8026.      * @param string   $tag 
  8027.      * @param callable $function_to_add 
  8028.      * @param int      $priority 
  8029.      * @param int      $accepted_args 
  8030.      * 
  8031.      * @uses   add_filter() 
  8032.      */ 
  8033.     function add_filter( $tag, $function_to_add, $priority = WP_FS__DEFAULT_PRIORITY, $accepted_args = 1 ) { 
  8034.         $this->_logger->entrance( $tag ); 
  8035.  
  8036.         add_filter( $this->get_action_tag( $tag ), $function_to_add, $priority, $accepted_args ); 
  8037.     } 
  8038.  
  8039.     /** 
  8040.      * Check if has filter. 
  8041.      * 
  8042.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  8043.      * @since  1.1.4 
  8044.      * 
  8045.      * @param string        $tag 
  8046.      * @param callable|bool $function_to_check Optional. The callback to check for. Default false. 
  8047.      * 
  8048.      * @return false|int 
  8049.      * 
  8050.      * @uses   has_filter() 
  8051.      */ 
  8052.     function has_filter( $tag, $function_to_check = false ) { 
  8053.         $this->_logger->entrance( $tag ); 
  8054.  
  8055.         return has_filter( $this->get_action_tag( $tag ), $function_to_check ); 
  8056.     }

  8074.     /** 
  8075.      * Update site information. 
  8076.      * 
  8077.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  8078.      * @since  1.0.1 
  8079.      * 
  8080.      * @param bool $store Flush to Database if true. 
  8081.      */ 
  8082.     private function _store_site( $store = true ) { 
  8083.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  8084.  
  8085.         if ( empty( $this->_site->id ) ) { 
  8086.             $this->_logger->error( "Empty install ID, can't store site." ); 
  8087.  
  8088.             return; 
  8089.         } 
  8090.  
  8091.         $encrypted_site = clone $this->_site; 
  8092.         $encrypted_site->plan = $this->_encrypt_entity( $this->_site->plan ); 
  8093.  
  8094.         $sites = self::get_all_sites(); 
  8095.         $sites[ $this->_slug ] = $encrypted_site; 
  8096.         self::$_accounts->set_option( 'sites', $sites, $store ); 
  8097.     } 
  8098.  
  8099.     /** 
  8100.      * Update plugin's plans information. 
  8101.      * 
  8102.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  8103.      * @since  1.0.2 
  8104.      * 
  8105.      * @param bool $store Flush to Database if true. 
  8106.      */ 
  8107.     private function _store_plans( $store = true ) { 
  8108.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  8109.  
  8110.         $plans = self::get_all_plans(); 
  8111.  
  8112.         // Copy plans. 
  8113.         $encrypted_plans = array(); 
  8114.         for ( $i = 0, $len = count( $this->_plans ); $i < $len; $i ++ ) { 
  8115.             $encrypted_plans[] = $this->_encrypt_entity( $this->_plans[ $i ] ); 
  8116.         } 
  8117.  
  8118.         $plans[ $this->_slug ] = $encrypted_plans; 
  8119.         self::$_accounts->set_option( 'plans', $plans, $store ); 
  8120.     } 
  8121.  
  8122.     /** 
  8123.      * Update user's plugin licenses. 
  8124.      * 
  8125.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  8126.      * @since  1.0.5 
  8127.      * 
  8128.      * @param bool                $store 
  8129.      * @param string|bool         $plugin_slug 
  8130.      * @param FS_Plugin_License[] $licenses 
  8131.      */ 
  8132.     private function _store_licenses( $store = true, $plugin_slug = false, $licenses = array() ) { 
  8133.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  8134.  
  8135.         $all_licenses = self::get_all_licenses(); 
  8136.  
  8137.         if ( ! is_string( $plugin_slug ) ) { 
  8138.             $plugin_slug = $this->_slug; 
  8139.             $licenses = $this->_licenses; 
  8140.         } 
  8141.  
  8142.         if ( ! isset( $all_licenses[ $plugin_slug ] ) ) { 
  8143.             $all_licenses[ $plugin_slug ] = array(); 
  8144.         } 
  8145.  
  8146.         $all_licenses[ $plugin_slug ][ $this->_user->id ] = $licenses; 
  8147.  
  8148.         self::$_accounts->set_option( 'licenses', $all_licenses, $store ); 
  8149.     }

  8151.     /**

  8159.     private function _store_user( $store = true ) { 
  8160.         $this->_logger->entrance();

  8163.             $this->_logger->error( "Empty user ID, can't store user." ); 
  8164.  
  8165.             return; 
  8166.         } 
  8167.

  8169.         $users[ $this->_user->id ] = $this->_user; 
  8170.         self::$_accounts->set_option( 'users', $users, $store ); 
  8171.     } 
  8172.  
  8173.     /** 
  8174.      * Update new updates information. 
  8175.      * 
  8176.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  8177.      * @since  1.0.4 
  8178.      * 
  8179.      * @param FS_Plugin_Tag|null $update 
  8180.      * @param bool               $store Flush to Database if true. 
  8181.      * @param bool|number        $plugin_id 
  8182.      */ 
  8183.     private function _store_update( $update, $store = true, $plugin_id = false ) { 
  8184.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  8185.  
  8186.         if ( $update instanceof FS_Plugin_Tag ) { 
  8187.             $update->updated = time(); 
  8188.         } 
  8189.  
  8190.         if ( ! is_numeric( $plugin_id ) ) { 
  8191.             $plugin_id = $this->_plugin->id; 
  8192.         } 
  8193.  
  8194.         $updates = self::get_all_updates(); 
  8195.         $updates[ $plugin_id ] = $update; 
  8196.         self::$_accounts->set_option( 'updates', $updates, $store ); 
  8197.     } 
  8198.  
  8199.     /** 
  8200.      * Update new updates information.

  8216.     /**

  8218.      * 
  8219.      * @author   Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  8220.      * @since    1.0.8 
  8221.      * 
  8222.      * @param bool $store 
  8223.      * 
  8224.      * @return bool 
  8225.      */ 
  8226.     private function _delete_account_addons( $store = true ) { 
  8227.         $all_addons = self::get_all_account_addons(); 
  8228.  
  8229.         if ( ! isset( $all_addons[ $this->_plugin->id ] ) ) { 
  8230.             return false; 
  8231.         } 
  8232.  
  8233.         unset( $all_addons[ $this->_plugin->id ] ); 
  8234.  
  8235.         self::$_accounts->set_option( 'account_addons', $all_addons, $store ); 
  8236.  
  8237.         return true;

  8257.     /**

  8261.      * @since  1.0.1 
  8262.      */ 
  8263.     private function _store_account() { 
  8264.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  8265.  
  8266.         $this->_store_site( false ); 
  8267.         $this->_store_user( false ); 
  8268.         $this->_store_plans( false ); 
  8269.         $this->_store_licenses( false );
