  8273.  
  8274.     /** 
  8275.      * Sync user's information. 
  8276.      * 
  8277.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  8278.      * @since  1.0.3 
  8279.      * @uses   FS_Api 
  8280.      */ 
  8281.     private function _handle_account_user_sync() { 
  8282.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  8283.  
  8284.         $api = $this->get_api_user_scope(); 
  8285.  
  8286.         // Get user's information. 
  8287.         $user = $api->get( '/', true ); 
  8288.  
  8289.         if ( isset( $user->id ) ) { 
  8290.             $this->_user->first = $user->first; 
  8291.             $this->_user->last = $user->last; 
  8292.             $this->_user->email = $user->email; 
  8293.  
  8294.             $is_menu_item_account_visible = $this->_menu->is_submenu_item_visible( 'account' ); 
  8295.  
  8296.             if ( $user->is_verified && 
  8297.                  ( ! isset( $this->_user->is_verified ) || false === $this->_user->is_verified ) 
  8298.  ) { 
  8299.                 $this->_user->is_verified = true; 
  8300.  
  8301.                 $this->do_action( 'account_email_verified', $user->email ); 
  8302.  
  8303.                 $this->_admin_notices->add( 
  8304.                     __fs( 'email-verified-message', $this->_slug ),  
  8305.                     __fs( 'right-on', $this->_slug ) . '!',  
  8306.                     'success',  
  8307.                     // Make admin sticky if account menu item is invisible,  
  8308.                     // since the page will be auto redirected to the plugin's 
  8309.                     // main settings page, and the non-sticky message 
  8310.                     // will disappear. 
  8311.                     ! $is_menu_item_account_visible,  
  8312.                     false,  
  8313.                     'email_verified' 
  8314.  ); 
  8315.             } 
  8316.  
  8317.             // Flush user details to DB. 
  8318.             $this->_store_user(); 
  8319.  
  8320.             $this->do_action( 'after_account_user_sync', $user ); 
  8321.  
  8322.             /** 
  8323.              * If account menu item is hidden, redirect to plugin's main settings page. 
  8324.              * 
  8325.              * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  8326.              * @since  1.1.6 
  8327.              * 
  8328.              * @link   https://github.com/Freemius/wordpress-sdk/issues/6 
  8329.              */ 
  8330.             if ( ! $is_menu_item_account_visible ) { 
  8331.                 fs_redirect( $this->_get_admin_page_url() ); 
  8332.             } 
  8333.         } 
  8334.     } 
  8335.  
  8336.     /** 
  8337.      * @param bool $store 
  8338.      * 
  8339.      * @return FS_Plugin_Plan|object|false 
  8340.      */ 
  8341.     private function _enrich_site_plan( $store = true ) { 
  8342.         // Try to load plan from local cache. 
  8343.         $plan = $this->_get_plan_by_id( $this->_site->plan->id ); 
  8344.  
  8345.         if ( false === $plan ) { 
  8346.             $plan = $this->_fetch_site_plan(); 
  8347.         } 
  8348.  
  8349.         if ( $plan instanceof FS_Plugin_Plan ) { 
  8350.             $this->_update_plan( $plan, $store ); 
  8351.         } 
  8352.  
  8353.         return $plan; 
  8354.     } 
  8355.  
  8356.     /** 
  8357.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  8358.      * @since  1.0.9 
  8359.      * @uses   FS_Api 
  8360.      * 
  8361.      * @param bool $store 
  8362.      * 
  8363.      * @return FS_Plugin_Plan|object|false 
  8364.      */ 
  8365.     private function _enrich_site_trial_plan( $store = true ) { 
  8366.         // Try to load plan from local cache. 
  8367.         $trial_plan = $this->_get_plan_by_id( $this->_site->trial_plan_id ); 
  8368.  
  8369.         if ( false === $trial_plan ) { 
  8370.             $trial_plan = $this->_fetch_site_plan( $this->_site->trial_plan_id ); 
  8371.         } 
  8372.  
  8373.         if ( $trial_plan instanceof FS_Plugin_Plan ) { 
  8374.             $this->_storage->store( 'trial_plan', $trial_plan, $store ); 
  8375.         } 
  8376.  
  8377.         return $trial_plan; 
  8378.     } 
  8379.  
  8380.     /** 
  8381.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  8382.      * @since  1.0.9 
  8383.      * @uses   FS_Api 
  8384.      * 
  8385.      * @param number|bool $license_id 
  8386.      * 
  8387.      * @return FS_Subscription|object|bool 
  8388.      */ 
  8389.     private function _fetch_site_license_subscription( $license_id = false ) { 
  8390.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  8391.         $api = $this->get_api_site_scope(); 
  8392.  
  8393.         if ( ! is_numeric( $license_id ) ) { 
  8394.             $license_id = $this->_license->id; 
  8395.         } 
  8396.  
  8397.         $result = $api->get( "/licenses/{$license_id}/subscriptions.json", true ); 
  8398.  
  8399.         return ! isset( $result->error ) ? 
  8400.             ( ( is_array( $result->subscriptions ) && 0 < count( $result->subscriptions ) ) ? 
  8401.                 new FS_Subscription( $result->subscriptions[0] ) : 
  8402.                 false 
  8403.  ) : 
  8404.             $result; 
  8405.     } 
  8406.  
  8407.     /** 
  8408.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  8409.      * @since  1.0.4 
  8410.      * @uses   FS_Api 
  8411.      * 
  8412.      * @param number|bool $plan_id 
  8413.      * 
  8414.      * @return FS_Plugin_Plan|object 
  8415.      */ 
  8416.     private function _fetch_site_plan( $plan_id = false ) { 
  8417.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  8418.         $api = $this->get_api_site_scope(); 
  8419.  
  8420.         if ( ! is_numeric( $plan_id ) ) { 
  8421.             $plan_id = $this->_site->plan->id; 
  8422.         } 
  8423.  
  8424.         $plan = $api->get( "/plans/{$plan_id}.json", true ); 
  8425.  
  8426.         return ! isset( $plan->error ) ? new FS_Plugin_Plan( $plan ) : $plan; 
  8427.     } 
  8428.  
  8429.     /** 
  8430.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  8431.      * @since  1.0.5 
  8432.      * @uses   FS_Api 
  8433.      * 
  8434.      * @return FS_Plugin_Plan[]|object 
  8435.      */ 
  8436.     private function _fetch_plugin_plans() { 
  8437.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  8438.         $api = $this->get_api_site_scope(); 
  8439.  
  8440.         $result = $api->get( '/plans.json', true ); 
  8441.  
  8442.         if ( $this->is_api_result_object( $result, 'plans' ) && is_array( $result->plans ) ) { 
  8443.             for ( $i = 0, $len = count( $result->plans ); $i < $len; $i ++ ) { 
  8444.                 $result->plans[ $i ] = new FS_Plugin_Plan( $result->plans[ $i ] ); 
  8445.             } 
  8446.  
  8447.             $result = $result->plans; 
  8448.         } 
  8449.  
  8450.         return $result; 
  8451.     } 
  8452.  
  8453.     /** 
  8454.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  8455.      * @since  1.0.5 
  8456.      * @uses   FS_Api 
  8457.      * 
  8458.      * @param number|bool $plugin_id 
  8459.      * @param number|bool $site_license_id 
  8460.      * 
  8461.      * @return FS_Plugin_License[]|object 
  8462.      */ 
  8463.     private function _fetch_licenses( $plugin_id = false, $site_license_id = false ) { 
  8464.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  8465.  
  8466.         $api = $this->get_api_user_scope(); 
  8467.  
  8468.         if ( ! is_numeric( $plugin_id ) ) { 
  8469.             $plugin_id = $this->_plugin->id; 
  8470.         } 
  8471.  
  8472.         $result = $api->get( "/plugins/{$plugin_id}/licenses.json", true ); 
  8473.  
  8474.         $is_site_license_synced = false; 
  8475.  
  8476.         $api_errors = array(); 
  8477.  
  8478.         if ( $this->is_api_result_object( $result, 'licenses' ) && 
  8479.              is_array( $result->licenses ) 
  8480.  ) { 
  8481.             for ( $i = 0, $len = count( $result->licenses ); $i < $len; $i ++ ) { 
  8482.                 $result->licenses[ $i ] = new FS_Plugin_License( $result->licenses[ $i ] ); 
  8483.  
  8484.                 if ( ( ! $is_site_license_synced ) && is_numeric( $site_license_id ) ) { 
  8485.                     $is_site_license_synced = ( $site_license_id == $result->licenses[ $i ]->id ); 
  8486.                 } 
  8487.             } 
  8488.  
  8489.             $result = $result->licenses; 
  8490.         } else { 
  8491.             $api_errors[] = $result; 
  8492.             $result = array(); 
  8493.         } 
  8494.  
  8495.         if ( ! $is_site_license_synced ) { 
  8496.             $api = $this->get_api_site_scope(); 
  8497.  
  8498.             if ( is_numeric( $site_license_id ) ) { 
  8499.                 // Try to retrieve a foreign license that is linked to the install. 
  8500.                 $api_result = $api->call( '/licenses.json' ); 
  8501.  
  8502.                 if ( $this->is_api_result_object( $api_result, 'licenses' ) && 
  8503.                      is_array( $api_result->licenses ) 
  8504.  ) { 
  8505.                     $licenses = $api_result->licenses; 
  8506.  
  8507.                     if ( ! empty( $licenses ) ) { 
  8508.                         $result[] = new FS_Plugin_License( $licenses[0] ); 
  8509.                     } 
  8510.                 } else { 
  8511.                     $api_errors[] = $api_result; 
  8512.                 } 
  8513.             } else if ( is_object( $this->_license ) ) { 
  8514.                 // Fetch foreign license by ID and license key. 
  8515.                 $license = $api->get( "/licenses/{$this->_license->id}.json?license_key=" . 
  8516.                                       urlencode( $this->_license->secret_key ) ); 
  8517.  
  8518.                 if ( $this->is_api_result_entity( $license ) ) { 
  8519.                     $result[] = new FS_Plugin_License( $license ); 
  8520.                 } else { 
  8521.                     $api_errors[] = $license; 
  8522.                 } 
  8523.             } 
  8524.         } 
  8525.  
  8526.         if ( is_array( $result ) && 0 < count( $result ) ) { 
  8527.             // If found at least one license, return license collection even if there are errors. 
  8528.             return $result; 
  8529.         } 
  8530.  
  8531.         if ( ! empty( $api_errors ) ) { 
  8532.             // If found any errors and no licenses, return first error. 
  8533.             return $api_errors[0]; 
  8534.         } 
  8535.  
  8536.         // Fallback to empty licenses list. 
  8537.         return $result; 
  8538.     } 
  8539.  
  8540.     /** 
  8541.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  8542.      * @since  1.2.0 
  8543.      * @uses   FS_Api 
  8544.      * 
  8545.      * @param number|bool $plugin_id 
  8546.      * 
  8547.      * @return FS_Payment[]|object 
  8548.      */ 
  8549.     function _fetch_payments( $plugin_id = false ) { 
  8550.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  8551.  
  8552.         $api = $this->get_api_user_scope(); 
  8553.  
  8554.         if ( ! is_numeric( $plugin_id ) ) { 
  8555.             $plugin_id = $this->_plugin->id; 
  8556.         } 
  8557.  
  8558.         $result = $api->get( "/plugins/{$plugin_id}/payments.json", true ); 
  8559.  
  8560.         if ( ! isset( $result->error ) ) { 
  8561.             for ( $i = 0, $len = count( $result->payments ); $i < $len; $i ++ ) { 
  8562.                 $result->payments[ $i ] = new FS_Payment( $result->payments[ $i ] ); 
  8563.             } 
  8564.             $result = $result->payments; 
  8565.         } 
  8566.  
  8567.         return $result; 
  8568.     } 
  8569.  
  8570.     /** 
  8571.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  8572.      * @since  1.2.1.5 
  8573.      * @uses   FS_Api 
  8574.      * 
  8575.      * @return \FS_Billing|mixed 
  8576.      */ 
  8577.     function _fetch_billing() { 
  8578.         require_once WP_FS__DIR_INCLUDES . '/entities/class-fs-billing.php'; 
  8579.  
  8580.         $billing = $this->get_api_user_scope()->call( 'billing.json' ); 
  8581.  
  8582.         if ( $this->is_api_result_entity( $billing ) ) { 
  8583.             $billing = new FS_Billing( $billing ); 
  8584.         } 
  8585.  
  8586.         return $billing; 
  8587.     } 
  8588.  
  8589.     /** 
  8590.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  8591.      * @since  1.0.4 
  8592.      * 
  8593.      * @param FS_Plugin_Plan $plan 
  8594.      * @param bool           $store 
  8595.      */ 
  8596.     private function _update_plan( $plan, $store = false ) { 
  8597.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  8598.  
  8599.         $this->_site->plan = $plan; 
  8600.         $this->_store_site( $store ); 
  8601.     } 
  8602.  
  8603.     /** 
  8604.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  8605.      * @since  1.0.5 
  8606.      * 
  8607.      * @param FS_Plugin_License[] $licenses 
  8608.      * @param string|bool         $plugin_slug 
  8609.      */ 
  8610.     private function _update_licenses( $licenses, $plugin_slug = false ) { 
  8611.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  8612.  
  8613.         if ( is_array( $licenses ) ) { 
  8614.             for ( $i = 0, $len = count( $licenses ); $i < $len; $i ++ ) { 
  8615.                 $licenses[ $i ]->updated = time(); 
  8616.             } 
  8617.         } 
  8618.  
  8619.         if ( ! is_string( $plugin_slug ) ) { 
  8620.             $this->_licenses = $licenses; 
  8621.         } 
  8622.  
  8623.         $this->_store_licenses( true, $plugin_slug, $licenses ); 
  8624.     } 
  8625.  
  8626.     /** 
  8627.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  8628.      * @since  1.0.4 
  8629.      * 
  8630.      * @param bool|number $plugin_id 
  8631.      * @param bool        $flush Since 1.1.7.3 
  8632.      * 
  8633.      * @return object|false New plugin tag info if exist. 
  8634.      */ 
  8635.     private function _fetch_newer_version( $plugin_id = false, $flush = true ) { 
  8636.         $latest_tag = $this->_fetch_latest_version( $plugin_id, $flush ); 
  8637.  
  8638.         if ( ! is_object( $latest_tag ) ) { 
  8639.             return false; 
  8640.         } 
  8641.  
  8642.         // Check if version is actually newer. 
  8643.         $has_new_version = 
  8644.             // If it's an non-installed add-on then always return latest. 
  8645.             ( $this->_is_addon_id( $plugin_id ) && ! $this->is_addon_activated( $plugin_id ) ) || 
  8646.             // Compare versions. 
  8647.             version_compare( $this->get_plugin_version(), $latest_tag->version, '<' ); 
  8648.  
  8649.         $this->_logger->departure( $has_new_version ? 'Found newer plugin version ' . $latest_tag->version : 'No new version' ); 
  8650.  
  8651.         return $has_new_version ? $latest_tag : false; 
  8652.     } 
  8653.  
  8654.     /** 
  8655.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  8656.      * @since  1.0.5 
  8657.      * 
  8658.      * @param bool|number $plugin_id 
  8659.      * @param bool        $flush Since 1.1.7.3 
  8660.      * 
  8661.      * @return bool|FS_Plugin_Tag 
  8662.      */ 
  8663.     function get_update( $plugin_id = false, $flush = true ) { 
  8664.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  8665.  
  8666.         if ( ! is_numeric( $plugin_id ) ) { 
  8667.             $plugin_id = $this->_plugin->id; 
  8668.         } 
  8669.  
  8670.         $this->_check_updates( true, $plugin_id, $flush ); 
  8671.         $updates = $this->get_all_updates(); 
  8672.  
  8673.         return isset( $updates[ $plugin_id ] ) && is_object( $updates[ $plugin_id ] ) ? $updates[ $plugin_id ] : false; 
  8674.     } 
  8675.  
  8676.     /** 
  8677.      * Check if site assigned with active license. 
  8678.      * 
  8679.      * @author     Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  8680.      * @since      1.0.6 
  8681.      * 
  8682.      * @deprecated Please use has_active_valid_license() instead because license can be cancelled. 
  8683.      */ 
  8684.     function has_active_license() { 
  8685.         return ( 
  8686.             is_object( $this->_license ) && 
  8687.             is_numeric( $this->_license->id ) && 
  8688.             ! $this->_license->is_expired() 
  8689.  ); 
  8690.     } 
  8691.  
  8692.     /** 
  8693.      * Check if site assigned with active & valid (not expired) license. 
  8694.      * 
  8695.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  8696.      * @since  1.2.1 
  8697.      */ 
  8698.     function has_active_valid_license() { 
  8699.         return ( 
  8700.             is_object( $this->_license ) && 
  8701.             is_numeric( $this->_license->id ) && 
  8702.             $this->_license->is_active() && 
  8703.             $this->_license->is_valid() 
  8704.  ); 
  8705.     } 
  8706.  
  8707.     /** 
  8708.      * Check if site assigned with license with enabled features. 
  8709.      * 
  8710.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  8711.      * @since  1.0.6 
  8712.      * 
  8713.      * @return bool 
  8714.      */ 
  8715.     function has_features_enabled_license() { 
  8716.         return ( 
  8717.             is_object( $this->_license ) && 
  8718.             is_numeric( $this->_license->id ) && 
  8719.             $this->_license->is_features_enabled() 
  8720.  ); 
  8721.     } 
  8722.  
  8723.     /** 
  8724.      * Check if user is a trial or have feature enabled license. 
  8725.      * 
  8726.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  8727.      * @since  1.1.7 
  8728.      * 
  8729.      * @return bool 
  8730.      */ 
  8731.     function can_use_premium_code() { 
  8732.         return $this->is_trial() || $this->has_features_enabled_license(); 
  8733.     } 
  8734.  
  8735.     /** 
  8736.      * Sync site's plan. 
  8737.      * 
  8738.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  8739.      * @since  1.0.3 
  8740.      * 
  8741.      * @uses   FS_Api 
  8742.      * 
  8743.      * @param bool $background Hints the method if it's a background sync. If false, it means that was initiated by 
  8744.      *                         the admin. 
  8745.      */ 
  8746.     private function _sync_license( $background = false ) { 
  8747.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  8748.  
  8749.         $plugin_id = fs_request_get( 'plugin_id', $this->get_id() ); 
  8750.  
  8751.         $is_addon_sync = ( ! $this->_plugin->is_addon() && $plugin_id != $this->get_id() ); 
  8752.  
  8753.         if ( $is_addon_sync ) { 
  8754.             $this->_sync_addon_license( $plugin_id, $background ); 
  8755.         } else { 
  8756.             $this->_sync_plugin_license( $background ); 
  8757.         } 
  8758.  
  8759.         $this->do_action( 'after_account_plan_sync', $this->_site->plan->name ); 
  8760.     } 
  8761.  
  8762.     /** 
  8763.      * Sync plugin's add-on license. 
  8764.      * 
  8765.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  8766.      * @since  1.0.6 
  8767.      * @uses   FS_Api 
  8768.      * 
  8769.      * @param number $addon_id 
  8770.      * @param bool   $background 
  8771.      */ 
  8772.     private function _sync_addon_license( $addon_id, $background ) { 
  8773.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  8774.  
  8775.         if ( $this->is_addon_activated( $addon_id ) ) { 
  8776.             // If already installed, use add-on sync. 
  8777.             $fs_addon = self::get_instance_by_id( $addon_id ); 
  8778.             $fs_addon->_sync_license( $background ); 
  8779.  
  8780.             return; 
  8781.         } 
  8782.  
  8783.         // Validate add-on exists. 
  8784.         $addon = $this->get_addon( $addon_id ); 
  8785.  
  8786.         if ( ! is_object( $addon ) ) { 
  8787.             return; 
  8788.         } 
  8789.  
  8790.         // Add add-on into account add-ons. 
  8791.         $account_addons = $this->get_account_addons(); 
  8792.         if ( ! is_array( $account_addons ) ) { 
  8793.             $account_addons = array(); 
  8794.         } 
  8795.         $account_addons[] = $addon->id; 
  8796.         $account_addons = array_unique( $account_addons ); 
  8797.         $this->_store_account_addons( $account_addons ); 
  8798.  
  8799.         // Load add-on licenses. 
  8800.         $licenses = $this->_fetch_licenses( $addon->id ); 
  8801.  
  8802.         // Sync add-on licenses. 
  8803.         if ( $this->is_array_instanceof( $licenses, 'FS_Plugin_License' ) ) { 
  8804.             $this->_update_licenses( $licenses, $addon->slug ); 
  8805.  
  8806.             if ( ! $this->is_addon_installed( $addon->slug ) && FS_License_Manager::has_premium_license( $licenses ) ) { 
  8807.                 $plans_result = $this->get_api_site_or_plugin_scope()->get( "/addons/{$addon_id}/plans.json" ); 
  8808.  
  8809.                 if ( ! isset( $plans_result->error ) ) { 
  8810.                     $plans = array(); 
  8811.                     foreach ( $plans_result->plans as $plan ) { 
  8812.                         $plans[] = new FS_Plugin_Plan( $plan ); 
  8813.                     } 
  8814.  
  8815.                     $this->_admin_notices->add_sticky( 
  8816.                         FS_Plan_Manager::instance()->has_free_plan( $plans ) ? 
  8817.                             sprintf( 
  8818.                                 __fs( 'addon-successfully-upgraded-message', $this->_slug ),  
  8819.                                 $addon->title 
  8820.  ) . ' ' . $this->_get_latest_download_link( 
  8821.                                 __fs( 'download-latest-version', $this->_slug ),  
  8822.                                 $addon_id 
  8823.  ) 
  8824.                             : 
  8825.                             sprintf( 
  8826.                                 __fs( 'addon-successfully-purchased-message', $this->_slug ),  
  8827.                                 $addon->title 
  8828.  ) . ' ' . $this->_get_latest_download_link( 
  8829.                                 __fs( 'download-latest-version', $this->_slug ),  
  8830.                                 $addon_id 
  8831.  ),  
  8832.                         'addon_plan_upgraded_' . $addon->slug,  
  8833.                         __fs( 'yee-haw', $this->_slug ) . '!' 
  8834.  ); 
  8835.                 } 
  8836.             } 
  8837.         } 
  8838.     } 
  8839.  
  8840.     /** 
  8841.      * Sync site's plugin plan. 
  8842.      * 
  8843.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  8844.      * @since  1.0.6 
  8845.      * @uses   FS_Api 
  8846.      * 
  8847.      * @param bool $background Hints the method if it's a background sync. If false, it means that was initiated by 
  8848.      *                         the admin. 
  8849.      */ 
  8850.     private function _sync_plugin_license( $background = false ) { 
  8851.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  8852.  
  8853.         /** 
  8854.          * Sync site info. 
  8855.          * 
  8856.          * @todo This line will execute install sync on a daily basis, even if running the free version (for opted-in users). The reason we want to keep it that way is for cases when the user was a paying customer, then there was a failure in subscription payment, and then after some time the payment was successful. This could be heavily optimized. For example, we can skip the $flush if the current install was never associated with a paid version. 
  8857.          */ 
  8858.         $site = $this->send_install_update( array(), true ); 
  8859.  
  8860.         $plan_change = 'none'; 
  8861.  
  8862.         if ( ! $this->is_api_result_entity( $site ) ) { 
  8863.             // Show API messages only if not background sync or if paying customer. 
  8864.             if ( ! $background || $this->is_paying() ) { 
  8865.                 // Try to ping API to see if not blocked. 
  8866.                 if ( ! FS_Api::test() ) { 
  8867.                     /** 
  8868.                      * Failed to ping API - blocked! 
  8869.                      * 
  8870.                      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  8871.                      * @since  1.1.6 Only show message related to one of the Freemius powered plugins. Once it will be resolved it will fix the issue for all plugins anyways. There's no point to scare users with multiple error messages. 
  8872.                      */ 
  8873.                     $api = $this->get_api_site_scope(); 
  8874.  
  8875.                     if ( ! self::$_global_admin_notices->has_sticky( 'api_blocked' ) ) { 
  8876.                         self::$_global_admin_notices->add( 
  8877.                             sprintf( 
  8878.                                 __fs( 'server-blocking-access', $this->_slug ),  
  8879.                                 $this->get_plugin_name(),  
  8880.                                 '<a href="' . $api->get_url() . '" target="_blank">' . $api->get_url() . '</a>' 
  8881.  ) . '<br> ' . __fs( 'server-error-message', $this->_slug ) . var_export( $site->error, true ),  
  8882.                             __fs( 'oops', $this->_slug ) . '...',  
  8883.                             'error',  
  8884.                             $background,  
  8885.                             false,  
  8886.                             'api_blocked' 
  8887.  ); 
  8888.                     } 
  8889.                 } else { 
  8890.                     // Authentication params are broken. 
  8891.                     $this->_admin_notices->add( 
  8892.                         __fs( 'wrong-authentication-param-message', $this->_slug ),  
  8893.                         __fs( 'oops', $this->_slug ) . '...',  
  8894.                         'error' 
  8895.  ); 
  8896.                 } 
  8897.             } 
  8898.  
  8899.             // No reason to continue with license sync while there are API issues. 
  8900.             return; 
  8901.         } 
  8902.  
  8903.         // Remove sticky API connectivity message. 
  8904.         self::$_global_admin_notices->remove_sticky( 'api_blocked' ); 
  8905.  
  8906.         $site = new FS_Site( $site ); 
  8907.  
  8908.         // Sync plans. 
  8909.         $this->_sync_plans(); 
  8910.  
  8911.         if ( ! $this->has_paid_plan() ) { 
  8912.             $this->_site = $site; 
  8913.             $this->_enrich_site_plan( true ); 
  8914.             $this->_store_site(); 
  8915.         } else { 
  8916.             /** 
  8917.              * Sync licenses. Pass the site's license ID so that the foreign licenses will be fetched if the license 
  8918.              * associated with that ID is not included in the user's licenses collection. 
  8919.              */ 
  8920.             $this->_sync_licenses( $site->license_id ); 
  8921.  
  8922.             // Check if plan / license changed. 
  8923.             if ( ! FS_Entity::equals( $site->plan, $this->_site->plan ) || 
  8924.                  // Check if trial started. 
  8925.                  $site->trial_plan_id != $this->_site->trial_plan_id || 
  8926.                  $site->trial_ends != $this->_site->trial_ends || 
  8927.                  // Check if license changed. 
  8928.                  $site->license_id != $this->_site->license_id 
  8929.  ) { 
  8930.                 if ( $site->is_trial() && ( ! $this->_site->is_trial() || $site->trial_ends != $this->_site->trial_ends ) ) { 
  8931.                     // New trial started. 
  8932.                     $this->_site = $site; 
  8933.                     $plan_change = 'trial_started'; 
  8934.  
  8935.                     // Store trial plan information. 
  8936.                     $this->_enrich_site_trial_plan( true ); 
  8937.  
  8938.                     // For trial with subscription use-case. 
  8939.                     $new_license = is_null( $site->license_id ) ? null : $this->_get_license_by_id( $site->license_id ); 
  8940.  
  8941.                     if ( is_object( $new_license ) && $new_license->is_valid() ) { 
  8942.                         $this->_site = $site; 
  8943.                         $this->_update_site_license( $new_license ); 
  8944.                         $this->_store_licenses(); 
  8945.                         $this->_enrich_site_plan( true ); 
  8946.  
  8947.                         $this->_sync_site_subscription( $this->_license ); 
  8948.                     } 
  8949.                 } else if ( $this->_site->is_trial() && ! $site->is_trial() && ! is_numeric( $site->license_id ) ) { 
  8950.                     // Was in trial, but now trial expired and no license ID. 
  8951.                     // New trial started. 
  8952.                     $this->_site = $site; 
  8953.                     $plan_change = 'trial_expired'; 
  8954.  
  8955.                     // Clear trial plan information. 
  8956.                     $this->_storage->trial_plan = null; 
  8957.  
  8958.                 } else { 
  8959.                     $is_free = $this->is_free_plan(); 
  8960.  
  8961.                     // Make sure license exist and not expired. 
  8962.                     $new_license = is_null( $site->license_id ) ? 
  8963.                         null : 
  8964.                         $this->_get_license_by_id( $site->license_id ); 
  8965.  
  8966.                     if ( $is_free && is_null( $new_license ) && $this->has_any_license() && $this->_license->is_cancelled ) { 
  8967.                         // License cancelled. 
  8968.                         $this->_site = $site; 
  8969.                         $this->_update_site_license( $new_license ); 
  8970.                         $this->_store_licenses(); 
  8971.                         $this->_enrich_site_plan( true ); 
  8972.  
  8973.                         $plan_change = 'cancelled'; 
  8974.                     } else if ( $is_free && ( ( ! is_object( $new_license ) || $new_license->is_expired() ) ) ) { 
  8975.                         // The license is expired, so ignore upgrade method. 
  8976.                     } else { 
  8977.                         // License changed. 
  8978.                         $this->_site = $site; 
  8979.                         $this->_update_site_license( $new_license ); 
  8980.                         $this->_store_licenses(); 
  8981.                         $this->_enrich_site_plan( true ); 
  8982.  
  8983.                         $plan_change = $is_free ? 
  8984.                             'upgraded' : 
  8985.                             ( is_object( $new_license ) ? 
  8986.                                 'changed' : 
  8987.                                 'downgraded' ); 
  8988.                     } 
  8989.                 } 
  8990.  
  8991.                 // Store updated site info. 
  8992.                 $this->_store_site(); 
  8993.             } else { 
  8994.                 if ( is_object( $this->_license ) && $this->_license->is_expired() ) { 
  8995.                     if ( ! $this->has_features_enabled_license() ) { 
  8996.                         $this->_deactivate_license(); 
  8997.                         $plan_change = 'downgraded'; 
  8998.                     } else { 
  8999.                         $plan_change = 'expired'; 
  9000.                     } 
  9001.                 } 
  9002.  
  9003.                 if ( is_numeric( $site->license_id ) && is_object( $this->_license ) ) { 
  9004.                     $this->_sync_site_subscription( $this->_license ); 
  9005.                 } 
  9006.             } 
  9007.         } 
  9008.  
  9009.         if ( $this->has_paid_plan() ) { 
  9010.             switch ( $plan_change ) { 
  9011.                 case 'none': 
  9012.                     if ( ! $background && is_admin() ) { 
  9013.                         $plan = $this->is_trial() ? 
  9014.                             $this->_storage->trial_plan : 
  9015.                             $this->_site->plan; 
  9016.  
  9017.                         $this->_admin_notices->add( 
  9018.                             sprintf( 
  9019.                                 __fs( 'plan-did-not-change-message', $this->_slug ),  
  9020.                                 '<i><b>' . $plan->title . ( $this->is_trial() ? ' ' . __fs( 'trial', $this->_slug ) : '' ) . '</b></i>' 
  9021.  ) . ' ' . sprintf( 
  9022.                                 '<a href="%s">%s</a>',  
  9023.                                 $this->contact_url( 
  9024.                                     'bug',  
  9025.                                     sprintf( __fs( 'plan-did-not-change-email-message', $this->_slug ),  
  9026.                                         strtoupper( $plan->name ) 
  9027.  ) 
  9028.  ),  
  9029.                                 __fs( 'contact-us-here', $this->_slug ) 
  9030.  ),  
  9031.                             __fs( 'hmm', $this->_slug ) . '...' 
  9032.  ); 
  9033.                     } 
  9034.                     break; 
  9035.                 case 'upgraded': 
  9036.                     $this->_admin_notices->add_sticky( 
  9037.                         sprintf( 
  9038.                             __fs( 'plan-upgraded-message', $this->_slug ),  
  9039.                             '<i>' . $this->get_plugin_name() . '</i>' 
  9040.  ) . $this->get_complete_upgrade_instructions(),  
  9041.                         'plan_upgraded',  
  9042.                         __fs( 'yee-haw', $this->_slug ) . '!' 
  9043.  ); 
  9044.  
  9045.                     $this->_admin_notices->remove_sticky( array( 
  9046.                         'trial_started',  
  9047.                         'trial_promotion',  
  9048.                         'trial_expired',  
  9049.                         'activation_complete',  
  9050.  ) ); 
  9051.                     break; 
  9052.                 case 'changed': 
  9053.                     $this->_admin_notices->add_sticky( 
  9054.                         sprintf( 
  9055.                             __fs( 'plan-changed-to-x-message', $this->_slug ),  
  9056.                             $this->_site->plan->title 
  9057.  ),  
  9058.                         'plan_changed' 
  9059.  ); 
  9060.  
  9061.                     $this->_admin_notices->remove_sticky( array( 
  9062.                         'trial_started',  
  9063.                         'trial_promotion',  
  9064.                         'trial_expired',  
  9065.                         'activation_complete',  
  9066.  ) ); 
  9067.                     break; 
  9068.                 case 'downgraded': 
  9069.                     $this->_admin_notices->add_sticky( 
  9070.                         sprintf( __fs( 'license-expired-blocking-message', $this->_slug ) ),  
  9071.                         'license_expired',  
  9072.                         __fs( 'hmm', $this->_slug ) . '...' 
  9073.  ); 
  9074.                     $this->_admin_notices->remove_sticky( 'plan_upgraded' ); 
  9075.                     break; 
  9076.                 case 'cancelled': 
  9077.                     $this->_admin_notices->add( 
  9078.                         __fs( 'license-cancelled', $this->_slug ) . ' ' . 
  9079.                         sprintf( 
  9080.                             '<a href="%s">%s</a>',  
  9081.                             $this->contact_url( 'bug' ),  
  9082.                             __fs( 'contact-us-here', $this->_slug ) 
  9083.  ),  
  9084.                         __fs( 'hmm', $this->_slug ) . '...',  
  9085.                         'error' 
  9086.  ); 
  9087.                     $this->_admin_notices->remove_sticky( 'plan_upgraded' ); 
  9088.                     break; 
  9089.                 case 'expired': 
  9090.                     $this->_admin_notices->add_sticky( 
  9091.                         sprintf( __fs( 'license-expired-non-blocking-message', $this->_slug ), $this->_site->plan->title ),  
  9092.                         'license_expired',  
  9093.                         __fs( 'hmm', $this->_slug ) . '...' 
  9094.  ); 
  9095.                     $this->_admin_notices->remove_sticky( 'plan_upgraded' ); 
  9096.                     break; 
  9097.                 case 'trial_started': 
  9098.                     $this->_admin_notices->add_sticky( 
  9099.                         sprintf( 
  9100.                             __fs( 'trial-started-message', $this->_slug ),  
  9101.                             '<i>' . $this->get_plugin_name() . '</i>' 
  9102.  ) . $this->get_complete_upgrade_instructions( $this->_storage->trial_plan->title ),  
  9103.                         'trial_started',  
  9104.                         __fs( 'yee-haw', $this->_slug ) . '!' 
  9105.  ); 
  9106.  
  9107.                     $this->_admin_notices->remove_sticky( array( 
  9108.                         'trial_promotion',  
  9109.  ) ); 
  9110.                     break; 
  9111.                 case 'trial_expired': 
  9112.                     $this->_admin_notices->add_sticky( 
  9113.                         __fs( 'trial-expired-message', $this->_slug ),  
  9114.                         'trial_expired',  
  9115.                         __fs( 'hmm', $this->_slug ) . '...' 
  9116.  ); 
  9117.                     $this->_admin_notices->remove_sticky( array( 
  9118.                         'trial_started',  
  9119.                         'trial_promotion',  
  9120.                         'plan_upgraded',  
  9121.  ) ); 
  9122.                     break; 
  9123.             } 
  9124.         } 
  9125.  
  9126.         if ( 'none' !== $plan_change ) { 
  9127.             $this->do_action( 'after_license_change', $plan_change, $this->_site->plan ); 
  9128.         } 
  9129.     } 
  9130.  
  9131.     /** 
  9132.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  9133.      * @since  1.0.5 
  9134.      * 
  9135.      * @param bool $background 
  9136.      */ 
  9137.     protected function _activate_license( $background = false ) { 
  9138.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  9139.  
  9140.         $license_id = fs_request_get( 'license_id' ); 
  9141.  
  9142.         if ( FS_Plugin_License::is_valid_id( $license_id ) && $license_id == $this->_site->license_id ) { 
  9143.             // License is already activated. 
  9144.             return; 
  9145.         } 
  9146.  
  9147.         $premium_license = FS_Plugin_License::is_valid_id( $license_id ) ? 
  9148.             $this->_get_license_by_id( $license_id ) : 
  9149.             $this->_get_available_premium_license(); 
  9150.  
  9151.         if ( ! is_object( $premium_license ) ) { 
  9152.             return; 
  9153.         } 
  9154.  
  9155.         /** 
  9156.          * If the premium license is already associated with the install, just 
  9157.          * update the license reference (activation is not required). 
  9158.          * 
  9159.          * @since 1.1.9 
  9160.          */ 
  9161.         if ( $premium_license->id == $this->_site->license_id ) { 
  9162.             // License is already activated. 
  9163.             $this->_update_site_license( $premium_license ); 
  9164.             $this->_enrich_site_plan( false ); 
  9165.             $this->_store_account(); 
  9166.  
  9167.             return; 
  9168.         } 
  9169.  
  9170.         if ( $this->_site->user_id != $premium_license->user_id ) { 
  9171.             $api_request_params = array( 'license_key' => $premium_license->secret_key ); 
  9172.         } else { 
  9173.             $api_request_params = array(); 
  9174.         } 
  9175.  
  9176.         $api = $this->get_api_site_scope(); 
  9177.         $license = $api->call( "/licenses/{$premium_license->id}.json", 'put', $api_request_params ); 
  9178.  
  9179.         if ( ! $this->is_api_result_entity( $license ) ) { 
  9180.             if ( ! $background ) { 
  9181.                 $this->_admin_notices->add( sprintf( 
  9182.                     '%s %s',  
  9183.                     __fs( 'license-activation-failed-message', $this->_slug ),  
  9184.                     ( is_object( $license ) && isset( $license->error ) ? 
  9185.                         $license->error->message : 
  9186.                         sprintf( '%s<br><code>%s</code>',  
  9187.                             __fs( 'server-error-message', $this->_slug ),  
  9188.                             var_export( $license, true ) 
  9189.  ) 
  9190.  ) 
  9191.  ),  
  9192.                     __fs( 'hmm', $this->_slug ) . '...',  
  9193.                     'error' 
  9194.  ); 
  9195.             } 
  9196.  
  9197.             return; 
  9198.         } 
  9199.  
  9200.         $premium_license = new FS_Plugin_License( $license ); 
  9201.  
  9202.         // Updated site plan. 
  9203.         $site = $this->get_api_site_scope()->get( '/', true ); 
  9204.         if ( $this->is_api_result_entity( $site ) ) { 
  9205.             $this->_site = new FS_Site( $site ); 
  9206.         } 
  9207.         $this->_update_site_license( $premium_license ); 
  9208.         $this->_enrich_site_plan( false ); 
  9209.  
  9210.         $this->_store_account(); 
  9211.  
  9212.         if ( ! $background ) { 
  9213.             $this->_admin_notices->add_sticky( 
  9214.                 __fs( 'license-activated-message', $this->_slug ) . 
  9215.                 $this->get_complete_upgrade_instructions(),  
  9216.                 'license_activated',  
  9217.                 __fs( 'yee-haw', $this->_slug ) . '!' 
  9218.  ); 
  9219.         } 
  9220.  
  9221.         $this->_admin_notices->remove_sticky( array( 
  9222.             'trial_promotion',  
  9223.             'license_expired',  
  9224.  ) ); 
  9225.     } 
  9226.  
  9227.     /** 
  9228.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  9229.      * @since  1.0.5 
  9230.      * 
  9231.      * @param bool $show_notice 
  9232.      */ 
  9233.     protected function _deactivate_license( $show_notice = true ) { 
  9234.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  9235.  
  9236.         if ( ! is_object( $this->_license ) ) { 
  9237.             $this->_admin_notices->add( 
  9238.                 sprintf( __fs( 'no-active-license-message', $this->_slug ), $this->_site->plan->title ),  
  9239.                 __fs( 'hmm', $this->_slug ) . '...' 
  9240.  ); 
  9241.  
  9242.             return; 
  9243.         } 
  9244.  
  9245.         $api = $this->get_api_site_scope(); 
  9246.         $license = $api->call( "/licenses/{$this->_site->license_id}.json", 'delete' ); 
  9247.  
  9248.         if ( isset( $license->error ) ) { 
  9249.             $this->_admin_notices->add( 
  9250.                 __fs( 'license-deactivation-failed-message', $this->_slug ) . '<br> ' . 
  9251.                 __fs( 'server-error-message', $this->_slug ) . ' ' . var_export( $license->error, true ),  
  9252.                 __fs( 'hmm', $this->_slug ) . '...',  
  9253.                 'error' 
  9254.  ); 
  9255.  
  9256.             return; 
  9257.         } 
  9258.  
  9259.         // Update license cache. 
  9260.         for ( $i = 0, $len = count( $this->_licenses ); $i < $len; $i ++ ) { 
  9261.             if ( $license->id == $this->_licenses[ $i ]->id ) { 
  9262.                 $this->_licenses[ $i ] = new FS_Plugin_License( $license ); 
  9263.             } 
  9264.         } 
  9265.  
  9266.         // Updated site plan to default. 
  9267.         $this->_sync_plans(); 
  9268.         $this->_site->plan->id = $this->_plans[0]->id; 
  9269.         // Unlink license from site. 
  9270.         $this->_update_site_license( null ); 
  9271.         $this->_enrich_site_plan( false ); 
  9272.  
  9273.         $this->_store_account(); 
  9274.  
  9275.         if ( $show_notice ) { 
  9276.             $this->_admin_notices->add( 
  9277.                 sprintf( __fs( 'license-deactivation-message', $this->_slug ), $this->_site->plan->title ),  
  9278.                 __fs( 'ok', $this->_slug ) 
  9279.  ); 
  9280.         } 
  9281.  
  9282.         $this->_admin_notices->remove_sticky( array( 
  9283.             'plan_upgraded',  
  9284.             'license_activated',  
  9285.  ) ); 
  9286.     } 
  9287.  
  9288.     /** 
  9289.      * Site plan downgrade. 
  9290.      * 
  9291.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  9292.      * @since  1.0.4 
  9293.      * 
  9294.      * @uses   FS_Api 
  9295.      */ 
  9296.     private function _downgrade_site() { 
  9297.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  9298.  
  9299.         $api = $this->get_api_site_scope(); 
  9300.         $site = $api->call( 'downgrade.json', 'put' ); 
  9301.  
  9302.         $plan_downgraded = false; 
  9303.         $plan = false; 
  9304.         if ( $this->is_api_result_entity( $site ) ) { 
  9305.             $prev_plan_id = $this->_site->plan->id; 
  9306.  
  9307.             // Update new site plan id. 
  9308.             $this->_site->plan->id = $site->plan_id; 
  9309.  
  9310.             $plan = $this->_enrich_site_plan(); 
  9311.             $subscription = $this->_sync_site_subscription( $this->_license ); 
  9312.  
  9313.             // Plan downgraded if plan was changed or subscription was cancelled. 
  9314.             $plan_downgraded = ( $plan instanceof FS_Plugin_Plan && $prev_plan_id != $plan->id ) || 
  9315.                                ( is_object( $subscription ) && ! isset( $subscription->error ) && ! $subscription->is_active() ); 
  9316.         } else { 
  9317.             // handle different error cases. 
  9318.  
  9319.         } 
  9320.  
  9321.         if ( $plan_downgraded ) { 
  9322.             // Remove previous sticky message about upgrade (if exist). 
  9323.             $this->_admin_notices->remove_sticky( 'plan_upgraded' ); 
  9324.  
  9325.             $this->_admin_notices->add( 
  9326.                 sprintf( __fs( 'plan-x-downgraded-message', $this->_slug ),  
  9327.                     $plan->title,  
  9328.                     human_time_diff( time(), strtotime( $this->_license->expiration ) ) 
  9329.  ) 
  9330.  ); 
  9331.  
  9332.             // Store site updates. 
  9333.             $this->_store_site(); 
  9334.         } else { 
  9335.             $this->_admin_notices->add( 
  9336.                 __fs( 'plan-downgraded-failure-message', $this->_slug ),  
  9337.                 __fs( 'oops', $this->_slug ) . '...',  
  9338.                 'error' 
  9339.  ); 
  9340.         } 
  9341.     } 
  9342.  
  9343.     /** 
  9344.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  9345.      * @since  1.1.8.1 
  9346.      * 
  9347.      * @param bool|string $plan_name 
  9348.      * 
  9349.      * @return bool If trial was successfully started. 
  9350.      */ 
  9351.     function start_trial( $plan_name = false ) { 
  9352.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  9353.  
  9354.         if ( $this->is_trial() ) { 
  9355.             // Already in trial mode. 
  9356.             $this->_admin_notices->add( 
  9357.                 __fs( 'in-trial-mode', $this->_slug ),  
  9358.                 __fs( 'oops', $this->_slug ) . '...',  
  9359.                 'error' 
  9360.  ); 
  9361.  
  9362.             return false; 
  9363.         } 
  9364.  
  9365.         if ( $this->_site->is_trial_utilized() ) { 
  9366.             // Trial was already utilized. 
  9367.             $this->_admin_notices->add( 
  9368.                 __fs( 'trial-utilized', $this->_slug ),  
  9369.                 __fs( 'oops', $this->_slug ) . '...',  
  9370.                 'error' 
  9371.  ); 
  9372.  
  9373.             return false; 
  9374.         } 
  9375.  
  9376.         if ( false !== $plan_name ) { 
  9377.             $plan = $this->get_plan_by_name( $plan_name ); 
  9378.  
  9379.             if ( false === $plan ) { 
  9380.                 // Plan doesn't exist. 
  9381.                 $this->_admin_notices->add( 
  9382.                     sprintf( __fs( 'trial-plan-x-not-exist', $this->_slug ), $plan_name ),  
  9383.                     __fs( 'oops', $this->_slug ) . '...',  
  9384.                     'error' 
  9385.  ); 
  9386.  
  9387.                 return false; 
  9388.             } 
  9389.  
  9390.             if ( ! $plan->has_trial() ) { 
  9391.                 // Plan doesn't exist. 
  9392.                 $this->_admin_notices->add( 
  9393.                     sprintf( __fs( 'plan-x-no-trial', $this->_slug ), $plan_name ),  
  9394.                     __fs( 'oops', $this->_slug ) . '...',  
  9395.                     'error' 
  9396.  ); 
  9397.  
  9398.                 return false; 
  9399.             } 
  9400.         } else { 
  9401.             if ( ! $this->has_trial_plan() ) { 
  9402.                 // None of the plans have a trial. 
  9403.                 $this->_admin_notices->add( 
  9404.                     __fs( 'no-trials', $this->_slug ),  
  9405.                     __fs( 'oops', $this->_slug ) . '...',  
  9406.                     'error' 
  9407.  ); 
  9408.  
  9409.                 return false; 
  9410.             } 
  9411.  
  9412.             $plans_with_trial = FS_Plan_Manager::instance()->get_trial_plans( $this->_plans ); 
  9413.  
  9414.             $plan = $plans_with_trial[0]; 
  9415.         } 
  9416.  
  9417.         $api = $this->get_api_site_scope(); 
  9418.         $plan = $api->call( "plans/{$plan->id}/trials.json", 'post' ); 
  9419.  
  9420.         if ( ! $this->is_api_result_entity( $plan ) ) { 
  9421.             // Some API error while trying to start the trial. 
  9422.             $this->_admin_notices->add( 
  9423.                 __fs( 'unexpected-api-error', $this->_slug ) . ' ' . var_export( $plan, true ),  
  9424.                 __fs( 'oops', $this->_slug ) . '...',  
  9425.                 'error' 
  9426.  ); 
  9427.  
  9428.             return false; 
  9429.         } 
  9430.  
  9431.         // Sync license. 
  9432.         $this->_sync_license(); 
  9433.  
  9434.         return $this->is_trial(); 
  9435.     } 
  9436.  
  9437.     /** 
  9438.      * Cancel site trial. 
  9439.      * 
  9440.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  9441.      * @since  1.0.9 
  9442.      * 
  9443.      * @uses   FS_Api 
  9444.      */ 
  9445.     private function _cancel_trial() { 
  9446.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  9447.  
  9448.         if ( ! $this->is_trial() ) { 
  9449.             $this->_admin_notices->add( 
  9450.                 __fs( 'trial-cancel-no-trial-message', $this->_slug ),  
  9451.                 __fs( 'oops', $this->_slug ) . '...',  
  9452.                 'error' 
  9453.  ); 
  9454.  
  9455.             return; 
  9456.         } 
  9457.  
  9458.         $api = $this->get_api_site_scope(); 
  9459.         $site = $api->call( 'trials.json', 'delete' ); 
  9460.  
  9461.         $trial_cancelled = false; 
  9462.  
  9463.         if ( $this->is_api_result_entity( $site ) ) { 
  9464.             $prev_trial_ends = $this->_site->trial_ends; 
  9465.  
  9466.             if ( $this->is_paid_trial() ) { 
  9467.                 $this->_license->expiration = $site->trial_ends; 
  9468.                 $this->_license->is_cancelled = true; 
  9469.                 $this->_update_site_license( $this->_license ); 
  9470.                 $this->_store_licenses(); 
  9471.  
  9472.                 // Clear subscription reference. 
  9473.                 $this->_sync_site_subscription( null ); 
  9474.             } 
  9475.  
  9476.             // Update site info. 
  9477.             $this->_site = new FS_Site( $site ); 
  9478.             $this->_enrich_site_plan(); 
  9479.  
  9480.             $trial_cancelled = ( $prev_trial_ends != $site->trial_ends ); 
  9481.         } else { 
  9482.             // handle different error cases. 
  9483.  
  9484.         } 
  9485.  
  9486.         if ( $trial_cancelled ) { 
  9487.             // Remove previous sticky messages about upgrade or trial (if exist). 
  9488.             $this->_admin_notices->remove_sticky( array( 
  9489.                 'trial_started',  
  9490.                 'trial_promotion',  
  9491.                 'plan_upgraded',  
  9492.  ) ); 
  9493.  
  9494.             // Store site updates. 
  9495.             $this->_store_site(); 
  9496.  
  9497.             if ( ! $this->is_addon() || 
  9498.                  ! $this->deactivate_premium_only_addon_without_license( true ) 
  9499.  ) { 
  9500.                 $this->_admin_notices->add( 
  9501.                     sprintf( __fs( 'trial-cancel-message', $this->_slug ), $this->_storage->trial_plan->title ) 
  9502.  ); 
  9503.             } 
  9504.  
  9505.             // Clear trial plan information. 
  9506.             unset( $this->_storage->trial_plan ); 
  9507.         } else { 
  9508.             $this->_admin_notices->add( 
  9509.                 __fs( 'trial-cancel-failure-message', $this->_slug ),  
  9510.                 __fs( 'oops', $this->_slug ) . '...',  
  9511.                 'error' 
  9512.  ); 
  9513.         } 
  9514.     } 
  9515.  
  9516.     /** 
  9517.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  9518.      * @since  1.0.6 
  9519.      * 
  9520.      * @param bool|number $plugin_id 
  9521.      * 
  9522.      * @return bool 
  9523.      */ 
  9524.     private function _is_addon_id( $plugin_id ) { 
  9525.         return is_numeric( $plugin_id ) && ( $this->get_id() != $plugin_id ); 
  9526.     } 
  9527.  
  9528.     /** 
  9529.      * Check if user eligible to download premium version updates. 
  9530.      * 
  9531.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  9532.      * @since  1.0.6 
  9533.      * 
  9534.      * @return bool 
  9535.      */ 
  9536.     private function _can_download_premium() { 
  9537.         return $this->has_active_valid_license() || 
  9538.                ( $this->is_trial() && ! $this->get_trial_plan()->is_free() ); 
  9539.     } 
  9540.  
  9541.     /** 
  9542.      * 
  9543.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  9544.      * @since  1.0.6 
  9545.      * 
  9546.      * @param bool|number $addon_id 
  9547.      * @param string      $type "json" or "zip" 
  9548.      * 
  9549.      * @return string 
  9550.      */ 
  9551.     private function _get_latest_version_endpoint( $addon_id = false, $type = 'json' ) { 
  9552.  
  9553.         $is_addon = $this->_is_addon_id( $addon_id ); 
  9554.  
  9555.         $is_premium = null; 
  9556.         if ( ! $is_addon ) { 
  9557.             $is_premium = $this->_can_download_premium(); 
  9558.         } else if ( $this->is_addon_activated( $addon_id ) ) { 
  9559.             $is_premium = self::get_instance_by_id( $addon_id )->_can_download_premium(); 
  9560.         } 
  9561.  
  9562.         return // If add-on, then append add-on ID. 
  9563.             ( $is_addon ? "/addons/$addon_id" : '' ) . 
  9564.             '/updates/latest.' . $type . 
  9565.             // If add-on and not yet activated, try to fetch based on server licensing. 
  9566.             ( is_bool( $is_premium ) ? '?is_premium=' . json_encode( $is_premium ) : '' ); 
  9567.     } 
  9568.  
  9569.     /** 
  9570.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  9571.      * @since  1.0.4 
  9572.      * 
  9573.      * @param bool|number $addon_id 
  9574.      * @param bool        $flush Since 1.1.7.3 
  9575.      * 
  9576.      * @return object|false Plugin latest tag info. 
  9577.      */ 
  9578.     function _fetch_latest_version( $addon_id = false, $flush = true ) { 
  9579.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  9580.  
  9581.         /** 
  9582.          * @since 1.1.7.3 Check for plugin updates from Freemius only if opted-in. 
  9583.          * @since 1.1.7.4 Also check updates for add-ons. 
  9584.          */ 
  9585.         if ( ! $this->is_registered() && 
  9586.              ! $this->_is_addon_id( $addon_id ) 
  9587.  ) { 
  9588.             return false; 
  9589.         } 
  9590.  
  9591.         $tag = $this->get_api_site_or_plugin_scope()->get( 
  9592.             $this->_get_latest_version_endpoint( $addon_id, 'json' ),  
  9593.             $flush 
  9594.  ); 
  9595.  
  9596.         $latest_version = ( is_object( $tag ) && isset( $tag->version ) ) ? $tag->version : 'couldn\'t get'; 
  9597.  
  9598.         $this->_logger->departure( 'Latest version ' . $latest_version ); 
  9599.  
  9600.         return ( is_object( $tag ) && isset( $tag->version ) ) ? $tag : false; 
  9601.     } 
  9602.  
  9603.     #---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- 
  9604.     #region Download Plugin 
  9605.     #---------------------------------------------------------------------------------- 
  9606.  
  9607.     /** 
  9608.      * Download latest plugin version, based on plan. 
  9609.      * 
  9610.      * Not like _download_latest(), this will redirect the page 
  9611.      * to secure download url to prevent dual download (from FS to WP server,  
  9612.      * and then from WP server to the client / browser). 
  9613.      * 
  9614.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  9615.      * @since  1.0.9 
  9616.      * 
  9617.      * @param bool|number $plugin_id 
  9618.      * 
  9619.      * @uses   FS_Api 
  9620.      * @uses   wp_redirect() 
  9621.      */ 
  9622.     private function _download_latest_directly( $plugin_id = false ) { 
  9623.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  9624.  
  9625.         wp_redirect( $this->_get_latest_download_api_url( $plugin_id ) ); 
  9626.     } 
  9627.  
  9628.     /** 
  9629.      * Get latest plugin FS API download URL. 
  9630.      * 
  9631.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  9632.      * @since  1.0.9 
  9633.      * 
  9634.      * @param bool|number $plugin_id 
  9635.      * 
  9636.      * @return string 
  9637.      */ 
  9638.     private function _get_latest_download_api_url( $plugin_id = false ) { 
  9639.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  9640.  
  9641.         return $this->get_api_site_scope()->get_signed_url( 
  9642.             $this->_get_latest_version_endpoint( $plugin_id, 'zip' ) 
  9643.  ); 
  9644.     } 
  9645.  
  9646.     /** 
  9647.      * Get payment invoice URL. 
  9648.      * 
  9649.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  9650.      * @since  1.2.0 
  9651.      * 
  9652.      * @param bool|number $payment_id 
  9653.      * 
  9654.      * @return string 
  9655.      */ 
  9656.     function _get_invoice_api_url( $payment_id = false ) {

  9658.  
  9659.         return $this->get_api_user_scope()->get_signed_url( 
  9660.             "/payments/{$payment_id}/invoice.pdf" 
  9661.  ); 
  9662.     } 
  9663.  
  9664.     /** 
  9665.      * Get latest plugin download link. 
  9666.      * 
  9667.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  9668.      * @since  1.0.9 
  9669.      * 
  9670.      * @param string      $label 
  9671.      * @param bool|number $plugin_id 
  9672.      * 
  9673.      * @return string 
  9674.      */ 
  9675.     private function _get_latest_download_link( $label, $plugin_id = false ) { 
  9676.         return sprintf( 
  9677.             '<a target="_blank" href="%s">%s</a>',  
  9678.             $this->_get_latest_download_local_url( $plugin_id ),  
  9679.             $label 
  9680.  ); 
  9681.     } 
  9682.  
  9683.     /** 
  9684.      * Get latest plugin download local URL. 
  9685.      * 
  9686.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  9687.      * @since  1.0.9 
  9688.      * 
  9689.      * @param bool|number $plugin_id 
  9690.      * 
  9691.      * @return string 
  9692.      */ 
  9693.     function _get_latest_download_local_url( $plugin_id = false ) { 
  9694.         // Add timestamp to protect from caching. 
  9695.         $params = array( 'ts' => WP_FS__SCRIPT_START_TIME ); 
  9696.  
  9697.         if ( ! empty( $plugin_id ) ) { 
  9698.             $params['plugin_id'] = $plugin_id; 
  9699.         } 
  9700.  
  9701.         return $this->get_account_url( 'download_latest', $params ); 
  9702.     } 
  9703.  
  9704.     #endregion Download Plugin ------------------------------------------------------------------ 
  9705.  
  9706.     /** 
  9707.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  9708.      * @since  1.0.4 
  9709.      * 
  9710.      * @uses   FS_Api 
  9711.      * 
  9712.      * @param bool        $background Hints the method if it's a background updates check. If false, it means that 
  9713.      *                                was initiated by the admin. 
  9714.      * @param bool|number $plugin_id 
  9715.      * @param bool        $flush      Since 1.1.7.3 
  9716.      */ 
  9717.     private function _check_updates( $background = false, $plugin_id = false, $flush = true ) { 
  9718.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  9719.  
  9720.         // Check if there's a newer version for download. 
  9721.         $new_version = $this->_fetch_newer_version( $plugin_id, $flush ); 
  9722.  
  9723.         $update = null; 
  9724.         if ( is_object( $new_version ) ) { 
  9725.             $update = new FS_Plugin_Tag( $new_version ); 
  9726.  
  9727.             if ( ! $background ) { 
  9728.                 $this->_admin_notices->add( 
  9729.                     sprintf( 
  9730.                         __fs( 'version-x-released', $this->_slug ) . ' ' . __fs( 'please-download-x', $this->_slug ),  
  9731.                         $update->version,  
  9732.                         sprintf( 
  9733.                             '<a href="%s" target="_blank">%s</a>',  
  9734.                             $this->get_account_url( 'download_latest' ),  
  9735.                             sprintf( __fs( 'latest-x-version', $this->_slug ), $this->_site->plan->title ) 
  9736.  ) 
  9737.  ),  
  9738.                     __fs( 'new', $this->_slug ) . '!' 
  9739.  ); 
  9740.             } 
  9741.         } else if ( false === $new_version && ! $background ) { 
  9742.             $this->_admin_notices->add( 
  9743.                 __fs( 'you-have-latest', $this->_slug ),  
  9744.                 __fs( 'you-are-good', $this->_slug ) 
  9745.  ); 
  9746.         } 
  9747.  
  9748.         $this->_store_update( $update, true, $plugin_id ); 
  9749.     } 
  9750.  
  9751.     /** 
  9752.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  9753.      * @since  1.0.4 
  9754.      * 
  9755.      * @param bool $flush Since 1.1.7.3 add 24 hour cache by default. 
  9756.      * 
  9757.      * @return FS_Plugin[] 
  9758.      * 
  9759.      * @uses   FS_Api 
  9760.      */ 
  9761.     private function _sync_addons( $flush = false ) { 
  9762.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  9763.  
  9764.         $api = $this->get_api_site_or_plugin_scope(); 
  9765.  
  9766.         /** 
  9767.          * @since 1.2.1 
  9768.          * 
  9769.          * If there's a cached version of the add-ons and not asking 
  9770.          * for a flush, just use the currently stored add-ons. 
  9771.          */ 
  9772.         if ( ! $flush && $api->is_cached( '/addons.json?enriched=true' ) ) { 
  9773.             $addons = self::get_all_addons(); 
  9774.  
  9775.             return $addons[ $this->_plugin->id ]; 
  9776.         } 
  9777.  
  9778.         $result = $api->get( '/addons.json?enriched=true', $flush ); 
  9779.  
  9780.         $addons = array(); 
  9781.         if ( $this->is_api_result_object( $result, 'plugins' ) && 
  9782.              is_array( $result->plugins ) 
  9783.  ) { 
  9784.             for ( $i = 0, $len = count( $result->plugins ); $i < $len; $i ++ ) { 
  9785.                 $addons[ $i ] = new FS_Plugin( $result->plugins[ $i ] ); 
  9786.             } 
  9787.  
  9788.             $this->_store_addons( $addons, true ); 
  9789.         } 
  9790.  
  9791.         return $addons; 
  9792.     } 
  9793.  
  9794.     /** 
  9795.      * Handle user email update. 
  9796.      * 
  9797.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  9798.      * @since  1.0.3 
  9799.      * @uses   FS_Api 
  9800.      * 
  9801.      * @param string $new_email 
  9802.      * 
  9803.      * @return object 
  9804.      */ 
  9805.     private function _update_email( $new_email ) { 
  9806.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  9807.  
  9808.  
  9809.         $api = $this->get_api_user_scope(); 
  9810.         $user = $api->call( "?plugin_id={$this->_plugin->id}&fields=id, email, is_verified", 'put', array( 
  9811.             'email' => $new_email,  
  9812.             'after_email_confirm_url' => $this->_get_admin_page_url( 
  9813.                 'account',  
  9814.                 array( 'fs_action' => 'sync_user' ) 
  9815.  ),  
  9816.  ) ); 
  9817.  
  9818.         if ( ! isset( $user->error ) ) { 
  9819.             $this->_user->email = $user->email; 
  9820.             $this->_user->is_verified = $user->is_verified; 
  9821.             $this->_store_user(); 
  9822.         } else { 
  9823.             // handle different error cases. 
  9824.  
  9825.         } 
  9826.  
  9827.         return $user; 
  9828.     }

  9831.     #region API Error Handling
