  9833.  
  9834.     /** 
  9835.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  9836.      * @since  1.1.1 
  9837.      * 
  9838.      * @param mixed $result 
  9839.      * 
  9840.      * @return bool Is API result contains an error. 
  9841.      */ 
  9842.     private function is_api_error( $result ) { 
  9843.         return FS_Api::is_api_error( $result ); 
  9844.     } 
  9845.  
  9846.     /** 
  9847.      * Checks if given API result is a non-empty and not an error object. 
  9848.      * 
  9849.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  9850.      * @since  1.2.1.5 
  9851.      * 
  9852.      * @param mixed       $result 
  9853.      * @param string|null $required_property Optional property we want to verify that is set. 
  9854.      * 
  9855.      * @return bool 
  9856.      */ 
  9857.     function is_api_result_object( $result, $required_property = null ) { 
  9858.         return FS_Api::is_api_result_object( $result, $required_property ); 
  9859.     } 
  9860.  
  9861.     /** 
  9862.      * Checks if given API result is a non-empty entity object with non-empty ID. 
  9863.      * 
  9864.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  9865.      * @since  1.2.1.5 
  9866.      * 
  9867.      * @param mixed $result 
  9868.      * 
  9869.      * @return bool 
  9870.      */ 
  9871.     private function is_api_result_entity( $result ) { 
  9872.         return FS_Api::is_api_result_entity( $result ); 
  9873.     } 
  9874.  
  9875.     #endregion 
  9876.  
  9877.     /** 
  9878.      * Make sure a given argument is an array of a specific type. 
  9879.      * 
  9880.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  9881.      * @since  1.2.1.5 
  9882.      * 
  9883.      * @param mixed  $array 
  9884.      * @param string $class 
  9885.      * 
  9886.      * @return bool 
  9887.      */ 
  9888.     private function is_array_instanceof( $array, $class ) { 
  9889.         return ( is_array( $array ) && ( empty( $array ) || $array[0] instanceof $class ) ); 
  9890.     } 
  9891.  
  9892.     /** 
  9893.      * Start install ownership change. 
  9894.      * 
  9895.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  9896.      * @since  1.1.1 
  9897.      * @uses   FS_Api 
  9898.      * 
  9899.      * @param string $candidate_email 
  9900.      * 
  9901.      * @return bool Is ownership change successfully initiated. 
  9902.      */ 
  9903.     private function init_change_owner( $candidate_email ) { 
  9904.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  9905.  
  9906.         $api = $this->get_api_site_scope(); 
  9907.         $result = $api->call( "/users/{$this->_user->id}.json", 'put', array( 
  9908.             'email' => $candidate_email,  
  9909.             'after_confirm_url' => $this->_get_admin_page_url( 
  9910.                 'account',  
  9911.                 array( 'fs_action' => 'change_owner' ) 
  9912.  ),  
  9913.  ) ); 
  9914.  
  9915.         return ! $this->is_api_error( $result ); 
  9916.     } 
  9917.  
  9918.     /** 
  9919.      * Handle install ownership change. 
  9920.      * 
  9921.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  9922.      * @since  1.1.1 
  9923.      * @uses   FS_Api 
  9924.      * 
  9925.      * @return bool Was ownership change successfully complete. 
  9926.      */ 
  9927.     private function complete_change_owner() { 
  9928.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  9929.  
  9930.         $site_result = $this->get_api_site_scope( true )->get(); 
  9931.         $site = new FS_Site( $site_result ); 
  9932.         $this->_site = $site; 
  9933.  
  9934.         $user = new FS_User(); 
  9935.         $user->id = fs_request_get( 'user_id' ); 
  9936.  
  9937.         // Validate install's user and given user. 
  9938.         if ( $user->id != $this->_site->user_id ) { 
  9939.             return false; 
  9940.         } 
  9941.  
  9942.         $user->public_key = fs_request_get( 'user_public_key' ); 
  9943.         $user->secret_key = fs_request_get( 'user_secret_key' ); 
  9944.  
  9945.         // Fetch new user information. 
  9946.         $this->_user = $user; 
  9947.         $user_result = $this->get_api_user_scope( true )->get(); 
  9948.         $user = new FS_User( $user_result ); 
  9949.         $this->_user = $user; 
  9950.  
  9951.         $this->_set_account( $user, $site ); 
  9952.  
  9953.         return true; 
  9954.     } 
  9955.  
  9956.     /** 
  9957.      * Handle user name update. 
  9958.      * 
  9959.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  9960.      * @since  1.0.9 
  9961.      * @uses   FS_Api 
  9962.      * 
  9963.      * @return object 
  9964.      */ 
  9965.     private function update_user_name() { 
  9966.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  9967.         $name = fs_request_get( 'fs_user_name_' . $this->_slug, '' ); 
  9968.  
  9969.         $api = $this->get_api_user_scope(); 
  9970.         $user = $api->call( "?plugin_id={$this->_plugin->id}&fields=id, first, last", 'put', array( 
  9971.             'name' => $name,  
  9972.  ) ); 
  9973.  
  9974.         if ( ! isset( $user->error ) ) { 
  9975.             $this->_user->first = $user->first; 
  9976.             $this->_user->last = $user->last; 
  9977.             $this->_store_user(); 
  9978.         } else { 
  9979.             // handle different error cases. 
  9980.  
  9981.         } 
  9982.  
  9983.         return $user; 
  9984.     } 
  9985.  
  9986.     /** 
  9987.      * Verify user email. 
  9988.      * 
  9989.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  9990.      * @since  1.0.3 
  9991.      * @uses   FS_Api 
  9992.      */ 
  9993.     private function verify_email() { 
  9994.         $this->_handle_account_user_sync(); 
  9995.  
  9996.         if ( $this->_user->is_verified() ) { 
  9997.             return; 
  9998.         } 
  9999.  
  10000.         $api = $this->get_api_site_scope(); 
  10001.         $result = $api->call( "/users/{$this->_user->id}/verify.json", 'put', array( 
  10002.             'after_email_confirm_url' => $this->_get_admin_page_url( 
  10003.                 'account',  
  10004.                 array( 'fs_action' => 'sync_user' ) 
  10005.  ) 
  10006.  ) ); 
  10007.  
  10008.         if ( ! isset( $result->error ) ) { 
  10009.             $this->_admin_notices->add( sprintf( 
  10010.                 __fs( 'verification-email-sent-message', $this->_slug ),  
  10011.                 sprintf( '<a href="mailto:%1s">%2s</a>', esc_url( $this->_user->email ), $this->_user->email ) 
  10012.  ) ); 
  10013.         } else { 
  10014.             // handle different error cases. 
  10015.  
  10016.         } 
  10017.     } 
  10018.  
  10019.     /** 
  10020.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  10021.      * @since  1.1.2 
  10022.      * 
  10023.      * @param array $params 
  10024.      * 
  10025.      * @return string 
  10026.      */ 
  10027.     private function get_activation_url( $params = array() ) { 
  10028.         return $this->apply_filters( 'connect_url', $this->_get_admin_page_url( '', $params ) ); 
  10029.     } 
  10030.  
  10031.     /** 
  10032.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  10033.      * @since  1.2.1.5 
  10034.      * 
  10035.      * @param array $params 
  10036.      * 
  10037.      * @return string 
  10038.      */ 
  10039.     function get_reconnect_url( $params = array() ) { 
  10040.         $params['fs_action'] = 'reset_anonymous_mode'; 
  10041.         $params['fs_slug'] = $this->_slug; 
  10042.  
  10043.         return $this->apply_filters( 'connect_url', $this->_get_admin_page_url( '', $params ) ); 
  10044.     } 
  10045.  
  10046.     /** 
  10047.      * Get the URL of the page that should be loaded after the user connect or skip in the opt-in screen. 
  10048.      * 
  10049.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  10050.      * @since  1.1.3 
  10051.      * 
  10052.      * @param string $filter Filter name. 
  10053.      * 
  10054.      * @return string 
  10055.      */ 
  10056.     function get_after_activation_url( $filter ) { 
  10057.         $first_time_path = $this->_menu->get_first_time_path(); 
  10058.  
  10059.         return $this->apply_filters( 
  10060.             $filter,  
  10061.             empty( $first_time_path ) ? 
  10062.                 $this->_get_admin_page_url() : 
  10063.                 $first_time_path 
  10064.  ); 
  10065.     } 
  10066.  
  10067.     /** 
  10068.      * Handle account page updates / edits / actions. 
  10069.      * 
  10070.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  10071.      * @since  1.0.2 
  10072.      * 
  10073.      */ 
  10074.     private function _handle_account_edits() { 
  10075.         if ( ! current_user_can( 'activate_plugins' ) ) { 
  10076.             return; 
  10077.         } 
  10078.  
  10079.         $plugin_id = fs_request_get( 'plugin_id', $this->get_id() ); 
  10080.         $action = fs_get_action(); 
  10081.  
  10082.         switch ( $action ) { 
  10083.             case 'delete_account': 
  10084.                 check_admin_referer( $action ); 
  10085.  
  10086.                 if ( $plugin_id == $this->get_id() ) { 
  10087.                     $this->delete_account_event(); 
  10088.  
  10089.                     // Clear user and site. 
  10090.                     $this->_site = null; 
  10091.                     $this->_user = null; 
  10092.  
  10093.                     fs_redirect( $this->get_activation_url() ); 
  10094.                 } else { 
  10095.                     if ( $this->is_addon_activated( $plugin_id ) ) { 
  10096.                         $fs_addon = self::get_instance_by_id( $plugin_id ); 
  10097.                         $fs_addon->delete_account_event(); 
  10098.  
  10099.                         fs_redirect( $this->_get_admin_page_url( 'account' ) ); 
  10100.                     } 
  10101.                 } 
  10102.  
  10103.                 return; 
  10104.  
  10105.             case 'downgrade_account': 
  10106.                 check_admin_referer( $action ); 
  10107.  
  10108.                 if ( $plugin_id == $this->get_id() ) { 
  10109.                     $this->_downgrade_site(); 
  10110.                 } else if ( $this->is_addon_activated( $plugin_id ) ) { 
  10111.                     $fs_addon = self::get_instance_by_id( $plugin_id ); 
  10112.                     $fs_addon->_downgrade_site(); 
  10113.                 } 
  10114.  
  10115.                 return; 
  10116.  
  10117.             case 'activate_license': 
  10118.                 check_admin_referer( $action ); 
  10119.  
  10120.                 if ( $plugin_id == $this->get_id() ) { 
  10121.                     $this->_activate_license(); 
  10122.                 } else { 
  10123.                     if ( $this->is_addon_activated( $plugin_id ) ) { 
  10124.                         $fs_addon = self::get_instance_by_id( $plugin_id ); 
  10125.                         $fs_addon->_activate_license(); 
  10126.                     } 
  10127.                 } 
  10128.  
  10129.                 return; 
  10130.  
  10131.             case 'deactivate_license': 
  10132.                 check_admin_referer( $action ); 
  10133.  
  10134.                 if ( $plugin_id == $this->get_id() ) { 
  10135.                     $this->_deactivate_license(); 
  10136.                 } else { 
  10137.                     if ( $this->is_addon_activated( $plugin_id ) ) { 
  10138.                         $fs_addon = self::get_instance_by_id( $plugin_id ); 
  10139.                         $fs_addon->_deactivate_license(); 
  10140.                     } 
  10141.                 } 
  10142.  
  10143.                 return; 
  10144.  
  10145.             case 'check_updates': 
  10146.                 check_admin_referer( $action ); 
  10147.                 $this->_check_updates(); 
  10148.  
  10149.                 return; 
  10150.  
  10151.             case 'change_owner': 
  10152.                 $state = fs_request_get( 'state', 'init' ); 
  10153.                 switch ( $state ) { 
  10154.                     case 'init': 
  10155.                         $candidate_email = fs_request_get( 'candidate_email', '' ); 
  10156.  
  10157.                         if ( $this->init_change_owner( $candidate_email ) ) { 
  10158.                             $this->_admin_notices->add( sprintf( __fs( 'change-owner-request-sent-x', $this->_slug ), '<b>' . $this->_user->email . '</b>' ) ); 
  10159.                         } 
  10160.                         break; 
  10161.                     case 'owner_confirmed': 
  10162.                         $candidate_email = fs_request_get( 'candidate_email', '' ); 
  10163.  
  10164.                         $this->_admin_notices->add( sprintf( __fs( 'change-owner-request_owner-confirmed', $this->_slug ), '<b>' . $candidate_email . '</b>' ) ); 
  10165.                         break; 
  10166.                     case 'candidate_confirmed': 
  10167.                         if ( $this->complete_change_owner() ) { 
  10168.                             $this->_admin_notices->add_sticky( 
  10169.                                 sprintf( __fs( 'change-owner-request_candidate-confirmed', $this->_slug ), '<b>' . $this->_user->email . '</b>' ),  
  10170.                                 'ownership_changed',  
  10171.                                 __fs( 'congrats', $this->_slug ) . '!' 
  10172.  ); 
  10173.                         } else { 
  10174.                             // @todo Handle failed ownership change message. 
  10175.                         } 
  10176.                         break; 
  10177.                 } 
  10178.  
  10179.                 return; 
  10180.  
  10181.             case 'update_email': 
  10182.                 check_admin_referer( 'update_email' ); 
  10183.  
  10184.                 $new_email = fs_request_get( 'fs_email_' . $this->_slug, '' ); 
  10185.                 $result = $this->_update_email( $new_email ); 
  10186.  
  10187.                 if ( isset( $result->error ) ) { 
  10188.                     switch ( $result->error->code ) { 
  10189.                         case 'user_exist': 
  10190.                             $this->_admin_notices->add( 
  10191.                                 __fs( 'user-exist-message', $this->_slug ) . ' ' . 
  10192.                                 sprintf( __fs( 'user-exist-message_ownership', $this->_slug ), '<b>' . $new_email . '</b>' ) . 
  10193.                                 sprintf( 
  10194.                                     '<a style="margin-left: 10px;" href="%s"><button class="button button-primary">%s  ➜</button></a>',  
  10195.                                     $this->get_account_url( 'change_owner', array( 
  10196.                                         'state' => 'init',  
  10197.                                         'candidate_email' => $new_email 
  10198.  ) ),  
  10199.                                     __fs( 'change-ownership', $this->_slug ) 
  10200.  ),  
  10201.                                 __fs( 'oops', $this->_slug ) . '...',  
  10202.                                 'error' 
  10203.  ); 
  10204.                             break; 
  10205.                     } 
  10206.                 } else { 
  10207.                     $this->_admin_notices->add( __fs( 'email-updated-message', $this->_slug ) ); 
  10208.                 } 
  10209.  
  10210.                 return; 
  10211.  
  10212.             case 'update_user_name': 
  10213.                 check_admin_referer( 'update_user_name' ); 
  10214.  
  10215.                 $result = $this->update_user_name(); 
  10216.  
  10217.                 if ( isset( $result->error ) ) { 
  10218.                     $this->_admin_notices->add( 
  10219.                         __fs( 'name-update-failed-message', $this->_slug ),  
  10220.                         __fs( 'oops', $this->_slug ) . '...',  
  10221.                         'error' 
  10222.  ); 
  10223.                 } else { 
  10224.                     $this->_admin_notices->add( __fs( 'name-updated-message', $this->_slug ) ); 
  10225.                 } 
  10226.  
  10227.                 return; 
  10228.  
  10229.             #region Actions that might be called from external links (e.g. email) 
  10230.  
  10231.             case 'cancel_trial': 
  10232.                 if ( $plugin_id == $this->get_id() ) { 
  10233.                     $this->_cancel_trial(); 
  10234.                 } else { 
  10235.                     if ( $this->is_addon_activated( $plugin_id ) ) { 
  10236.                         $fs_addon = self::get_instance_by_id( $plugin_id ); 
  10237.                         $fs_addon->_cancel_trial(); 
  10238.                     } 
  10239.                 } 
  10240.  
  10241.                 return; 
  10242.  
  10243.             case 'verify_email': 
  10244.                 $this->verify_email(); 
  10245.  
  10246.                 return; 
  10247.  
  10248.             case 'sync_user': 
  10249.                 $this->_handle_account_user_sync(); 
  10250.  
  10251.                 return; 
  10252.  
  10253.             case $this->_slug . '_sync_license': 
  10254.                 $this->_sync_license(); 
  10255.  
  10256.                 return; 
  10257.  
  10258.             case 'download_latest': 
  10259.                 $this->_download_latest_directly( $plugin_id ); 
  10260.  
  10261.                 return; 
  10262.  
  10263.             #endregion 
  10264.         } 
  10265.  
  10266.         if ( WP_FS__IS_POST_REQUEST ) { 
  10267.             $properties = array( 'site_secret_key', 'site_id', 'site_public_key' ); 
  10268.             foreach ( $properties as $p ) { 
  10269.                 if ( 'update_' . $p === $action ) { 
  10270.                     check_admin_referer( $action ); 
  10271.  
  10272.                     $this->_logger->log( $action ); 
  10273.  
  10274.                     $site_property = substr( $p, strlen( 'site_' ) ); 
  10275.                     $site_property_value = fs_request_get( 'fs_' . $p . '_' . $this->_slug, '' ); 
  10276.                     $this->get_site()->{$site_property} = $site_property_value; 
  10277.  
  10278.                     // Store account after modification. 
  10279.                     $this->_store_site(); 
  10280.  
  10281.                     $this->do_action( 'account_property_edit', 'site', $site_property, $site_property_value ); 
  10282.  
  10283.                     $this->_admin_notices->add( sprintf( 
  10284.                         __fs( 'x-updated', $this->_slug ),  
  10285.                         '<b>' . str_replace( '_', ' ', $p ) . '</b>' ) ); 
  10286.  
  10287.                     return; 
  10288.                 } 
  10289.             } 
  10290.         } 
  10291.     } 
  10292.  
  10293.     /** 
  10294.      * Account page resources load. 
  10295.      * 
  10296.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  10297.      * @since  1.0.6 
  10298.      */ 
  10299.     function _account_page_load() { 
  10300.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  10301.  
  10302.         $this->_logger->info( var_export( $_REQUEST, true ) ); 
  10303.  
  10304.         fs_enqueue_local_style( 'fs_account', '/admin/account.css' ); 
  10305.  
  10306.         if ( $this->has_addons() ) { 
  10307.             wp_enqueue_script( 'plugin-install' ); 
  10308.             add_thickbox(); 
  10309.  
  10310.             function fs_addons_body_class( $classes ) { 
  10311.                 $classes .= ' plugins-php'; 
  10312.  
  10313.                 return $classes; 
  10314.             } 
  10315.  
  10316.             add_filter( 'admin_body_class', 'fs_addons_body_class' ); 
  10317.         } 
  10318.  
  10319.         if ( $this->has_paid_plan() && 
  10320.              ! $this->has_any_license() && 
  10321.              ! $this->is_sync_executed() && 
  10322.              $this->is_tracking_allowed() 
  10323.  ) { 
  10324.             /** 
  10325.              * If no licenses found and no sync job was executed during the last 24 hours,  
  10326.              * just execute the sync job right away (blocking execution). 
  10327.              * 
  10328.              * @since 1.1.7.3 
  10329.              */ 
  10330.             $this->run_manual_sync(); 
  10331.         } 
  10332.  
  10333.         $this->_handle_account_edits(); 
  10334.  
  10335.         $this->do_action( 'account_page_load_before_departure' ); 
  10336.     }

  10350.         } else {

  10493.     /** SDK 
  10494.     ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------*/ 
  10495.     private $_user_api; 
  10496.  
  10497.     /** 
  10498.      * 
  10499.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  10500.      * @since  1.0.2 
  10501.      * 
  10502.      * @param bool $flush 
  10503.      * 
  10504.      * @return FS_Api 
  10505.      */ 
  10506.     function get_api_user_scope( $flush = false ) { 
  10507.         if ( ! isset( $this->_user_api ) || $flush ) { 
  10508.             $this->_user_api = FS_Api::instance( 
  10509.                 $this->_slug,  
  10510.                 'user',  
  10511.                 $this->_user->id,  
  10512.                 $this->_user->public_key,  
  10513.                 ! $this->is_live(),  
  10514.                 $this->_user->secret_key 
  10515.  ); 
  10516.         } 
  10517.  
  10518.         return $this->_user_api; 
  10519.     } 
  10520.  
  10521.     private $_site_api;

  10523.     /** 
  10524.      * 
  10525.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  10526.      * @since  1.0.2

  10529.      * 
  10530.      * @return FS_Api 
  10531.      */ 
  10532.     function get_api_site_scope( $flush = false ) { 
  10533.         if ( ! isset( $this->_site_api ) || $flush ) { 
  10534.             $this->_site_api = FS_Api::instance( 
  10535.                 $this->_slug,  
  10536.                 'install',

  10539.                 ! $this->is_live(),

  10545.     } 
  10546.  
  10547.     private $_plugin_api;

  10549.     /**

  10557.     function get_api_plugin_scope() {

  10564.                 ! $this->is_live()

  10571.     /** 
  10572.      * Get site API scope object (fallback to public plugin scope when not registered). 
  10573.      * 
  10574.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  10575.      * @since  1.0.7 
  10576.      * 
  10577.      * @return FS_Api 
  10578.      */ 
  10579.     function get_api_site_or_plugin_scope() {

  10581.             $this->get_api_site_scope() : 
  10582.             $this->get_api_plugin_scope(); 
  10583.     }

  10585.     /** 
  10586.      * Show trial promotional notice (if any trial exist).

  10593.     function _check_for_trial_plans( $plans ) {

  10595.     } 
  10596.  
  10597.     /** 
  10598.      * During trial promotion the "upgrade" submenu item turns to 
  10599.      * "start trial" to encourage the trial. Since we want to keep 
  10600.      * the same menu item handler and there's no robust way to 
  10601.      * add new arguments to the menu item link's querystring,  
  10602.      * use JavaScript to find the menu item and update the href of 
  10603.      * the link. 
  10604.      * 
  10605.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  10606.      * @since  1.2.1.5 
  10607.      */ 
  10608.     function _fix_start_trial_menu_item_url() { 
  10609.         $template_args = array( 'slug' => $this->_slug ); 
  10610.         fs_require_template( 'add-trial-to-pricing.php', $template_args ); 
  10611.     } 
  10612.  
  10613.     /** 
  10614.      * Show trial promotional notice (if any trial exist). 
  10615.      * 
  10616.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  10617.      * @since  1.0.9 
  10618.      * 
  10619.      * @return bool If trial notice added. 
  10620.      */ 
  10621.     function _add_trial_notice() { 
  10622.         if ( ! current_user_can( 'activate_plugins' ) ) { 
  10623.             return false; 
  10624.         } 
  10625.  
  10626.         if ( ! $this->is_user_in_admin() ) { 
  10627.             return false; 
  10628.         } 
  10629.  
  10630.         // Check if trial message is already shown. 
  10631.         if ( $this->_admin_notices->has_sticky( 'trial_promotion' ) ) { 
  10632.             add_action( 'admin_footer', array( &$this, '_fix_start_trial_menu_item_url' ) ); 
  10633.  
  10634.             $this->_menu->add_counter_to_menu_item( 1, 'fs-trial' ); 
  10635.  
  10636.             return false; 
  10637.         } 
  10638.  
  10639.         if ( $this->is_premium() && ! WP_FS__DEV_MODE ) { 
  10640.             // Don't show trial if running the premium code, unless running in DEV mode. 
  10641.             return false; 
  10642.         } 
  10643.  
  10644.         if ( ! $this->has_trial_plan() ) { 
  10645.             // No plans with trial. 
  10646.             return false; 
  10647.         } 
  10648.  
  10649.         if ( ! $this->apply_filters( 'show_trial', true ) ) { 
  10650.             // Developer explicitly asked not to show the trial promo. 
  10651.             return false; 
  10652.         } 
  10653.  
  10654.         if ( $this->is_registered() ) { 
  10655.             // Check if trial already utilized. 
  10656.             if ( $this->_site->is_trial_utilized() ) { 
  10657.                 return false; 
  10658.             } 
  10659.  
  10660.             if ( $this->is_paying_or_trial() ) { 
  10661.                 // Don't show trial if paying or already in trial. 
  10662.                 return false; 
  10663.             } 
  10664.         } 
  10665.  
  10666.         if ( $this->is_activation_mode() || $this->is_pending_activation() ) { 
  10667.             // If not yet opted-in/skipped, or pending activation, don't show trial. 
  10668.             return false; 
  10669.         } 
  10670.  
  10671.         $last_time_trial_promotion_shown = $this->_storage->get( 'trial_promotion_shown', false ); 
  10672.         $was_promotion_shown_before = ( false !== $last_time_trial_promotion_shown ); 
  10673.  
  10674.         // Show promotion if never shown before and 24 hours after initial activation with FS. 
  10675.         if ( ! $was_promotion_shown_before && 
  10676.              $this->_storage->install_timestamp > ( time() - WP_FS__TIME_24_HOURS_IN_SEC ) 
  10677.  ) { 
  10678.             return false; 
  10679.         } 
  10680.  
  10681.         // OR if promotion was shown before, try showing it every 30 days. 
  10682.         if ( $was_promotion_shown_before && 
  10683.              30 * WP_FS__TIME_24_HOURS_IN_SEC > time() - $last_time_trial_promotion_shown 
  10684.  ) { 
  10685.             return false; 
  10686.         } 
  10687.  
  10688.         $trial_period = $this->_trial_days; 
  10689.         $require_payment = $this->_is_trial_require_payment; 
  10690.         $trial_url = $this->get_trial_url(); 
  10691.         $plans_string = strtolower( __fs( 'awesome', $this->_slug ) ); 
  10692.  
  10693.         if ( $this->is_registered() ) { 
  10694.             // If opted-in, override trial with up to date data from API. 
  10695.             $trial_plans = FS_Plan_Manager::instance()->get_trial_plans( $this->_plans ); 
  10696.             $trial_plans_count = count( $trial_plans ); 
  10697.  
  10698.             if ( 0 === $trial_plans_count ) { 
  10699.                 // If there's no plans with a trial just exit. 
  10700.                 return false; 
  10701.             } 
  10702.  
  10703.             /** 
  10704.              * @var FS_Plugin_Plan $paid_plan 
  10705.              */ 
  10706.             $paid_plan = $trial_plans[0]; 
  10707.             $require_payment = $paid_plan->is_require_subscription; 
  10708.             $trial_period = $paid_plan->trial_period; 
  10709.  
  10710.             $total_paid_plans = count( $this->_plans ) - ( FS_Plan_Manager::instance()->has_free_plan( $this->_plans ) ? 1 : 0 ); 
  10711.  
  10712.             if ( $total_paid_plans !== $trial_plans_count ) { 
  10713.                 // Not all paid plans have a trial - generate a string of those that have it. 
  10714.                 for ( $i = 0; $i < $trial_plans_count; $i ++ ) { 
  10715.                     $plans_string .= sprintf( 
  10716.                         '<a href="%s">%s</a>',  
  10717.                         $trial_url,  
  10718.                         $trial_plans[ $i ]->title 
  10719.  ); 
  10720.  
  10721.                     if ( $i < $trial_plans_count - 2 ) { 
  10722.                         $plans_string .= ', '; 
  10723.                     } else if ( $i == $trial_plans_count - 2 ) { 
  10724.                         $plans_string .= ' and '; 
  10725.                     } 
  10726.                 } 
  10727.             } 
  10728.         } 
  10729.  
  10730.         $message = sprintf( 
  10731.             __fs( 'hey', $this->_slug ) . '! ' . __fs( 'trial-x-promotion-message', $this->_slug ),  
  10732.             sprintf( '<b>%s</b>', $this->get_plugin_name() ),  
  10733.             $plans_string,  
  10734.             $trial_period 
  10735.  ); 
  10736.  
  10737.         // "No Credit-Card Required" or "No Commitment for N Days". 
  10738.         $cc_string = $require_payment ? 
  10739.             sprintf( __fs( 'no-commitment-for-x-days', $this->_slug ), $trial_period ) : 
  10740.             __fs( 'no-cc-required', $this->_slug ) . '!'; 
  10741.  
  10742.  
  10743.         // Start trial button. 
  10744.         $button = ' ' . sprintf( 
  10745.                 '<a style="margin-left: 10px; vertical-align: super;" href="%s"><button class="button button-primary">%s  ➜</button></a>',  
  10746.                 $trial_url,  
  10747.                 __fs( 'start-free-trial', $this->_slug ) 
  10748.  ); 
  10749.  
  10750.         $this->_admin_notices->add_sticky( 
  10751.             $this->apply_filters( 'trial_promotion_message', "{$message} {$cc_string} {$button}" ),  
  10752.             'trial_promotion',  
  10753.             '',  
  10754.             'promotion' 
  10755.  ); 
  10756.  
  10757.         $this->_storage->trial_promotion_shown = WP_FS__SCRIPT_START_TIME; 
  10758.  
  10759.         return true; 
  10760.     } 
  10761.  
  10762.     /** 
  10763.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  10764.      * @since  1.2.1.5 
  10765.      */ 
  10766.     function _enqueue_common_css() { 
  10767.         if ( $this->has_paid_plan() && ! $this->is_paying() ) { 
  10768.             // Add basic CSS for admin-notices and menu-item colors. 
  10769.             fs_enqueue_local_style( 'fs_common', '/admin/common.css' ); 
  10770.         } 
  10771.     } 
  10772.  
  10773.     /** Action Links 
  10774.     ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------*/ 
  10775.     private $_action_links_hooked = false; 
  10776.     private $_action_links = array(); 
  10777.  
  10778.     /** 
  10779.      * Hook to plugin action links filter. 
  10780.      * 
  10781.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  10782.      * @since  1.0.0 
  10783.      */ 
  10784.     private function hook_plugin_action_links() { 
  10785.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  10786.  
  10787.         $this->_action_links_hooked = true; 
  10788.  
  10789.         $this->_logger->log( 'Adding action links hooks.' ); 
  10790.  
  10791.         // Add action link to settings page. 
  10792.         add_filter( 'plugin_action_links_' . $this->_plugin_basename, array( 
  10793.             &$this,  
  10794.             '_modify_plugin_action_links_hook' 
  10795.  ), WP_FS__DEFAULT_PRIORITY, 2 ); 
  10796.         add_filter( 'network_admin_plugin_action_links_' . $this->_plugin_basename, array( 
  10797.             &$this,  
  10798.             '_modify_plugin_action_links_hook' 
  10799.  ), WP_FS__DEFAULT_PRIORITY, 2 ); 
  10800.     } 
  10801.  
  10802.     /** 
  10803.      * Add plugin action link. 
  10804.      * 
  10805.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  10806.      * @since  1.0.0 
  10807.      * 
  10808.      * @param      $label 
  10809.      * @param      $url 
  10810.      * @param bool $external 
  10811.      * @param int  $priority 
  10812.      * @param bool $key 
  10813.      */ 
  10814.     function add_plugin_action_link( $label, $url, $external = false, $priority = WP_FS__DEFAULT_PRIORITY, $key = false ) { 
  10815.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  10816.  
  10817.         if ( ! isset( $this->_action_links[ $priority ] ) ) { 
  10818.             $this->_action_links[ $priority ] = array(); 
  10819.         } 
  10820.  
  10821.         if ( false === $key ) { 
  10822.             $key = preg_replace( "/[^A-Za-z0-9 ]/", '', strtolower( $label ) ); 
  10823.         } 
  10824.  
  10825.         $this->_action_links[ $priority ][] = array( 
  10826.             'label' => $label,  
  10827.             'href' => $url,  
  10828.             'key' => $key,  
  10829.             'external' => $external 
  10830.  ); 
  10831.     } 
  10832.  
  10833.     /** 
  10834.      * Adds Upgrade and Add-Ons links to the main Plugins page link actions collection. 
  10835.      * 
  10836.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  10837.      * @since  1.0.0 
  10838.      */ 
  10839.     function _add_upgrade_action_link() { 
  10840.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  10841.  
  10842.         if ( $this->is_registered() ) { 
  10843.             if ( ! $this->is_paying() && $this->has_paid_plan() ) { 
  10844.                 $this->add_plugin_action_link( 
  10845.                     __fs( 'upgrade', $this->_slug ),  
  10846.                     $this->get_upgrade_url(),  
  10847.                     false,  
  10848.                     7,  
  10849.                     'upgrade' 
  10850.  ); 
  10851.             } 
  10852.  
  10853.             if ( $this->has_addons() ) { 
  10854.                 $this->add_plugin_action_link( 
  10855.                     __fs( 'add-ons', $this->_slug ),  
  10856.                     $this->_get_admin_page_url( 'addons' ),  
  10857.                     false,  
  10858.                     9,  
  10859.                     'addons' 
  10860.  ); 
  10861.             } 
  10862.         } 
  10863.     } 
  10864.  
  10865.     /** 
  10866.      * Adds "Activate License" or "Change License" link to the main Plugins page link actions collection. 
  10867.      * 
  10868.      * @author Leo Fajardo (@leorw) 
  10869.      * @since  1.1.9 
  10870.      */ 
  10871.     function _add_license_action_link() { 
  10872.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  10873.  
  10874.         if ( $this->is_free_plan() && $this->is_addon() ) { 
  10875.             return; 
  10876.         } 
  10877.  
  10878.         if ( ! $this->is_ajax() ) { 
  10879.             // Inject license activation dialog UI and client side code. 
  10880.             add_action( 'admin_footer', array( &$this, '_add_license_activation_dialog_box' ) ); 
  10881.         } 
  10882.  
  10883.         $link_text = __fs( 
  10884.             $this->is_free_plan() ? 'activate-license' : 'change-license',  
  10885.             $this->_slug 
  10886.  ); 
  10887.  
  10888.         $this->add_plugin_action_link( 
  10889.             $link_text,  
  10890.             '#',  
  10891.             false,  
  10892.             11,  
  10893.             ( 'activate-license ' . $this->_slug ) 
  10894.  ); 
  10895.     } 
  10896.  
  10897.     /** 
  10898.      * Adds "Opt in" or "Opt out" link to the main "Plugins" page link actions collection. 
  10899.      * 
  10900.      * @author Leo Fajardo (@leorw) 
  10901.      * @since  1.2.1.5 
  10902.      */ 
  10903.     function _add_tracking_links() { 
  10904.         if ( ! current_user_can( 'activate_plugins' ) ) { 
  10905.             return; 
  10906.         } 
  10907.  
  10908.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  10909.  
  10910.         if ( ! $this->is_enable_anonymous() ) { 
  10911.             // Don't allow to opt-out if anonymous mode is disabled. 
  10912.             return; 
  10913.         } 
  10914.  
  10915.         if ( ! $this->is_free_plan() ) { 
  10916.             // Don't allow to opt-out if running in paid plan. 
  10917.             return; 
  10918.         } 
  10919.  
  10920.         if ( $this->add_ajax_action( 'stop_tracking', array( &$this, '_stop_tracking_callback' ) ) ) { 
  10921.             return; 
  10922.         } 
  10923.  
  10924.         if ( $this->add_ajax_action( 'allow_tracking', array( &$this, '_allow_tracking_callback' ) ) ) { 
  10925.             return; 
  10926.         } 
  10927.  
  10928.         if ( fs_request_is_action_secure( $this->_slug . '_reconnect' ) ) { 
  10929.             if ( ! $this->is_registered() && $this->is_anonymous() ) { 
  10930.                 $this->connect_again(); 
  10931.  
  10932.                 return; 
  10933.             } 
  10934.         } 
  10935.  
  10936.         $url = '#'; 
  10937.  
  10938.         if ( $this->is_registered() ) { 
  10939.             if ( $this->is_tracking_allowed() ) { 
  10940.                 $link_text_id = 'opt-out'; 
  10941.             } else { 
  10942.                 $link_text_id = 'opt-in'; 
  10943.             } 
  10944.  
  10945.             add_action( 'admin_footer', array( &$this, '_add_optout_dialog' ) ); 
  10946.         } else { 
  10947.             $link_text_id = 'opt-in'; 
  10948.  
  10949.             $params = ! $this->is_anonymous() ? 
  10950.                 array() : 
  10951.                 array( 
  10952.                     'nonce' => wp_create_nonce( $this->_slug . '_reconnect' ),  
  10953.                     'fs_action' => ( $this->_slug . '_reconnect' ),  
  10954.  ); 
  10955.  
  10956.             $url = $this->get_activation_url( $params ); 
  10957.         } 
  10958.  
  10959.         $this->add_plugin_action_link( 
  10960.             __fs( $link_text_id, $this->_slug ),  
  10961.             $url,  
  10962.             false,  
  10963.             13,  
  10964.             "opt-in-or-opt-out {$this->_slug}" 
  10965.  ); 
  10966.     } 
  10967.  
  10968.     /** 
  10969.      * Get the URL of the page that should be loaded right after the plugin activation. 
  10970.      * 
  10971.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  10972.      * @since  1.1.7.4 
  10973.      * 
  10974.      * @return string 
  10975.      */ 
  10976.     function get_after_plugin_activation_redirect_url() { 
  10977.         $url = false; 
  10978.         $plugin_fs = false; 
  10979.  
  10980.         if ( ! $this->is_addon() ) { 
  10981.             $first_time_path = $this->_menu->get_first_time_path(); 
  10982.             $plugin_fs = $this; 
  10983.             $url = $plugin_fs->is_activation_mode() ? 
  10984.                 $plugin_fs->get_activation_url() : 
  10985.                 ( empty( $first_time_path ) ? 
  10986.                     $this->_get_admin_page_url() : 
  10987.                     $first_time_path ); 
  10988.         } else { 
  10989.             if ( $this->is_parent_plugin_installed() ) { 
  10990.                 $plugin_fs = self::get_parent_instance(); 
  10991.             } 
  10992.  
  10993.             if ( is_object( $plugin_fs ) ) { 
  10994.                 if ( ! $plugin_fs->is_registered() ) { 
  10995.                     // Forward to parent plugin connect when parent not registered. 
  10996.                     $url = $plugin_fs->get_activation_url(); 
  10997.                 } else { 
  10998.                     // Forward to account page. 
  10999.                     $url = $plugin_fs->_get_admin_page_url( 'account' ); 
  11000.                 } 
  11001.             } 
  11002.         } 
  11003.  
  11004.         return $url; 
  11005.     } 
  11006.  
  11007.     /** 
  11008.      * Forward page to activation page. 
  11009.      * 
  11010.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  11011.      * @since  1.0.3 
  11012.      */ 
  11013.     function _redirect_on_activation_hook() { 
  11014.         $url = $this->get_after_plugin_activation_redirect_url(); 
  11015.  
  11016.         if ( is_string( $url ) ) { 
  11017.             fs_redirect( $url ); 
  11018.         } 
  11019.     } 
  11020.  
  11021.     /** 
  11022.      * Modify plugin's page action links collection. 
  11023.      * 
  11024.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  11025.      * @since  1.0.0 
  11026.      * 
  11027.      * @param array $links 
  11028.      * @param       $file 
  11029.      * 
  11030.      * @return array 
  11031.      */ 
  11032.     function _modify_plugin_action_links_hook( $links, $file ) { 
  11033.         $this->_logger->entrance(); 
  11034.  
  11035.         $passed_deactivate = false; 
  11036.         $deactivate_link = ''; 
  11037.         $before_deactivate = array(); 
  11038.         $after_deactivate = array(); 
  11039.         foreach ( $links as $key => $link ) { 
  11040.             if ( 'deactivate' === $key ) { 
  11041.                 $deactivate_link = $link; 
  11042.                 $passed_deactivate = true; 
  11043.                 continue; 
  11044.             } 
  11045.  
  11046.             if ( ! $passed_deactivate ) { 
  11047.                 $before_deactivate[ $key ] = $link; 
  11048.             } else { 
  11049.                 $after_deactivate[ $key ] = $link; 
  11050.             } 
  11051.         } 
  11052.  
  11053.         ksort( $this->_action_links ); 
  11054.  
  11055.         foreach ( $this->_action_links as $new_links ) { 
  11056.             foreach ( $new_links as $link ) { 
  11057.                 $before_deactivate[ $link['key'] ] = '<a href="' . $link['href'] . '"' . ( $link['external'] ? ' target="_blank"' : '' ) . '>' . $link['label'] . '</a>'; 
  11058.             } 
  11059.         } 
  11060.  
  11061.         if ( ! empty( $deactivate_link ) ) { 
  11062.             if ( ! $this->is_paying_or_trial() || $this->is_premium() ) { 
  11063.                 /** 
  11064.                  * This HTML element is used to identify the correct plugin when attaching an event to its Deactivate link. 
  11065.                  * 
  11066.                  * If user is paying or in trial and have the free version installed,  
  11067.                  * assume that the deactivation is for the upgrade process, so this is not needed. 
  11068.                  */ 
  11069.                 $deactivate_link .= '<i class="fs-slug" data-slug="' . $this->_slug . '"></i>'; 
  11070.             } 
  11071.  
  11072.             // Append deactivation link. 
  11073.             $before_deactivate['deactivate'] = $deactivate_link; 
  11074.         } 
  11075.  
  11076.         return array_merge( $before_deactivate, $after_deactivate ); 
  11077.     } 
  11078.  
  11079.     /** 
  11080.      * Adds admin message. 
  11081.      * 
  11082.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  11083.      * @since  1.0.4

  11086.      * @param string $title 
  11087.      * @param string $type 
  11088.      */ 
  11089.     function add_admin_message( $message, $title = '', $type = 'success' ) { 
  11090.         $this->_admin_notices->add( $message, $title, $type ); 
  11091.     } 
  11092.  
  11093.     /** 
  11094.      * Adds sticky admin message.

  11096.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf)

  11098.      *

  11104.     function add_sticky_admin_message( $message, $id, $title = '', $type = 'success' ) {

  11106.     } 
  11107.  
  11108.     /** 
  11109.      * Helper function that returns the final steps for the upgrade completion. 
  11110.      * 
  11111.      * If the module is already running the premium code, returns an empty string. 
  11112.      * 
  11113.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  11114.      * @since  1.2.1 
  11115.      * 
  11116.      * @param string $plan_title 
  11117.      * 
  11118.      * @return string 
  11119.      */ 
  11120.     private function get_complete_upgrade_instructions( $plan_title = '' ) { 
  11121.         if ( $this->is_premium() ) { 
  11122.             return ''; 
  11123.         } 
  11124.  
  11125.         if ( empty( $plan_title ) ) { 
  11126.             $plan_title = $this->_site->plan->title; 
  11127.         } 
  11128.  
  11129.         // @since 1.2.1.5 The free version is auto deactivated. 
  11130.         $deactivation_step = version_compare( $this->version, '1.2.1.5', '<' ) ? 
  11131.             ( '<li>' . __fs( 'deactivate-free-version', $this->_slug ) . '.</li>' ) : 
  11132.             ''; 
  11133.  
  11134.         return sprintf( 
  11135.             ' %s: <ol><li>%s.</li>%s<li>%s (<a href="%s" target="_blank">%s</a>).</li></ol>',  
  11136.             __fs( 'follow-steps-to-complete-upgrade', $this->_slug ),  
  11137.             $this->_get_latest_download_link( sprintf( 
  11138.                 __fs( 'download-latest-x-version', $this->_slug ),  
  11139.                 $plan_title 
  11140.  ) ),  
  11141.             $deactivation_step,  
  11142.             __fs( 'upload-and-activate', $this->_slug ),  
  11143.             '//bit.ly/upload-wp-plugin',  
  11144.             __fs( 'howto-upload-activate', $this->_slug ) 
  11145.  ); 
  11146.     }

  11148.     /** Plugin Auto-Updates (@since 1.0.4) 
  11149.     ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------*/ 
  11150.     /** 
  11151.      * @var string[] 
  11152.      */ 
  11153.     private static $_auto_updated_plugins; 
  11154.  
  11155.     /** 
  11156.      * @todo   TEST IF IT WORKS!!! 
  11157.      * 
  11158.      * Include plugins for automatic updates based on stored settings. 
  11159.      * 
  11160.      * @see    http://wordpress.stackexchange.com/questions/131394/how-do-i-exclude-plugins-from-getting-automatically-updated/131404#131404 
  11161.      * 
  11162.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  11163.      * @since  1.0.4 
  11164.      * 
  11165.      * @param bool   $update Whether to update (not used for plugins) 
  11166.      * @param object $item   The plugin's info 
  11167.      * 
  11168.      * @return bool 
  11169.      */ 
  11170.     static function _include_plugins_in_auto_update( $update, $item ) { 
  11171.         // Before version 3.8.2 the $item was the file name of the plugin,  
  11172.         // while in 3.8.2 statistics were added (https://core.trac.wordpress.org/changeset/27905). 
  11173.         $by_slug = ( (int) str_replace( '.', '', get_bloginfo( 'version' ) ) >= 382 ); 
  11174.  
  11175.         if ( ! isset( self::$_auto_updated_plugins ) ) { 
  11176.             $plugins = self::$_accounts->get_option( 'plugins', array() ); 
  11177.  
  11178.             $identifiers = array(); 
  11179.             foreach ( $plugins as $p ) { 
  11180.                 /** 
  11181.                  * @var FS_Plugin $p 
  11182.                  */ 
  11183.                 if ( isset( $p->auto_update ) && $p->auto_update ) { 
  11184.                     $identifiers[] = ( $by_slug ? $p->slug : plugin_basename( $p->file ) ); 
  11185.                 } 
  11186.             } 
  11187.  
  11188.             self::$_auto_updated_plugins = $identifiers; 
  11189.         } 
  11190.  
  11191.         if ( in_array( $by_slug ? $item->slug : $item, self::$_auto_updated_plugins ) ) { 
  11192.             return true; 
  11193.         } 
  11194.  
  11195.         // Pass update decision to next filters 
  11196.         return $update; 
  11197.     } 
  11198.  
  11199.     #----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

  11201.     #----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

  11204.      * Check if Freemius in SDK upgrade mode. 
  11205.      * 
  11206.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  11207.      * @since  1.0.9 
  11208.      * 
  11209.      * @return bool 
  11210.      */ 
  11211.     function is_sdk_upgrade_mode() { 
  11212.         return isset( $this->_storage->sdk_upgrade_mode ) ? 
  11213.             $this->_storage->sdk_upgrade_mode : 
  11214.             false; 
  11215.     } 
  11216.  
  11217.     /**

  11222.      */

  11224.         $this->_storage->sdk_upgrade_mode = false; 
  11225.     }

  11259.     /** 
  11260.      * Check if specific permission requested. 
  11261.      * 
  11262.      * @author Vova Feldman (@svovaf) 
  11263.      * @since  1.1.6 
  11264.      * 
  11265.      * @param string $permission 
  11266.      * 
  11267.      * @return bool 
  11268.      */ 
  11269.     function is_permission_requested( $permission ) { 
  11270.         return isset( $this->_permissions[ $permission ] ) && ( true === $this->_permissions[ $permission ] ); 
  11271.     }
